DĀ 30

Dīrghāgama 长阿含经

Chapter 4 第四分

30 （三〇）世记经

Parallel to: MN 130 (~) / AN 3.36 (~) / MĀ 64 (~) / EĀ 32.4 (~)

Thus have I heard:

如是我闻：

At one time, the Buddha was at Anāthapiṇḍada's Park in the Jeta Grove near Śrāvastī, together with a great assembly of 1,250 bhikṣus.

一时，佛在舍卫国祇树给孤独园俱利窟中，与大比丘众千二百五十人俱。

At that time, the bhikṣus gathered in the Dharma hall after the meal and discussed, "Venerable ones! It is unprecedented. How did this world come to be destroyed? How did it come to be formed? What are the lands where sentient beings dwell like?"

时，众比丘于食后集讲堂上议言：「诸贤！未曾有也，今此天地何由而败？何由而成？众生所居国土云何？」

At that time, the World-Honored One, in a secluded place, listened with his divine ear and heard the bhikṣus discussing such matters in the Dharma hall after the meal. Then the World-Honored One rose from his quiet cave, went to the Dharma hall, sat down, and knowingly asked, "What were you discussing just now?"

尔时，世尊于闲静处天耳彻听，闻诸比丘于食后集讲堂上议如此言。尔时世尊于静窟起，诣讲堂坐，知而故问，问诸比丘：「向者所议，议何等事？」

The bhikṣus said to the Buddha, "After the meal, we gathered in the Dharma hall and discussed, 'Venerable ones! It is unprecedented. How did this world come to be destroyed? How did it come to be formed? What are the lands where sentient beings dwell like?' We gathered in the hall to discuss such matters."

诸比丘白佛言：「我等于食后集法讲堂议言：『诸贤！未曾有也，今是天地何由而败？何由而成？众生所居国土云何？』我等集堂议如是事。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "Excellent! Excellent! Those who have left home should practice two things: the noble silence and discussing the Dharma. When you gather in the Dharma hall, you should also be like this - practicing the noble silence and discussing the Dharma. Bhikṣus! Do you wish to hear the Tathāgata's explanation of the formation and destruction of the world and the lands where sentient beings dwell?"

佛告诸比丘言：「善哉！善哉！凡出家者应行二法：一贤圣默然，二讲论法语。汝等集在讲堂，亦应如此贤圣默然，讲论法语。诸比丘！汝等欲闻如来记天地成败、众生所居国邑不耶？」

At that time, the bhikṣus said to the Buddha, "Yes, World-Honored One! Now is the right time. We wish to hear it with joy. After the World-Honored One has spoken, we will uphold it."

时，诸比丘白佛言：「唯然。世尊！今正是时，愿乐欲闻。世尊说已，当奉持之。」

The Buddha said, "Bhikṣus! Listen attentively, listen attentively, and consider it well. I will explain it for you."

佛言：「比丘！谛听，谛听，善思念之，当为汝说。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "Just as the sun and moon circle the four continents in a day, illuminating with their light, so too are the thousand worlds. In the thousand worlds, there are a thousand suns and moons, a thousand Mount Sumerus, four thousand continents, four thousand great continents, four thousand seas, four thousand great oceans, four thousand dragons, four thousand great dragons, four thousand garuḍas, four thousand great garuḍas, four thousand evil paths, four thousand great evil paths, four thousand kings, four thousand great kings, seven thousand great trees, eight thousand great hells, ten thousand great mountains, a thousand Yama kings, a thousand Four Heavenly Kings, a thousand Trāyastriṃśa Heavens, a thousand Yama Heavens, a thousand Tuṣita Heavens, a thousand Nirmāṇarati Heavens, a thousand Paranirmitavaśavartin Heavens, a thousand Brahmā Heavens - this is called a small chiliocosm. As in a small chiliocosm, so too are the thousand small chiliocosms - this is called a dichiliocosm. As in a dichiliocosm, so too are the thousand dichiliocosms - this is called a trichiliocosm. The formation and destruction of such a world system is called a buddha-land where sentient beings dwell."

佛告诸比丘：「如一日月周行四天下，光明所照，如是千世界，千世界中有千日月、千须弥山王、四千天下、四千大天下、四千海水、四千大海、四千龙、四千大龙、四千金翅鸟、四千大金翅鸟、四千恶道、四千大恶道、四千王、四千大王、七千大树、八千大泥犁、十千大山、千阎罗王、千四天王、千忉利天、千焰摩天、千兜率天、千化自在天、千他化自在天、千梵天，是为小千世界。如一小千世界，尔所小千千世界，是为中千世界。如一中千世界，尔所中千千世界，是为三千大千世界。如是世界周匝成败，众生所居名一佛刹。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "Now this great earth is sixteen thousand eight hundred yojanas deep, its edge boundless. The earth rests on water, the water is three thousand thirty yojanas deep, its edge boundless. The water rests on wind, the wind is six thousand forty yojanas deep, its edge boundless. Bhikṣus! The great ocean is eight thousand four hundred yojanas deep, its edge boundless. Mount Sumeru enters the ocean water eight thousand four hundred yojanas, and rises above the sea water eight thousand four hundred yojanas. Its base is connected to the earth, with many solid earth layers. The mountain rises straight up, without any bends. Various trees grow, with many fragrances. The fragrance pervades the forests, with many sages and gods dwelling there. The mountain's base is made of pure golden sand. On the four sides of the mountain, four terraces emerge, seven hundred yojanas high, with various colors and seven treasures. The four terraces slope and curve over the ocean.

佛告比丘：「今此大地深十六万八千由旬，其边无际，地止于水，水深三千三十由旬，其边无际，水止于风，风深六千四十由旬，其边无际。比丘！其大海水深八万四千由旬，其边无际，须弥山王入海水中八万四千由旬，出海水上高八万四千由旬，下根连地，多固地分，其山直上，无有阿曲，生种种树，树出众香，香遍山林，多诸贤圣，大神妙天之所居止。其山下基纯有金沙，其山四面有四埵出，高七百由旬，杂色间厕，七宝所成，四埵斜低，曲临海上。

Mount Sumeru has seven jeweled stairways. The lower stairway is sixty yojanas wide. On both sides of the stairway are seven jeweled walls, seven railings, seven nets, and seven rows of trees. The golden walls have silver gates, the silver walls have golden gates, the crystal walls have lapis lazuli gates, the lapis lazuli walls have crystal gates, the red pearl walls have agate gates, the agate walls have red pearl gates, and the quartz walls have gates of various treasures. The railings are made of gold with silver crossbars, silver with golden crossbars, crystal with lapis lazuli crossbars, lapis lazuli with crystal crossbars, red pearls with agate crossbars, agate with red pearl crossbars, and quartz with crossbars of various treasures. Above the railings are jeweled nets. The golden nets hang silver bells, the silver nets hang golden bells, the lapis lazuli nets hang crystal bells, the crystal nets hang lapis lazuli bells, the red pearl nets hang agate bells, the agate nets hang red pearl bells, and the quartz nets hang bells of various treasures. The golden trees have golden roots and branches with silver leaves and fruits, the silver trees have silver roots and branches with golden leaves and fruits, the crystal trees have crystal roots and branches with lapis lazuli leaves and flowers, the lapis lazuli trees have lapis lazuli roots and branches with crystal leaves and flowers, the red pearl trees have red pearl roots and branches with agate leaves and flowers, the agate trees have agate roots and branches with red pearl leaves and flowers, and the quartz trees have quartz roots and branches with leaves and flowers of various treasures.

「须弥山王有七宝阶道，其下阶道广六十由旬，挟道两边有七重宝墙、七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，金墙银门，银墙金门，水精墙琉璃门，琉璃墙水精门，赤珠墙马瑙门，马瑙墙赤珠门，车璩墙众宝门。其栏楯者，金栏银桄，银栏金桄，水精栏琉璃桄，琉璃栏水精桄，赤珠栏马瑙桄，马瑙栏赤珠桄，车璩栏众宝桄。其栏楯上有宝罗网，其金罗网下悬银铃，其银罗网下悬金铃，琉璃罗网悬水精铃，水精罗网悬琉璃铃，赤珠罗网悬马瑙铃，马瑙罗网悬赤珠铃，车璩罗网悬众宝铃。其金树者金根金枝银叶华实，其银树者银根银枝金叶华实，其水精树水精根枝琉璃华叶，其琉璃树琉璃根枝水精华叶，其赤珠树赤珠根枝马瑙华叶，其马瑙树者马瑙根枝赤珠华叶，车璩树者车璩根枝] cf.【丽】众宝华叶。

The seven jeweled walls have four gates, and the gates have railings. On top of the seven jeweled walls are all pavilions and terraces, surrounded by gardens and bathing ponds, with various jeweled flowers and leaves. Rows of jeweled trees are lush with flowers and fruits. Fragrant breezes blow in all directions, pleasing the minds of people. There are countless thousands of ducks, geese, mandarin ducks, and other exotic birds, singing in harmony.

「其七重墙，墙有四门，门有栏楯，七重墙上皆有楼阁台观，周匝围遶有园观浴池，生众宝华叶，宝树行列，花果繁茂，香风四起，悦可人心，凫鴈鸳鸯，异类奇鸟，无数千种，相和而鸣。

The middle level stairway of Mount Sumeru is forty yojanas wide. On both sides of the stairway are seven jeweled walls, seven railings, seven nets, and seven rows of trees. The upper level stairway is twenty yojanas wide. On both sides of the stairway are seven jeweled walls, seven railings, seven nets, and seven rows of trees. There are also countless birds singing in harmony, just like on the middle stairway.

「又须弥山王中级阶道广四十由旬，挟道两边有七重宝墙、栏楯七重、罗网七重、行树七重，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦如下阶。上级阶道广二十由旬，挟道两边有七重宝墙、栏楯七重、罗网七重、行树七重，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦如中阶。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "The lower stairway is inhabited by yakṣas named Garuḍapāda. The middle stairway is inhabited by yakṣas named Mālatī. The upper stairway is inhabited by yakṣas named Nandana. The four corners rise up 42,000 yojanas, where the palaces of the Four Heavenly Kings are located. There are seven jeweled walls, seven railings, seven nets, and seven rows of trees. The jeweled bells and countless birds singing in harmony are also like this. On the summit of Mount Sumeru is the palace of the Thirty-three Heavens, with seven jeweled walls, seven railings, seven nets, and seven rows of trees. The jeweled bells and countless birds singing in harmony are also like this. Beyond the Thirty-three Heavens by one yojana is the palace of the Yāma Heaven. Beyond the Yāma Heaven by one yojana is the palace of the Tuṣita Heaven. Beyond the Tuṣita Heaven by one yojana is the palace of the Nirmāṇarati Heaven. Beyond the Nirmāṇarati Heaven by one yojana is the palace of the Paranirmitavaśavartin Heaven. Beyond the Paranirmitavaśavartin Heaven by one yojana is the palace of the Brahmakāyika Heaven.

佛告比丘：「其下阶道有鬼神住，名曰伽楼罗足。其中阶道有鬼神住，名曰持鬘。其上阶道有鬼神住，名曰喜乐。其四埵出高四万二千由旬，四天大王所居宫殿，有七重宝城、栏楯七重、罗网七重、行树七重，诸宝铃乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。须弥山顶有三十三天宫，宝城七重、栏楯七重、罗网七重、行树七重，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦] cf.【丽】复如是。过三十三天由旬一倍有焰摩天宫，过焰摩天宫由旬一倍有兜率天宫，过兜率天宫由旬一倍有化自在天宫，过化自在天宫由旬一倍有他化自在天宫，过他化自在天宫由旬一倍有梵加夷天宫。

Between the Paranirmitavaśavartin Heaven and the Brahmakāyika Heaven, there is the palace of the Māra Heaven, 6,000 yojanas long and wide. The palace walls are sevenfold, with seven railings, seven nets, and seven rows of trees. The jeweled bells and countless birds singing in harmony are also like this. Beyond the Brahmakāyika Heaven by one yojana is the palace of the Ābhāsvara Heaven. Beyond the Ābhāsvara Heaven by one yojana is the palace of the Śubhakṛtsna Heaven. Beyond the Śubhakṛtsna Heaven by one yojana is the palace of the Bṛhatphala Heaven. Beyond the Bṛhatphala Heaven by one yojana is the palace of the Āsaṃjñika Heaven. Beyond the Āsaṃjñika Heaven by one yojana is the palace of the Naivasaṃjñānāsaṃjñāyatana Heaven. Beyond the Naivasaṃjñānāsaṃjñāyatana Heaven by one yojana is the palace of the Avīci Heaven. Beyond the Avīci Heaven by one yojana is the palace of the Sudarśana Heaven. Beyond the Sudarśana Heaven by one yojana is the palace of the Sudarśanottara Heaven. Beyond the Sudarśanottara Heaven by one yojana is the palace of the Akaniṣṭha Heaven. Beyond the Akaniṣṭha Heaven is the Ākāśānantyāyatana Heaven, the Vijñānānantyāyatana Heaven, the Ākiñcanyāyatana Heaven, and the Naivasaṃjñānāsaṃjñāyatana Heaven. This is the limit of sentient beings, the world of sentient beings. All sentient beings are born, age, get sick, die, and experience the aggregates and existence. This is the limit.

「于他化自在天、梵加夷天中间，有摩天宫，纵广六千由旬，宫墙七重、栏楯七重、罗网七重、行树七重，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。过梵伽夷天宫由旬一倍有光音天宫，过光音天由旬一倍有遍净天宫，过遍净天由旬一倍有果实天宫，过果实天由旬一倍有无想天宫，过无想天由旬一倍有无造天宫，过无造天由旬一倍有无热天宫，过无热天由旬一倍有善见天宫，过善见天由旬一倍有大善见天宫，过大善见天由旬一倍有色究竟天宫，过色究竟天上有空处智天、识处智天、无所有处智天、有想无想处智天，齐此名众生边际、众生世界，一切众生生、老、病、死、受阴、受有，齐此不过。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "To the north of Mount Sumeru is a continent called Uttarakuru, square in shape, 10,000 yojanas long and wide. The faces of the people are also square, resembling the shape of the land. To the east of Mount Sumeru is a continent called Pūrvavideha, round in shape, 9,000 yojanas long and wide. The faces of the people are also round, resembling the shape of the land. To the west of Mount Sumeru is a continent called Aparagodānīya, shaped like a half-moon, 8,000 yojanas long and wide. The faces of the people are also like that, resembling the shape of the land. To the south of Mount Sumeru is a continent called Jambudvīpa, narrow in the south and broad in the north, 7,000 yojanas long and wide. The faces of the people are also like that, resembling the shape of the land. The northern side of Mount Sumeru is made of celestial gold, illuminating the north. The eastern side of Mount Sumeru is made of celestial silver, illuminating the east. The western side of Mount Sumeru is made of celestial crystal, illuminating the west. The southern side of Mount Sumeru is made of celestial lapis lazuli, illuminating the south.

佛告比丘：「须弥山北有天下，名欝单曰，其土正方，纵广一万由旬，人面亦方，像彼地形。须弥山东有天下，名弗于逮，其土正圆，纵广九千由旬，人面亦圆，像彼地形。须弥山西有天下，名俱耶尼，其土形如半月，纵广八千由旬，人面亦尔，像彼地形。须弥山南有天下，名阎浮提，其土南狭北广，纵广七千由旬，人面亦尔，像此地形。须弥山北面天金所成，光照北方。须弥山东面天银所成，光照东方。须弥山西面天水精所成，光照西方。须弥山南面天琉璃所成，光照南方。

In Uttarakuru there is a great tree king called Ambara, with a circumference of seven yojanas, a height of one hundred yojanas, and branches and leaves spreading fifty yojanas in all directions. In Pūrvavideha there is a great tree king called Kalāpa, with a circumference of seven yojanas, a height of one hundred yojanas, and branches and leaves spreading fifty yojanas in all directions. In Aparagodānīya there is a great tree king called Kinti, with a circumference of seven yojanas, a height of one hundred yojanas, and branches and leaves spreading fifty yojanas in all directions; and under the tree is a stone bull banner, one yojana high. In Jambudvīpa there is a great tree king called Jambū, with a circumference of seven yojanas, a height of one hundred yojanas, and branches and leaves spreading fifty yojanas in all directions. The garuḍa king and the nāga king have a tree called Kurīṣa, with a circumference of seven yojanas, a height of one hundred yojanas, and branches and leaves spreading fifty yojanas in all directions. The asura king has a tree called Suvidita, with a circumference of seven yojanas, a height of one hundred yojanas, and branches and leaves spreading fifty yojanas in all directions. The Trāyastriṃśa Heaven has a tree called Trayastriṃśa, with a circumference of seven yojanas, a height of one hundred yojanas, and branches and leaves spreading fifty yojanas in all directions.

「欝单曰有大树王，名庵婆罗，围七由旬，高百由旬，枝叶四布五十由旬。弗于逮有大树王，名伽蓝浮，围七由旬，高百由旬，枝叶四布五十由旬。俱耶尼有大树王，名曰斤提，围七由旬，高百由旬，枝叶四布五十由旬；又其树下有石牛幢，高一由旬。阎浮提有大树王，名曰阎浮提，围七由旬，高百由旬，枝叶四布五十由旬。金翅鸟王及龙王树，名俱利睒婆罗，围七由旬，高百由旬，枝叶四布五十由旬。阿修罗王有树，名善画，围七由旬，高百由旬，枝叶四布五十由旬。忉利天有树，名曰昼度，围七由旬，高百由旬，枝叶四布五十由旬。

Beside Mount Sumeru is a mountain called Gandhamādana, 42,000 yojanas high and 42,000 yojanas long and wide. Its edges are vast and varied, made of the seven treasures. The mountain is 84,000 yojanas away from Mount Sumeru. In between, there are only blue lotuses, red lotuses, white lotuses, and pink lotuses, with reeds, pines, and bamboo growing among them, emitting various fragrances that fill the air. Not far from Mount Gandhamādana is a mountain called Īṣādhara, 21,000 yojanas high and 21,000 yojanas long and wide. Its edges are vast and varied, made of the seven treasures. It is 42,000 yojanas away from Mount Gandhamādana. In between, there are only blue lotuses, red lotuses, white lotuses, and pink lotuses, with reeds, pines, and bamboo growing among them, emitting various fragrances that fill the air. Not far from Mount Īṣādhara is a mountain called Nimimdhara, 10,500 yojanas high and 10,500 yojanas long and wide. Its edges are vast and varied, made of the seven treasures. It is 21,000 yojanas away from Mount Īṣādhara. In between, there are only four kinds of mixed flowers, with reeds, pines, and bamboo growing among them, emitting various fragrances that fill the air. Not far from Mount Nimimdhara is a mountain called Sudarśana, 3,000 yojanas high and 3,000 yojanas long and wide. Its edges are vast and varied, made of the seven treasures. It is 10,500 yojanas away from Mount Nimimdhara. In between, there are only four kinds of mixed flowers, with reeds, pines, and bamboo growing among them, emitting various fragrances that fill the air.

「须弥山边有山，名伽陀罗，高四万二千由旬，纵广四万二千由旬，其边广远，杂色间厕，七宝所成，其山去须弥山八万四千由旬，其间纯生优钵罗花、钵头摩花、俱物头花、分陀利花，芦苇、松、竹丛生其中，出种种香，香亦充遍。去佉陀罗山不远有山，名伊沙陀罗，高二万一千由旬，纵广二万一千由旬，其边广远，杂色间厕，七宝所成，去佉陀罗山四万二千由旬，其间纯生优钵罗花、钵头摩花、俱勿头花、分陀利花，芦苇、松、竹丛生其中，出种种香，香气充遍。去伊沙陀罗山不远有山，名树巨陀罗，高万二千由旬，纵广万二千由旬，其边广远，杂色间厕，七宝所成。去伊沙陀罗山二万一千由旬，其间纯生四种杂花，芦苇、松、竹丛生其中，出种种香，香气充遍。去树巨陀罗山不远有山，名善见，高六千由旬，纵广六千由旬，其边广远，杂色间厕，七宝所成，去树巨陀罗山万二千由旬，其间纯生四种杂花，芦苇、松、竹丛生其中，出种种香，香气充遍。

「去大金刚山不远有大海水，海水北岸有大树王，名曰阎浮，围七由旬，高百由旬，枝叶四布五十由旬，其边空地复有丛林，名庵婆罗，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名曰阎婆，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名曰娑罗，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名曰多罗，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名曰那多罗，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名曰为男，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名曰为女，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名曰男女，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名曰散那，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名曰栴檀，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名曰佉詶罗，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名曰波［木＊奈］婆罗，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名曰毗罗，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名曰香［木＊奈］，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名曰为梨，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名曰安石留，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名曰为甘，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名呵梨勒，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名毗醯勒，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名阿摩勒，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名阿摩犁，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名［木＊奈］，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名甘蔗，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名苇，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名竹，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名舍罗，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名舍罗业，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名木瓜，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名大木瓜，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名解脱华，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名瞻婆，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名婆罗罗，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名修摩那，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名婆师，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名多罗梨，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名伽耶，纵广五十由旬。复有丛林名葡萄，纵广五十由旬。

Beyond this land of emptiness, there are also flower ponds in the empty land, fifty yojanas long and wide. There are also lotus ponds, blue lotus ponds, and white lotus ponds, filled with poisonous snakes, each fifty yojanas long and wide. Beyond this land of emptiness, there is a great ocean called Utse, below which is the path of the wheel-turning sage kings, twelve yojanas wide. On both sides of the path are sevenfold walls, sevenfold railings, sevenfold nets, and sevenfold rows of trees, all adorned with the seven treasures. When a wheel-turning sage king appears in the world, the water naturally recedes and the path appears level. Not far from the sea is a mountain called Utse, which is majestic, with luxuriant trees, abundant flowers and fruits, fragrant scents, and various birds and beasts. Not far from Mount Utse is a mountain called Golden Wall, with eighty thousand caves. Eighty thousand elephant kings live in these caves, their bodies pure white with variegated heads, and their mouths with six tusks filled with gold. Beyond Mount Golden Wall is Mount Snow, five hundred yojanas long and wide, and five hundred yojanas deep, extending into the sea from east to west. In the middle of Mount Snow is a jeweled mountain, twenty yojanas high.

「过是地空，其空地中复有花池，纵广五十由旬，复有钵头摩池、俱物头池、分陀利池，毒蛇满中，各纵广五十由旬。过是地空，其空地中有大海水，名欝禅那，此水下有转轮圣王道，广十二由旬。挟道两边有七重墙、七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成，阎浮提地转轮圣王出于世时，水自然去，其道平现。去海不远有山，名欝禅，其山端严，树木繁茂，花果炽盛，众香芬馥，异类禽兽靡所不有。去欝禅山不远有山，名金壁，中有八万岩窟，八万象王止此窟中，其身纯白，头有杂色，口有六牙，齿间金填。过金壁山已，有山名雪山，纵广五百由旬，深五百由旬，东西入海，雪山中间有宝山，高二十由旬。

Mount Snow rises one hundred yojanas high. On the summit of the mountain is Lake Anavatapta, fifty yojanas long and wide. Its water is clear, cool, pure, and unpolluted. It is paved with the seven treasures, with sevenfold railings, sevenfold nets, and sevenfold rows of trees, all of various colors, made of the seven treasures. The railings are golden with silver crossbars, silver with golden crossbars, lapis lazuli with crystal crossbars, crystal with lapis lazuli crossbars, red pearl with agate crossbars, agate with red pearl crossbars, and carnelian with all kinds of precious crossbars. The golden net has silver bells, the silver net has golden bells, the lapis lazuli net has crystal bells, the crystal net has lapis lazuli bells, the carnelian net has all kinds of precious bells. The golden tāla tree has a golden root and branches, silver leaves and fruit, the silver tāla tree has a silver root and branches, golden leaves and fruit, the crystal tree has a crystal root and branches, lapis lazuli flowers and fruit, the red pearl tree has a red pearl root and branches, agate leaves and flowers and fruit, the carnelian tree has a carnelian root and branches, all kinds of precious flowers and fruit.

「雪山埵出高百由旬，其山顶上有阿耨达池，纵广五十由旬，其水清冷，澄净无秽，七宝砌垒、七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，种种异色，七宝合成。其栏楯者，金栏银桄，银栏金桄，琉璃栏水精桄，水精栏琉璃桄，赤珠栏马瑙桄，马瑙栏赤珠桄，车璩栏众宝所成。金网银铃，银网金铃，琉璃网水精铃，水精网琉璃铃，车璩网七宝所成。金多罗树金根金枝银叶银果，银多罗树银根银枝金叶金果，水精树水精根枝琉璃花果，赤珠树赤珠根枝马瑙叶马瑙花果，车璩树车璩根枝众宝花果。

"Beside Lake Anavatapta are gardens and ponds, with flowers piled up, various tree leaves, abundant flowers and fruits, various fragrant breezes blowing in all directions, and various kinds of birds singing harmoniously. The bottom of Lake Anavatapta is filled with golden sand. On the four sides of the lake are all steps, with golden crossbars and silver steps, silver crossbars and golden steps, lapis lazuli crossbars and crystal steps, crystal crossbars and lapis lazuli steps, red pearl crossbars and agate steps, agate crossbars and red pearl steps, carnelian crossbars and all kinds of precious steps. Around the lake are all railings, with four kinds of flowers - blue, yellow, red, and white, mixed together, the flowers are like wheels, and the flower roots are like wheels. The juice from the flower roots is white like milk, and tastes sweet like honey. To the east of Lake Anavatapta is the Ganges River, which flows from the mouth of an ox and enters the Eastern Sea with five hundred rivers. To the south of Lake Anavatapta is the Sindhu River, which flows from the mouth of a lion and enters the Southern Sea with five hundred rivers. To the west of Lake Anavatapta is the Vaksu River, which flows from the mouth of a horse and enters the Western Sea with five hundred rivers. To the north of Lake Anavatapta is the Sita River, which flows from the mouth of an elephant and enters the Northern Sea with five hundred rivers. In the palace of Anavatapta is a five-pillar hall, where the dragon king Anavatapta always resides."

「阿耨达池侧皆有园观浴池，众花积聚，种种树叶，花果繁茂，种种香风，芬馥四布，种种异类，诸鸟哀鸣相和。阿耨达池底，金沙充满。其池四边皆有梯陛，金桄银陛，银桄金陛，琉璃桄水精陛，水精桄琉璃陛，赤珠桄马瑙陛，马瑙桄赤珠陛，车璩桄众宝陛。遶池周匝皆有栏楯，生四种花，青、黄、赤、白，杂色参间，华如车轮，根如车毂，花根出汁，色白如乳，味甘如蜜。阿耨达池东有恒伽河，从牛口出，从五百河入于东海。阿耨达池南有新头河，从师子口出，从五百河入于南海。阿耨达池西有婆叉河，从马口出，从五百河入于西海。阿耨达池北有斯陀河，从象口中出，从五百河入于北海。阿耨达宫中有五柱堂，阿耨达龙王恒于中止。」

The Buddha said, "Why is it called Anavatapta? What does Anavatapta mean? All the dragon kings in this Jambudvipa have three afflictions, but the dragon king Anavatapta has none of the three afflictions. What are the three? First, all the dragons in Jambudvipa are scorched by hot winds and hot sand, burning their skin, flesh, and bones, causing them pain and suffering. The dragon king Anavatapta has none of these afflictions. Second, in the palaces of all the dragons in Jambudvipa, violent winds blow, blowing away their jeweled ornaments and revealing their dragon bodies, causing them pain and suffering. The dragon king Anavatapta has none of these afflictions. Third, when all the dragon kings in Jambudvipa are in their palaces enjoying themselves, the great garuḍa bird enters the palace and seizes them, or just born, to eat them. The dragons are terrified and always suffer from heat. The dragon king Anavatapta has none of these afflictions; if the garuḍa bird has the thought of going there, it will immediately die, thus it is called Anavatapta."

佛言：「何故名为阿耨达？阿耨达其义云何？此阎浮提所有龙王尽有三患，唯阿耨达龙无有三患。云何为三？一者举阎浮提所有诸龙，皆被热风、热沙著身，烧其皮肉，及烧骨髓以为苦恼，唯阿耨达龙无有此患。二者举阎浮提所有龙宫，恶风暴起，吹其宫内，失宝饰衣，龙身自现以为苦恼，唯阿耨达龙王无如是患。三者举阎浮提所有龙王，各在宫中相娱乐时，金翅大鸟入宫搏撮或始生方便，欲取龙食，诸龙怖惧，常怀热恼，唯阿耨达龙无如此患；若金翅鸟生念欲往] cf.【丽】，即便命终，故名阿耨达。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "To the right of the Snow Mountains is a city called Vaiśālī. To the north of the city are seven black mountains. To the north of the seven black mountains is the Fragrant Mountain. On the mountain there is always the sound of singing, music, and playing. There are two caves on the mountain, one named Day and the other named Good Day. They are made of the seven treasures of heaven, soft and fragrant, like heavenly garments. The gandharva king of wonderful sounds lives there with five hundred gandharvas. To the north of the Day and Good Day caves is a king of śāla trees named Good Abiding, surrounded by eight thousand trees on all sides. Under the Good Abiding tree is an elephant king also named Good Abiding, living under the tree. Its body is pure white, standing evenly on seven places. It can fly with strength. Its head is red, with variegated hair in between. It has six slender tusks filled with gold. It is surrounded and followed by eight thousand elephants. The eight thousand elephants under the eight thousand trees are also like this.

佛告比丘：「雪山右面有城，名毗舍离，其城北有七黑山，七黑山北有香山，其山常有歌唱伎乐音乐之声。山有二窟，一名为昼，二名善昼，天七宝成，柔濡香洁，犹如天衣，妙音干闼婆王从五百干闼婆在其中止。昼、善昼窟北有娑罗树王，名曰善住，有八千树王围遶四面。善住树王下有象王，亦名善住，止此树下，身体纯白，七处平住，力能飞行，其头赤色，杂色毛间，六牙纤佣，金为间填，有八千象围遶随从；其八千树王下八千象，亦复如是。

To the north of the Good Abiding tree is a great bathing pond named Motian, fifty yojanas long and wide, surrounded by eight thousand bathing ponds. The water is clear and cool, without any dust or impurities. It is surrounded by seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven rows of trees, all made of the seven treasures. The golden railings have silver crossbars, the silver railings have golden crossbars, the crystal railings have lapis lazuli crossbars, the lapis lazuli railings have crystal crossbars, the red pearl railings have agate crossbars, the agate railings have red pearl crossbars, and the carnelian railings have various precious crossbars. The golden nets hang silver bells, the silver nets hang golden bells, the crystal nets hang lapis lazuli bells, the lapis lazuli nets hang crystal bells, the red pearl nets hang agate bells, the agate nets hang red pearl bells, and the carnelian nets hang various precious bells. The golden trees have golden roots and branches, silver leaves and fruits. The silver trees have silver roots and branches, golden leaves and fruits. The crystal trees have crystal roots and branches, lapis lazuli flowers and fruits. The lapis lazuli trees have lapis lazuli roots and branches, crystal flowers and fruits. The red pearl trees have red pearl roots and branches, agate flowers and fruits. The agate trees have agate roots and branches, red pearl flowers and fruits. The carnelian trees have carnelian roots and branches, various precious flowers and fruits.

「善住树王北有大浴池，名摩陀延，纵广五十由旬，有八千浴池周匝围遶，其水清凉，无有尘秽，以七宝堑周匝砌垒，遶池有七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，皆七宝成，金栏银桄，银栏金桄，水精栏琉璃桄，琉璃栏水精桄，赤珠栏马瑙桄，马瑙栏赤珠桄，车璩栏众宝桄。其金罗网下埀银铃，其银罗网下埀金铃，水精罗网埀琉璃铃，琉璃罗网埀水精铃，赤珠罗网垂马瑙铃，马瑙罗网埀赤珠铃，砗璩罗网埀众宝铃。其金树者金根金枝银叶花实，其银树者银根银枝金叶花实，水精树者水精根枝琉璃花实，琉璃树者琉璃根枝水精花实，赤珠树者赤珠根枝马瑙花实，马瑙树者马瑙根枝赤珠花实，砗璩树者车璩根枝众宝花实。

The bottom of the pond is covered with golden sand. Around the pond are seven steps made of the seven treasures. The golden steps have silver treads, the silver steps have golden treads, the crystal steps have lapis lazuli treads, the lapis lazuli steps have crystal treads, the red pearl steps have agate treads, the agate steps have red pearl treads, and the carnelian steps have various precious treads. On both sides of the steps are jeweled railings. In the pond grow four kinds of flowers, blue, yellow, red, and white, with various colors mixed. The flowers are like cart wheels, and their roots are like cart hubs. The sap from the flower roots is white like milk, and tastes sweet like honey. Around the pond on all sides are various gardens, groves, and ponds, growing various flowers. The trees are cool, with abundant flowers and fruits. The birds of various kinds sing harmoniously, also like this. When the Good Abiding elephant king wants to play and bathe in the pond, he thinks of the eight thousand elephant kings. Then the eight thousand elephant kings also think to themselves, 'The Good Abiding elephant king is now thinking of us. We should go to where the elephant king is.' Then the elephants immediately go forward and stand before him.

「又其池底金沙布散，遶池周匝有七宝阶道，金陛银蹬，银陛金蹬，水精陛琉璃蹬，琉璃陛水精蹬，赤珠陛马瑙蹬，马瑙陛赤珠蹬，车璩陛众宝蹬。挟陛两边有宝栏楯。又其池中生四种华，青、黄、赤、白，众色参间，华如车轮，根如车毂，花根出汁，色白如乳，味甘如蜜。遶池四面有众园观、丛林、浴池，生种种花，树木清凉，花果丰盛，无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。善住象王念欲游戏，入池浴时，即念八千象王，时，八千象王复自念言：『善住象王今以念我，我等宜往至象王所。』于是，众象即往前立。

Then the Good Abiding elephant king, with the eight thousand elephants, went to the Motian pond. Among the elephants, some held parasols for the king, some held jeweled fans to fan the elephant king, and some performed music and dance as a leading escort. At that time, the Good Abiding elephant king entered the pond to bathe, performed music and dance, and enjoyed himself together. Some elephants washed the king's nose, some washed his mouth, head, tusks, ears, belly, back, tail, and feet. Some pulled out flower roots, washed them, and fed them to the king. Some took the four kinds of flowers and scattered them over the king. At that time, the Good Abiding elephant king, after bathing and eating, enjoyed himself together. He then came out of the pond and stood under the Good Abiding tree. The eight thousand elephants then each entered the pond to bathe, eat, and enjoy themselves. After finishing, they came out and went to where the elephant king was.

「时，善住象王从八千象至摩陀延池，其诸象中有为王持盖者，有执宝扇扇象王者，中有作倡伎乐前导从者。时，善住象王入池洗浴，作倡伎乐，共相娱乐，或有象为王洗鼻者，或有洗口、洗头、洗牙、洗耳、洗腹、洗背、洗尾、洗足者，中有拔华根洗之与王食者，中有取四种花散王上者。尔时，善住象王洗浴、饮食，共相娱乐已，即出岸上，向善住树立。其八千象然后各自入池洗浴、饮食，共相娱乐。讫已还出，至象王所。

"Then the elephant king, with the eight thousand elephants as a leading escort, went to the Good Abiding tree king. Some held parasols to cover the elephant king, some held jeweled fans to fan the elephant king, and some performed music and dance as a leading escort. At that time, the Good Abiding elephant king, after arriving at the tree king, sat, lay down, and walked as he pleased. The remaining eight thousand elephants each sat, lay down, and walked as they pleased under their own trees. In the grove, there were trees with a circumference of eight zhang, nine zhang, up to ten zhang, and fifteen zhang. Only the Good Abiding elephant king's banyan tree king had a circumference of sixteen zhang. When the branches and leaves of the eight thousand banyan trees fell, a gentle breeze blew them far outside the grove. Also, when the eight thousand elephants defecated and urinated, the yakṣa ghosts removed them outside the grove."

「时，象王从八千象前后导从，至善住树王所，中有持葢覆象王者，有执宝扇扇象王者，中有作倡伎乐在前导者。时，善住象王诣树王已，坐卧行步随意所游，余八千象各自在树下，坐卧行步随意所游。其树林中有围八寻者，有围九寻至十寻、十五寻者，唯善住象王婆罗树王围十六寻，其八千婆罗树枝叶堕落时，清风远吹置于林外，又八千象大小便时，诸夜叉鬼除之林外。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "The Good Abiding elephant king has great divine power and merits like this. Although he is an animal, he receives blessings like this."

佛告比丘：「善住象王有大神力，功德如是，虽为畜生，受福如是。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "In the Uttarakuru world, there are many mountains. On the sides of those mountains, there are gardens, ponds, and various flowers. The trees are cool, with abundant flowers and fruits. Countless birds sing harmoniously together. Moreover, in those mountains, there are many flowing streams. The water is gentle and not abrupt. Covered with various flowers, it flows slowly. On both sides of the banks, there are many trees with soft branches and abundant flowers and fruits. The ground is covered with soft grass, curling to the right, the color like a peacock's feathers, the fragrance like a pārijāta flower, and soft like heavenly garments. The ground is soft and smooth. When one steps on the ground, it sinks four inches, and when one lifts the foot, it returns to level, as flat as the palm of the hand, without any high or low.

佛告比丘：「欝单曰天下多有诸山，其彼山侧有诸园观浴池，生众杂花，树木清凉，花果丰茂，无数众鸟相和而鸣。又其山中多众流水，其水洋顺，无有卒暴，众花复上，泛泛徐流。挟岸两边多众树木，枝条柔弱，花果繁炽，地生濡草，槃萦右旋，色如孔翠，香如婆师，濡若天衣，其地柔濡，以足蹈] cf.【丽】地，地凹四寸，举足还复，地平如掌，无有高下。

Bhikṣus! In the Uttarakuru land, there are four Anavatapta ponds on the four sides, each one hundred yojanas in length and width. The water is clear and free from impurities. The banks are lined with the seven treasures, and there are countless birds singing harmoniously together, just like the Madhyamaka pond. The four great ponds each give rise to four great rivers, ten yojanas wide. The water is gentle and not abrupt, covered with various flowers, flowing slowly. On both sides of the banks, there are many trees with soft branches and abundant flowers and fruits. The ground is covered with soft grass, curling to the right, the color like a peacock's feathers, the fragrance like a pārijāta flower, and soft like heavenly garments. The ground is soft and smooth. When one steps on the ground, it sinks four inches, and when one lifts the foot, it returns to level, as flat as the palm of the hand, without any high or low.

「比丘！彼欝单曰土四面有四阿耨达池，各纵广百由旬，其水澄清，无有垢秽，以七宝堑厕砌其边，乃至无数众鸟相和悲鸣，与摩陀延池严饰无异。彼四大池各出四大河，广十由旬，其水洋顺，无有卒暴，众花复上，泛泛徐流。挟岸两边多众树木，枝条柔弱，花果繁炽，地生濡草，槃萦右旋，色如孔翠，香犹婆师，濡若天衣，其地柔濡，以足蹈地，地凹四寸，举足还复，地平如掌，无有高下。又彼土地无有沟涧、坑坎、荆棘、株杌，亦无蚊虻、蚖蛇、蜂蝎、虎豹、恶兽，地纯众宝，无有石沙，阴阳调柔，四气和顺，不寒不热，无众恼患，其地润泽，尘秽不起，如油涂地，无有游尘，百草常生，无有冬夏，树木繁茂，花果炽盛，地生濡草，槃萦右旋，色如孔翠，香犹婆师，濡若天衣，其地柔濡，以足蹈地，地凹四寸，举足还复，地平如掌，无有高下。

The land always has naturally grown glutinous rice, which grows without planting and is free from husks, like a cluster of white flowers. It is like the food of the Trāyastriṃśa Heaven, with all flavors complete. The land always has naturally grown cauldrons and pots, with a jewel called flame light placed under the pots. When the rice is cooked, the light goes out. It does not require firewood or human effort. There are trees in the land called bent body, with leaves overlapping each other. When it rains, it does not leak. The men and women of that land take shelter under them. There are also fragrant trees, seventy yojanas high, with abundant flowers and fruits. When the fruits ripen, the shells split open by themselves and the fragrance naturally comes out. Some of the trees are sixty yojanas high, some fifty, forty, and the smallest is five yojanas high. They are all abundant with flowers and fruits. When the fruits ripen, the shells split open by themselves and the fragrance naturally comes out.

「其土常有自然粳米，不种自生，无有糠糩，如白花聚，犹忉利天食，众味具足。其土常有自然釜鍑，有摩尼珠，名曰焰光，置于鍑下，饭熟光灭，不假樵火，不劳人功。其土有树，名曰曲躬，叶叶相次，天雨不漏，彼诸男女止宿其下。复有香树，高七十里，花果繁茂，其果熟时，皮壳自裂，自然香出，其树或高六十里，或五十、四十，极小高五里，皆花果繁茂，其果熟时，皮壳自裂，自然香出。

There are also clothing trees, seventy yojanas high, with abundant flowers and fruits. When the fruits ripen, the shells split open by themselves and various kinds of clothing come out. Some of the trees are sixty yojanas high, some fifty, forty, and the smallest is five yojanas high. They are all abundant with flowers and fruits, producing various kinds of clothing.

「复有衣树，高七十里，花果繁茂，其果熟时，皮壳自裂，出种种衣，其树或高六十里、五十、四十，极小高五里，皆花果繁茂，出种种衣。复有庄严树，高七十里，花果繁茂，其果熟时，皮壳自裂，出种种严身之具，其树或高六十里、五十、四十里，极小高五里，皆花果繁茂，出种种严身之具。复有花鬘树，高七十里，花果繁茂，其果熟时，皮壳自裂，出种种鬘，树或高六十里、五十、四十里，极小高五里，亦皆花果繁茂，出种种鬘。复有器树，高七十里，花果繁茂，其果熟时，皮壳自裂，出种种器，其树或高六十里、五十、四十，极小高五里，皆花果繁茂，出种种器。复有果树，高七十里，花果繁茂，其果熟时，皮壳自裂，出种种果，树或高六十里、五十、四十，极小高五里，皆花果繁茂，出种种果。复有乐器树，高七十里，花果繁茂，其果熟时，皮壳自裂，出种种乐器，其树或高六十里、五十、四十，极小高五里，皆花果繁茂，出种种乐器。

There is a pond in the land called Good View, one hundred yojanas long and wide. The water is clear and pure, without any impurities. It is surrounded by seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven rows of trees, all the way to the countless birds singing harmoniously, also like this.

「其土有池，名曰善见，纵广百由旬，其水清澄，无有垢秽，以七宝堑厕砌其边，遶池四面有七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。其善见池北有树，名庵婆罗，周围七里，上高百里，枝叶四布遍五十里。其善见池东出善道河，广一由旬，其水徐流，无有洄澓，种种杂花覆蔽水上，挟岸两边树木繁茂，枝条柔弱，花果炽盛，地生濡草，槃萦右旋，色如孔翠，香如婆师，濡若天衣，其地柔濡，足蹈] cf.【丽】地时，地凹四寸，举足还复，地平如掌，无有高下。

There are also various jeweled boats in the river. When the people of that land want to enter the river to bathe and play, they take off their clothes on the shore, board the boat in the middle of the river, and play and enjoy themselves. When they are done, they cross the water, pick up their clothes, and put them on. The first ones out put them on first, and the last ones out put them on last. They do not seek their original clothes.

「又其河中有众宝船，彼方人民欲入中洗浴游戏时，脱衣岸上，乘船中流，游戏娱乐讫已，度水遇衣便著，先出先著，后出后著，不求本衣。次至香树，树为曲躬，其人手取种种杂香，以自涂身。次到衣树，树为曲躬，其人手取种种杂衣，随意所著。次到庄严树，树为曲躬，其人手取种种庄严，以自严饰。次到鬘树，树为曲躬，其人手取种种杂鬘，以著头上。次到器树，树为曲躬，其人手取种种宝器，取宝器已。次到果树，树为曲躬，其人手取种种美果，或噉食者，或口含者，或漉汁饮者。次到乐器树，树为曲躬，其人手取种种乐器，调弦鼓之，并以妙声和弦，而行诣于园林，随意娱乐，或一日、二日至于七日，然后复去，无有定处。

To the south of the Good View Pond flows the River of Wonderful Body, to the west flows the River of Wonderful Taste, and to the north flows the River of Light and Shadow, also like this.

「善见池南出妙体河，善见池西出妙味河，善见池北出光影河，亦复如是。善见池东有园林名善见，纵广百由旬，遶园四边有七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，杂色间厕，七宝所成，其园四面有四大门，周匝栏楯，皆七宝成。园内清净，无有荆棘，其地平正，无有沟涧、坑坎、陵阜，亦无蚊虻、蝇蚤虱、蚖蛇、蜂蝎、虎狼、恶兽，地纯众宝，无有石沙，阴阳调柔，四气和顺，不寒不热，无众恼患，其地润泽，无有尘秽，如油涂地，游尘不起，百草常生，无有冬夏，树木繁茂，花果炽盛，地生濡草，盘萦右旋，色如孔翠，香如婆师，濡若天衣，其地柔濡，足蹈地时，地凹四寸，举足还复。

There is a garden called Good View to the east of the Good View Pond, one hundred yojanas long and wide, surrounded by seven railings, seven nets, and seven rows of trees, interspersed with various colors, made of the seven treasures. The garden has four great gates on all four sides, surrounded by railings, all made of the seven treasures. The garden inside is pure, without thorns or brambles. The ground is level, without ditches, pits, or hills. There are also no mosquitoes, flies, fleas, lice, snakes, bees, wasps, tigers, wolves, or vicious beasts. The ground is pure gold, without stones or sand. The yin and yang are balanced, and the four seasons are harmonious. It is neither cold nor hot, without any afflictions. The ground is moist and free from dust and dirt, like oil smeared on the ground, with no dust rising. Various grasses grow all year round, without winter or summer. The trees are luxuriant, with abundant flowers and fruits. The ground grows soft grass, curling to the right, the color like a peacock's feathers, the fragrance like the pāśīka flower, and as soft as heavenly garments. When one steps on the ground, it sinks four inches, and when one lifts the foot, it returns to its original state.

「其园常生自然粳米，无有糠糩，如白花聚，众味具足，如忉利天食。其园常有自然釜鍑，有摩尼珠，名曰焰光，置于鍑下，饭熟光灭，不假樵火，不劳人功。其园有树，名曰曲躬，叶叶相次，天雨不漏，使诸男女止宿其下。复有香树，高七十里，花果繁茂，其果熟时，皮壳自裂，出种种香，树有高六十里、五十、四十，至高五里，花果繁茂，出种种香，乃至乐器树，亦复如是。其土人民至彼园中游戏娱乐，一日、二日，至于七日，其善见园无人守护，随意游戏，然后复去。

To the south of the Good View Pond is a garden called Great Good View. To the west of the Good View Pond is a garden called Entertainment. To the north of the Good View Pond is a garden called Equal Flowers, also like this.

「善见池南有园林，名大善见。善见池西有园林，名曰娱乐。善见池北有园林，名曰等花，亦复如是。其土中夜、后夜，阿耨达龙王数数随时起清净云，周遍世界而降甘雨，如搆牛顷，以八味水润泽普洽，水不留停，地无泥淖，犹如鬘师以水洒华，使不萎枯，润泽鲜明。时，彼土于中夜后无有云翳，空中清明，海出凉风，清净柔和，微吹人身，举体快乐。其土丰饶，人民炽盛，设须食时，以自然粳米著于釜中，以焰光珠置于釜下，饭自然熟，珠光自灭。诸有来者，自恣食之，其主不起，饭终不尽；若其主起，饭则尽赐。其饭鲜洁，如白花聚，其味具足，如忉利天食，彼食此饭，无有众病，气力充足，颜色和悦，无有衰耗。

The people of that land are similar in appearance, with equal features, indistinguishable. Their appearance is youthful, like twenty people in Jambudvīpa. Their teeth are even, clean, and white, close together without gaps. Their hair is dark blue, without dust or dirt. Their hair hangs down eight fingers, stopping at the eyebrows, neither long nor short. When the people of that land give rise to desire, they look at the woman and leave. The woman follows to the garden. If that woman is a relative of the man's father or mother, the tree does not bend to shade them, and they disperse. If she is not a relative of the man's father or mother, the tree bends to shade them, and they can enjoy themselves as they please for one, two, or up to seven days before dispersing. When the woman becomes pregnant, after seven or eight days she gives birth. The child is placed at the crossroads and left there. Travelers passing by will suckle the child, and sweet milk will flow from their fingers to nourish the child. After seven days, the child grows to be the same size as the people there. The boys go to the boys' group, and the girls go to the girls' group.

「又其土] cf.【丽】人身体相类，形貌同等，不可分别，其貌少壮，如阎浮提二十许人，其人口齿平正洁白，密致无间，发绀青色，无有尘垢，发埀八指，齐眉而止，不长不短。若其土人起欲心时，则熟视女人而舍之去，彼女随后往诣园林，若彼女人是彼男子父亲、母亲骨肉中表不应行欲者，树不曲荫，各自散去。若非父亲、母亲骨肉中表应行欲者，树则曲躬，回荫其身，随意娱乐，一日、二日，或至七日，尔乃散去。彼人怀姙，七日、八日便产，随生男女，置于四衢大交道头，舍之而去。诸有行人经过其边，出指令嗽，指出甘乳，充适儿身。过七日已，其儿长成与彼人等，男向男众，女向女众。

When they die, they do not cry or mourn. They adorn the corpse and leave it at the crossroads. There is a bird called Ucchedaka that takes the corpse to another place. Also, when the people of that land defecate, the ground opens up for them, and when they are done, the ground closes up again. The people of that land have no attachments or hoarding. Their lifespan is always fixed, and when they die, they are reborn in heaven. Why is the lifespan of those people always fixed? In their past lives, they practiced the ten wholesome actions. When their bodies disintegrated and their lives ended, they were reborn in Uttarakuru, with a lifespan of one thousand years, neither increasing nor decreasing. Therefore, the lifespan of those people is exactly the same.

「彼人命终，不相哭泣，庄严死尸，置四衢道，舍之而去；有鸟名忧慰禅伽，接彼死尸置于他方。又其土人，大小便时，地即为开，便利讫已，地还自合。其土人民无所系恋，亦无畜积，寿命常定，死尽生天。彼人何故寿命常定？其人前世修十善行，身坏命终，生欝单曰，寿命千岁，不增不减。是故彼人寿命正等。

"Furthermore, those who kill fall into evil destinies, while those who do not kill are reborn in good destinies. Those who steal, engage in sexual misconduct, speak divisively, harshly, falsely, or frivolously, are covetous, jealous, and have wrong views fall into evil destinies; those who do not steal, engage in sexual misconduct, speak divisively, harshly, falsely, or frivolously, are not covetous, jealous, or have wrong views are reborn in good destinies. If there are those who do not kill, steal, engage in sexual misconduct, speak divisively, harshly, falsely, or frivolously, are not covetous, jealous, or have wrong views, and when their bodies disintegrate and their lives end, they are reborn in Uttarakuru, with a lifespan of one thousand years, neither increasing nor decreasing. Therefore, the lifespan of those people is exactly the same. Furthermore, those who are stingy and covetous, unable to give, fall into evil destinies when they die; those who open their hearts, are not stingy, and are able to give are reborn in good places. There are those who give to śramaṇas, brāhmaṇas, and the poor, beggars, the sick, and the suffering, providing them with clothing, food, carriages, flower garlands, perfumes, beds, and dwellings, and also building stupas and offering lamps. When their bodies disintegrate and their lives end, they are reborn in Uttarakuru, with a lifespan of one thousand years, neither increasing nor decreasing. Therefore, the lifespan of those people is exactly the same. Why is Uttarakuru called superior? The people of that land do not practice the ten wholesome actions, but their movements naturally accord with the ten wholesome actions. When their bodies disintegrate and their lives end, they are reborn in the good destinies of the heavens. Therefore, those people are called superior Uttarakuru. What does Uttarakuru mean? Among the three worlds, that land is the most supreme and superior, so it is called Uttarakuru."

「复次，杀生者堕恶趣，不杀者生善趣，如是窃盗、邪婬、两舌、恶口、妄言、绮语、贪取、嫉妬、邪见者，堕恶趣中；不盗，不婬，不两舌、恶口、妄言、绮语，不贪取、嫉妬、邪见者，则生善趣。若有不杀，不盗，不婬，不两舌、恶口、妄言、绮语，不贪取、嫉妬、邪见，身坏命终，生欝单曰，寿命千岁，不增不减。是故彼人寿命正等。复次，悭悋贪取，不能施惠，死堕恶道；开心不悋，能为施惠者，则生善处。有人施沙门、婆罗门，及施贫穷乞儿、疮病、困苦者，给其衣服、饭食、乘舆、花鬘、涂香、床［木＊翕］、房舍，又造立塔庙，灯烛供养，其人身坏命终，生欝单曰，寿命千岁，不增不减。是故彼人寿命正等。何故称欝单曰为胜？其土人民不受十善，举动自然与十善合，身坏命终，生天善处，是故彼人得称为胜欝单曰。欝单曰者，其义云何？于三天下，其土最上最胜，故名欝单曰。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "In the world, there are wheel-turning sage kings who accomplish the seven treasures and possess the four divine virtues. How do wheel-turning sage kings accomplish the seven treasures? First, the golden wheel treasure, second, the white elephant treasure, third, the dark horse treasure, fourth, the divine jewel treasure, fifth, the jade woman treasure, sixth, the householder treasure, and seventh, the military commander treasure. How do wheel-turning sage kings accomplish the golden wheel treasure? If a wheel-turning sage king appears in the land of Jambudvīpa, of the kṣatriya water-sprinkled head family, on the full moon day of the fifteenth, bathing in fragrant water, ascending to the high palace, together with the harem women enjoying entertainment, a heavenly golden wheel treasure suddenly appears before him, with a thousand spokes, its radiance complete, made of heavenly gold, crafted by heavenly artisans, not of the world, with a diameter of four zhang. The wheel-turning sage king, seeing it, silently thinks to himself: 'I have heard from the elders that if a kṣatriya king of the water-sprinkled head family, on the full moon day of the fifteenth, bathing in fragrant water, ascending to the Dharma hall, surrounded by harem women, a golden wheel suddenly appears before him, with a thousand spokes, its radiance complete, crafted by heavenly artisans, not of the world, with a diameter of four zhang, then he is called a wheel-turning sage king. Now that this wheel appears, could it be so? Now I should test this wheel treasure.'

佛告比丘：「世间有转轮圣王，成就七宝，有四神德。云何转轮圣王成就七宝？一金轮宝，二白象宝，三绀马宝，四神珠宝，五玉女宝，六居士宝，七主兵宝。云何转轮圣王金轮宝成就？若转轮圣王出阎浮提地，刹利水浇头种，以十五日月满时，沐浴香汤，上高殿上，与婇女众共相娱乐，天金轮宝忽现在前，轮有千辐，其光色具足，天金所成，天匠所造，非世所有，轮径丈四。转轮圣王见已，默自念言：『我曾从先宿诸旧闻如是语：「若刹利王水浇头种，以十五日月满时，沐浴香汤，升法殿上，婇女围遶，自然金轮忽现在前，轮有千辐，光色具足，天匠所造，非世所有，轮径丈四，是则名为转轮圣王。」今此轮现，将无是耶？今我宁可试此轮宝。』

At that time, the wheel-turning sage king immediately summoned the four divisions of troops, facing the golden wheel treasure, baring his right arm, kneeling on his right knee, stroking the golden wheel with his right hand, and saying: 'Turn towards the east according to the Dharma, do not violate the usual principles.' The wheel then turned east. At that time, the wheel-turning sage king immediately led the four divisions of troops to follow behind it. The four divine guides led the way in front of the golden wheel treasure. Wherever the wheel stopped, the king would halt his carriage. At that time, the kings of the small countries in the east saw the great king arrive. They brought golden bowls filled with silver grains and silver bowls filled with golden grains, came to where the king was, bowed their heads and said: 'Excellent! Great King! Now this land in the east is abundant and prosperous, with many precious treasures and a flourishing population. The people are kind and gentle, filial, loyal, and obedient. We only wish that the sage king would govern here. We will serve and obey you.' At that time, the wheel-turning sage king said to the small kings: 'Stop! Stop! All of you are already making offerings to me. You should only govern with the right Dharma, without partiality or injustice. Do not let there be any unrighteous conduct in the country. Do not kill living beings yourself, and do not teach others to kill living beings, steal, engage in sexual misconduct, speak divisively, harshly, falsely, or frivolously, be covetous, jealous, or have wrong views. This is what I call governing.'

「时，转轮王即召四兵，向金轮宝，偏露右臂，右膝著地，以右手摩扪金轮语言：『汝向东方，如法而转，勿违常则。』轮即东转。时，转轮王即将四兵随其后行，金轮宝前有四神导，轮所住处，王即止驾。尔时，东方诸小国王见大王至，以金钵盛银粟，银钵盛金粟，来诣王所，拜首白言：『善哉！大王！今此东方土地丰乐，多诸珍宝，人民炽盛，志性仁和，慈孝忠顺，唯愿圣王于此治政，我等当给使左右承受所当。』时，转轮王语小王言：『止！止！诸贤！汝等则为供养我已，但当以正法治化，勿使偏枉，无令国内有非法行，身不杀生，教人不杀生、偷盗、邪婬、两舌、恶口、妄言、绮语、贪取、嫉妬、邪见之人，此即名为我之所治。』

At that time, the small kings, having heard this teaching, immediately followed the great king on a tour of the countries, reaching the eastern seacoast. They then proceeded to the south, west, and north, wherever the wheel went. The kings of those countries each offered their lands, just like the small kings in the east. This Jambudvīpa is renowned for its fertile fields, abundant harvests, and many precious treasures. The forests and waters are pure and clean. Wherever the wheel goes, it measures and marks the land, extending twelve yojanas from east to west and ten yojanas from south to north. The divine beings build a city there during the night. The city has seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees, all adorned with the seven treasures, and so on, with countless birds singing harmoniously. After building the city, the golden wheel treasure again measures and marks the land within the city, extending four yojanas from east to west and two yojanas from south to north. The divine beings build a palace there during the night. The palace walls are also seven layers, made of the seven treasures, and so on, with countless birds singing harmoniously, just like before. After building the palace, the golden wheel treasure then abides in the sky above the palace, complete and unmoving. The wheel-turning sage king joyfully declares: 'This golden wheel treasure is truly a good omen for me. I am now truly a wheel-turning sage king.' This is called the accomplishment of the golden wheel treasure.

「时，诸小王闻是教已，即从大王巡行诸国，至东海表，次行南方、西方、北方，随轮所至，其诸国王各献国土，亦如东方诸小王比。此阎浮提所有名曰土沃野丰，多出珍宝，林水清净，平广之处，轮则周行，封尽图度东西十二由旬，南北十由旬，天神于中夜造城墎，其城七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，七宝所成，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣。造此城已，金轮宝复于其城中，图度封地东西四由旬，南北二由旬，天神于中夜造宫殿，宫墙七重，七宝所成，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。造宫殿已，时，金轮宝在宫殿上虚空中住，完具而不动转。转轮圣王踊跃而言：『此金轮宝真为我瑞，我今真为转轮圣王。』是为金轮宝成就。

What is meant by the accomplishment of the white elephant treasure? When the wheel-turning sage king sits in the main hall in the early morning, the white elephant treasure suddenly appears before him. Its fur is pure white, standing evenly on seven points, and it can fly with strength. Its head is multicolored, with six slender tusks inlaid with pure gold. At that time, the king, seeing it, thinks: 'This elephant is virtuous. If well-trained, it can be ridden.' He then tries to train it, and it is able to do all. At that time, the wheel-turning sage king wants to test the elephant himself. He rides it, leaving the city in the early morning, traveling around the four seas, and returning for a meal. At that time, the wheel-turning sage king joyfully declares: 'This white elephant treasure is truly a good omen for me. I am now truly a wheel-turning sage king.' This is called the accomplishment of the elephant treasure.

「云何白象宝成就？转轮圣王清旦于正殿上坐，自然象宝忽现在前，其毛纯白，七处平住，力能飞行，其首杂色，六牙纤佣，真金间填。时，王见已念言：『此象贤良，若善调者可中御乘。』即试调习，诸能悉备。时，转轮王欲自试象，即乘其上，清旦出城，周行四海，食时以还。时，转轮王踊跃而言：『此白象宝真为我瑞，我今真为转轮圣王。』是为象宝成就。

What is meant by the accomplishment of the wheel-turning sage king's dark blue horse treasure? When the wheel-turning sage king sits in the main hall in the early morning, the dark blue horse treasure suddenly appears before him. It is dark blue in color, with a red mane and tail, and a head and neck like an elephant. It can fly with strength. At that time, the king, seeing it, thinks: 'This horse is virtuous. If well-trained, it can be ridden.' He then tries to train it, and it is able to do all. At that time, the wheel-turning sage king wants to test the horse treasure himself. He rides it, leaving the city in the early morning, traveling around the four seas, and returning for a meal. At that time, the wheel-turning sage king joyfully declares: 'This dark blue horse treasure is truly a good omen for me. I am now truly a wheel-turning sage king.' This is called the accomplishment of the dark blue horse treasure.

「云何转轮圣王绀马宝成就？时，转轮圣王清旦在正殿上坐，自然马宝忽现在前，绀青色，朱騣尾，头颈如象，力能飞行。时，王见已念言：『此马贤良，若善调者，可中御乘。』即试调习，诸能悉备。时，转轮圣王欲自试马宝，即乘其上，清旦出城，周行四海，食时已还。时，转轮王踊跃而言：『此绀马宝真为我瑞，我今真为转轮圣王。』是为绀马宝成就。

What is meant by the accomplishment of the wheel-turning sage king's divine jewel treasure? When the wheel-turning sage king sits in the main hall in the early morning, the divine jewel treasure suddenly appears before him. Its substance is clear and pure, without flaws. At that time, the king, seeing it, says: 'This jewel is wonderful. If it has light, it can illuminate the palace.' At that time, the wheel-turning sage king wants to test this jewel. He immediately summons the four divisions of troops, places this jewel on a tall banner, and carries the banner out of the city at night. The light of the jewel illuminates one yojana, and the people in the city all rise to work, thinking it is daytime. At that time, the wheel-turning sage king joyfully declares: 'This divine jewel is truly a good omen for me. I am now truly a wheel-turning sage king.' This is called the accomplishment of the divine jewel treasure.

「云何神珠宝成就？时，转轮圣王于清旦在正殿上坐，自然神珠忽现在前，质色清彻，无有瑕秽。时，王见已言：『此珠妙好，若有光明，可照宫内。』时，转轮王欲试此珠，即召四兵，以此宝珠置高幢上，于夜冥中，赍幢出城。其珠光明照一由旬，现城中人皆起作务，谓为是昼。时，转轮圣王踊跃而言：『今此神珠真为我瑞，我今真为转轮圣王。』是为神珠宝成就。

What is meant by the accomplishment of the wheel-turning sage king's jade maiden treasure? When the jade maiden treasure suddenly appears, her complexion is radiant, her facial features are upright, she is neither tall nor short, neither coarse nor fine, neither white nor black, neither hard nor soft. In winter, her body is warm, and in summer, her body is cool. The pores of her body emit the fragrance of sandalwood, and her mouth emits the fragrance of blue lotus flowers. Her speech is gentle and her movements are calm. She rises first and sits later, never losing propriety. At that time, the wheel-turning sage king, seeing her, is unattached and does not think of her for a moment, let alone be intimate with her. At that time, the wheel-turning sage king, seeing her, joyfully declares: 'This jade maiden treasure is truly a good omen for me. I am now truly a wheel-turning sage king.' This is called the accomplishment of the jade maiden treasure.

「云何玉女宝成就？时，玉女宝忽然出现，颜色溶溶，面貌端正，不长不短，不麤不细，不白不黑，不刚不柔，冬则身温，夏则身凉，举身毛孔出栴檀香，口出优钵罗花香，言语柔濡，举动安详，先起后坐，不失宜则。时，转轮圣王见已无著，心不暂念，况复亲近？时，转轮圣王见已，踊跃而言：『此玉女宝真为我瑞，我今真为转轮圣王。』是为玉女宝成就。

What is meant by the accomplishment of the wheel-turning sage king's householder treasure? When the householder treasure suddenly appears, his treasure store is naturally boundless in wealth. The householder, due to past merit, can see through the ground and know where the hidden treasures are, whether they have an owner or not. For those with an owner, he can protect them; for those without an owner, he takes them to provide for the king. At that time, the householder treasure goes to the king and says: 'Great King! Do not worry about providing for me. I can provide for myself.' The wheel-turning sage king wants to test the householder treasure, so he orders a boat to be prepared for playing in the water. He tells the householder: 'I need gold and jewels. Bring them to me quickly.' The householder replies: 'Great King, please wait a moment. I need to go to the shore.' The king presses him, saying: 'I need them now. Bring them here quickly.' The householder treasure, being pressed by the king's order, kneels on the boat and puts his right hand into the water. Treasure vases in the water follow his hand and come out, like insects climbing a tree. The householder treasure is also like this. When he puts his hand in the water, treasures follow his hand and come out, filling the boat. He says to the king: 'Do you need treasures now? How many do you need?' The wheel-turning sage king tells the householder: 'Stop! Stop! I have no need. I was just testing you. You have already provided for me.' When the householder hears the king's words, he immediately puts the treasures back into the water. At that time, the wheel-turning sage king joyfully declares: 'This householder treasure is truly a good omen for me. I am now truly a wheel-turning sage king.' This is called the accomplishment of the householder treasure.

「云何居士宝成就？时，居士丈夫忽然自出，宝藏自然财富无量，居士宿福，眼能彻视地中伏藏，有主无主皆悉见知，其有主者能为拥护，其无主者取给王用。时，居士宝往白王言：『大王！有所给与，不足为忧，我自能办。』转轮圣王欲试居士宝，即勅严船于水游戏，告居士曰：『我须金宝，汝速与我。』居士报曰：『大王小待，须至岸上。』王寻逼言：『我今须用，正尔得来。』时，居士宝被王严勅，即于船上长跪，以右手内著水中，水中宝瓶随手而出，如虫缘树，彼居士宝亦复如是，内手水中，宝缘手出，充满船上，而白王言：『向须宝用，为须几许？』时，转轮圣王语居士言：『止！止！吾无所须，向相试耳，汝今便为供养我已。』时，居士闻王语已，寻以宝物还没水中。时，转轮圣王踊跃而言：『此居士宝真为我瑞，我今真为转轮圣王。』是为居士宝成就。

What is meant by the accomplishment of the wheel-turning sage king's military commander treasure? When the military commander treasure suddenly appears, he is wise, courageous, and decisive. He goes to the king and says: 'Great King! Do not worry about subduing and punishing. I can handle it myself.' At that time, the wheel-turning sage king wants to test the military commander treasure, so he assembles the four divisions and tells him: 'Now you use the army. Assemble those who are not assembled, dismiss those who are assembled, arm those who are not armed, disarm those who are armed, march those who are not marching, and halt those who are marching.' At that time, the military commander treasure, hearing the king's words, immediately orders the four divisions to assemble those who are not assembled, dismiss those who are assembled, arm those who are not armed, disarm those who are armed, march those who are not marching, and halt those who are marching. At that time, the wheel-turning sage king, seeing this, joyfully declares: 'This military commander treasure is truly a good omen for me. I am now truly a wheel-turning sage king.' This is called the accomplishment of the wheel-turning sage king's seven treasures.

「云何主兵宝成就？时，主兵宝忽然出现，智谋雄猛，英略独决，即诣王所白言：『大王！有所讨罚，不足为忧，我自能办。』时，转轮圣王欲试主兵宝，即集四兵而告之曰：『汝今用兵，未集者集，已集者放，未严者严，已严者解，未去者去，已去者住。』时，主兵宝闻王语已，即令四兵，未集者集，已集者放，未严者严，已严者解，未去者去，已去者住。时，转轮圣王见已，踊跃而言：『此主兵宝真为我瑞，我今真为转轮圣王。』是为转轮圣王七宝成就。

What is meant by the wheel-turning sage king's four divine virtues? The first is long life without premature death, which is unsurpassed. The second is a strong body without illness, which is unsurpassed. The third is a handsome and upright appearance, which is unsurpassed. The fourth is abundant treasure stores, which are unsurpassed. These are the wheel-turning sage king's accomplishment of the seven treasures and four divine virtues.

「谓四神德，一者长寿不夭无能及者，二者身强无患无能及者，三者颜貌端正无能及者，四者宝藏盈溢无能及者，是为转轮圣王成就七宝及四功德。

At that time, the wheel-turning sage king, after a long time, ordered the carriage to go out to the rear garden, and told the charioteer: 'You should drive well. Because I want to carefully observe the peace and happiness of the country and the people.' At that time, the people of the country who were watching by the roadside also said to their attendants: 'You should walk slowly. I want to carefully observe the majestic appearance of the sage king.' At that time, the wheel-turning sage king loved the people and the land like a father loves his children, and the people of the country admired the king like a child looks up to his father. They offered all their precious treasures to the king, hoping that he would accept them as he wished. At that time, the king replied: 'Stop! All of you! I already have treasures. You can keep them for yourselves.'

「时，转轮圣王久乃命驾出游后园，寻告御者：『汝当善御而行。所以然者？吾欲谛观国土人民安乐无患。』时，国人民路次观者，复语侍人：『汝且徐行，吾欲谛观圣王威颜。』时，转轮圣王慈育民物如父爱子，国民慕王如子仰父，所有珍琦尽以贡王，愿埀纳受，在意所与。时，王报曰：『且止！诸人！吾自有宝，汝可自用。』

When the wheel-turning sage king ruled this Jambudvīpa, the ground was level and even, without thorns, pits, mounds, or hills. There were also no mosquitoes, bees, wasps, flies, fleas, snakes, or other harmful insects. Pebbles, stones, and gravel naturally sank into the ground, and gold, silver, and jewels appeared on the surface. The four seasons were harmonious, neither cold nor hot. The ground was soft and smooth, without dust or dirt, like oil applied to the ground, clean and glossy. When the wheel-turning sage king ruled the world, the ground was also like this. There were flowing springs on the ground, pure and inexhaustible. Soft grass grew, always green in winter and summer. The trees were luxuriant, with abundant flowers and fruits. The ground produced soft grass, the color of a peacock's feathers, fragrant like a pāśa tree, soft like heavenly garments. When one stepped on the ground, it would sink four inches, and when one lifted one's foot, it would return to its original state, without any empty or vacant places. There was naturally grown rice without any husks, with all the flavors complete. At that time, there were fragrant trees with luxuriant flowers and fruits. When the fruits ripened, the shells would naturally split open, releasing natural fragrances that permeated the air. There were also clothing trees with luxuriant flowers and fruits. When the fruits ripened, the shells would naturally split open, revealing various garments. There were also adornment trees with luxuriant flowers and fruits. When the fruits ripened, the shells would naturally split open, revealing various adornment implements. There were also garland trees with luxuriant flowers and fruits. When the fruits ripened, the shells would naturally split open, revealing various garlands. There were also vessel trees with luxuriant flowers and fruits. When the fruits ripened, the shells would naturally split open, revealing various vessels. There were also fruit trees with luxuriant flowers and fruits. When the fruits ripened, the shells would naturally split open, revealing various fruits. There were also musical instrument trees with luxuriant flowers and fruits. When the fruits ripened, the shells would naturally split open, revealing various musical instruments.

「转轮圣王治此阎浮提时，其地平正，无有荆棘、坑坎、堆阜，亦无蚊虻、蜂蝎、蝇蚤、蛇蚖、恶虫，石沙、瓦砾自然沉没，金银宝玉现于地上，四时和调，不寒不热，其地柔濡，无有尘秽，如油涂地，洁净光泽，无有尘秽。转轮圣王治于世时，地亦如是，地出流泉，清净无竭，生柔濡草，冬夏常青，树木繁茂，花果炽盛，地生濡草，色如孔翠，香若婆师，濡如天衣，足蹈地时，地凹四寸，举足还复，无空缺处，自然粳米无有糠糩，众味具足。时有香树，花果茂盛，其果熟时，果自然裂，出自然香，香气馥熏。复有衣树，花果茂盛，其果熟时，皮壳自裂，出种种衣。复有庄严树，花果炽盛，其果熟时，皮壳自裂，出种种庄严具。复有鬘树，花果茂盛，其果熟时，皮壳自裂，出种种鬘。复有器树，花果茂盛，其果熟时，皮壳自裂，出种种器。复有果树，花果茂盛，其果熟时，皮壳自裂，出种种果。复有乐器树，花果茂盛，其果熟时，皮壳自裂，出众乐器。

When the wheel-turning sage king ruled the world, the dragon king Anavatapta would rise from the middle of the night and cover the world with thick clouds, then pour down a great rain in the time it takes to milk a cow. The rain would be of eight flavors, moistening everywhere. The ground would not retain any water, nor would there be any mud or mire. The moisture would be just right, nourishing the growth of plants and trees. It would be like a garland maker sprinkling water on flower garlands to keep them fresh and prevent them from wilting. The timely rain would be like this as well. Moreover, in the middle of the night, the sky would be clear and free from clouds and haze. A cool breeze would rise from the ocean, pure and gentle, touching the body and bringing pleasure. When the sage king ruled, in this Jambudvīpa the five grains would be abundant and cheap, the people would be prosperous, and wealth and treasures would be plentiful, without any lack.

「转轮圣王治于世时，阿耨达龙王于中夜后起大密云，弥满世界而降大雨，如搆牛顷，雨八味水，润泽周普，地无停水，亦无泥淖] cf.【丽】，润泽沾洽，生长草木。犹如鬘师水洒花鬘，使花鲜泽，令不萎枯，时雨润泽，亦复如是。又时于中夜后，空中清明，净无云曀，海出凉风，清净调柔，触身生乐。圣王治时，此阎浮提五谷丰贱，人民炽盛，财宝丰饶，无所匮乏。

At that time, the wheel-turning sage king ruled the country righteously, without any injustice. He practiced the ten wholesome deeds. At that time, the people also practiced the right view and the ten wholesome deeds. After a long time, the king developed a serious illness and passed away. It was like a musician who, after eating a little too much, became slightly uncomfortable and passed away. He was reborn in the Brahma Heaven. At that time, the queen, the chief minister, the general, and the people of the country played music and buried the sage king's body. The queen, the chief minister, the general, and the people of the country bathed the king's body with fragrant water, wrapped it in five hundred layers of fine silk, and placed it in a golden coffin. They poured fragrant oil on it and placed it in an iron coffin. They then wrapped it with another wooden coffin. They piled up fragrant firewood and cremated it at the crossroads. They built a seven-jeweled stupa one yojana wide and high, with various colors and made of seven jewels. The stupa had a gate on each of the four sides, surrounded by railings made of seven jewels. The ground around the stupa was five yojanas wide, with seven layers of walls, seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven rows of trees. The golden walls had silver gates, the silver walls had golden gates, the lapis lazuli walls had crystal gates, the crystal walls had lapis lazuli gates, the red pearl walls had agate gates, the agate walls had red pearl gates, and the vehicle-jade walls had gates made of various jewels. The railings were made of gold with silver crossbars, silver with gold crossbars, crystal with lapis lazuli crossbars, lapis lazuli with crystal crossbars, red pearls with agate crossbars, agate with red pearl crossbars, and vehicle jade with crossbars made of various jewels. The golden nets had silver bells hanging below, the silver nets had golden bells hanging below, the lapis lazuli nets had crystal bells hanging below, the crystal nets had lapis lazuli bells hanging below, the red pearl nets had agate bells hanging below, the agate nets had red pearl bells hanging below, and the vehicle jade nets had bells made of various jewels hanging below. The golden trees had silver leaves and fruits, the silver trees had golden leaves and fruits, the lapis lazuli trees had crystal leaves and flowers, the crystal trees had lapis lazuli leaves and flowers, the red pearl trees had agate leaves and flowers, the agate trees had red pearl leaves and flowers, and the vehicle jade trees had leaves and flowers made of various jewels. The four walls of the gardens had four gates, surrounded by railings. On top of the walls were pavilions and treasure platforms. The walls on all four sides had trees, gardens, flowing springs, and ponds with various flowers blooming. The trees were

「当时，转轮圣王以正治国，无有阿抂，修十善行，尔时诸人民亦修正见，具十善行。其王久久，身生重患，而取命终。时犹如乐人，食如小过，身小不适，而便命终，生梵天上。时玉女宝、居士宝、主兵宝及国士民作倡伎乐，葬圣王身。其王玉女宝、居士宝、主兵宝、国内士民，以香汤洗浴王身，以劫贝缠五百张叠，次如缠之，奉举王身，置金棺里，以香油灌置铁椁里。复以木椁重衣其外，积众香薪重衣其上，而耶维之，于四衢道头起七宝塔，纵广一由旬，杂色参间，以七宝成。其塔四面各有一门，周匝栏楯，以七宝成。其塔四面空地纵广五由旬，园墙七重、七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，金墙银门，银墙金门，琉璃墙水精门，水精墙琉璃门，赤珠墙马瑙门，马瑙墙赤珠门，车璩墙众宝门。其栏楯者，金栏银桄，银栏金桄，水精栏琉璃桄，琉璃栏水精桄，赤珠栏马瑙桄，马瑙栏赤珠桄，车璩栏众宝桄。其金罗网下悬银铃，其银罗网下悬金铃，琉璃罗网悬水精铃，水精罗网悬琉璃铃，赤珠罗网悬马瑙铃，马瑙罗网悬赤珠铃，车璩罗网悬众宝铃。其金树者银叶花实，其银树者金叶花实，其琉璃树水精花叶，水精树琉璃花叶，赤珠树者马瑙花叶，马瑙树赤珠花叶，车璩树众宝花叶。其四园墙复有四门，周匝栏楯。又其墙上皆有楼阁宝台，其墙四面有树木园林、流泉浴池，生种种花，树木繁茂，花果炽盛，众香芬馥，异鸟哀鸣。其塔成已，玉女宝、居士宝、典兵宝、举国士民皆来供养此塔，施诸穷乏，须食与食，须衣与衣，象马宝乘，给众所须，随意所与。转轮圣王威神功德，其事如是。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "Outside of these four continents, there are eight thousand continents surrounding them. There is also a great ocean surrounding the eight thousand continents. Outside the great ocean is a great diamond mountain. Outside the diamond mountain is a second great diamond mountain. Between the two mountains is pitch black, so dark that even the sun, moon, and gods with great supernatural powers cannot illuminate it with their light. There are eight great hells there, and each great hell has sixteen smaller hells. The first great hell is called Saṃjīva, the second is called Kālasūtra, the third is called Saṃghāta, the fourth is called Raurava, the fifth is called Mahāraurava, the sixth is called Tapana, the seventh is called Pratāpana, and the eighth is called Avīci. The Saṃjīva hell has sixteen smaller hells. Each smaller hell is five hundred yojanas long and wide. The first smaller hell is called Black Sand, the second is called Boiling Excrement, the third is called Five Hundred Men, the fourth is called Hunger, the fifth is called Thirst, the sixth is called One Copper Pot, the seventh is called Many Copper Pots, the eighth is called Stone Grindstone, the ninth is called Pus and Blood, the tenth is called Measured Fire, the eleventh is called Ash River, the twelfth is called Iron Ball, the thirteenth is called Axe and Adze, the fourteenth is called Wolves and Jackals, the fifteenth is called Sword Tree, and the sixteenth is called Cold Ice.

佛告比丘：「此四天下有八千天下围遶其外，复有大海水周匝围遶八千天下，复有大金刚山遶大海水。金刚山外复有第二大金刚山，二山中间窈窈冥冥，日月神天有大威力，不能以光照及于彼。彼有八大地狱，其一地狱有十六小地狱。第一大地狱名想，第二名黑绳，第三名堆压，第四名叫唤，第五名大叫唤，第六名烧炙，第七名大烧炙，第八名无间。其想地狱有十六小狱，小狱纵广五百由旬，第一小狱名曰黑沙，二名沸屎，三名五百丁，四名饥，五名渴，六名一铜釜，七名多铜釜，八名石磨，九名脓血，十名量火，十一名灰河，十二名铁丸，十三名𬬱斧，十四名犲狼，十五名剑树，十六名寒氷。

What is the Saṃjīva Hell? The beings there have iron claws growing from their hands, long and sharp. They become angry with each other, harboring thoughts of harm. They scratch each other with their claws, and the flesh falls off. They think they are dead. A cool wind blows, and the skin and flesh grow back. They revive and stand up. They think to themselves, 'I am now alive.' The other beings say, 'I think you are alive.' Because of these thoughts, it is called the Saṃjīva Hell.

「云何名想地狱？其中众生手生铁爪，其爪长利，迭相瞋忿，怀毒害想，以爪相爴] cf.【丽】，应手肉堕，想为已死；冷风来吹，皮肉还生，寻活起立。自想言：『我今已活。』余众生言：『我想汝活。』以是想故，名想地狱。

Furthermore, in the Saṃjīva Hell, the beings there harbor thoughts of harm and disturb each other. They naturally hold swords and knives, sharp and sharp. They slash and stab each other, flay and cut, and their bodies are shattered on the ground. They think they are dead. A cool wind blows, and the skin and flesh grow back. They revive and stand up. They think to themselves, 'I am now alive.' The other beings say, 'I think you are alive.' For this reason, it is called the Saṃjīva Hell.

「复次，想地狱其中众生怀毒害想，共相触娆，手执自然刀剑，刀剑锋利，迭相斫刺，［利－禾＋皮］剥脔割，身碎在地，想谓为死；冷风来吹，皮肉更生，寻活起立。彼自想言：『我今已活。』余众生言：『我想汝活。』以此因缘故，名想地狱。

Furthermore, in the Saṃjīva Hell, the beings there harbor thoughts of harm and disturb each other. They naturally hold swords and knives, sharp and sharp. They slash and stab each other, flay and cut, and think they are dead. A cool wind blows, and the skin and flesh grow back. They revive and stand up. They say to themselves, 'I am alive.' The other beings say, 'I think you are alive.' For this reason, it is called the Saṃjīva Hell.

「复次，想地狱其中众生怀毒害想，迭相触娆，手执刀剑，刀劒锋利，共相斫刺，［利－禾＋皮］剥脔割，想谓为死；冷风来吹，皮肉更生，寻活起立。自言：『我活。』余众生言：『我想汝活。』以此因缘故，名想地狱。

Furthermore, in the Saṃjīva Hell, the beings there harbor thoughts of harm and disturb each other. They naturally hold oil-shadowed knives, sharp and sharp. They slash and stab each other, flay and cut, and think they are dead. A cool wind blows, and the skin and flesh grow back. They revive and stand up. They say to themselves, 'I am alive.' The other beings say, 'I think you are alive.' For this reason, it is called the Saṃjīva Hell.

「复次，想地狱其中众生怀毒害想，迭相触娆，手执油影刀，其刀锋利，更相斫刺，［利－禾＋皮］剥脔割，想谓为死；冷风来吹，皮肉更生，寻活起立。自言：『我活。』余众生言：『我想汝活。』以是因缘，名为想地狱。

Furthermore, in the Saṃjīva Hell, the beings there harbor thoughts of harm and disturb each other. They naturally hold small knives, sharp and sharp. They slash and stab each other, flay and cut, and think they are dead. A cool wind blows, and the skin and flesh grow back. They revive and stand up. They say to themselves, 'I am alive.' The other beings say, 'I think you are alive.' For this reason, it is called the Saṃjīva Hell.

「复次，想地狱其中众生怀毒害想，迭相触娆，手执小刀，其刀锋利，更相斫刺，［利－禾＋皮］剥脔割，想谓为死；冷风来吹，皮肉更生，寻活起立。自言：『我活。』余众生言：『我想汝活。』以是因缘故，名想地狱。

After suffering for a long time in the Saṃjīva Hell, the beings emerge and wander in panic, seeking to save themselves. Driven by past karma, they unknowingly arrive at the Black Sand Hell. At that time, a hot wind suddenly blows, carrying hot black sand that lands on their bodies, turning them completely black, like black clouds. The hot sand burns their skin, flesh, and bones. Black flames arise from the bodies of the sinful beings, circling around them and then returning into their bodies, causing them to suffer various torments, being burned and scorched. Due to the causes and conditions of their sins, they receive these painful retributions. Their sins are not yet exhausted, so they are not allowed to die.

「其中众生久受罪已，出想地狱，慞惶驰走，求自救护，宿罪所牵，不觉忽到黑沙地狱。时，有热风暴起，吹热黑沙，来著其身，举体尽黑，犹如黑云，热沙烧皮，尽肉彻骨，罪人身中有黑焰起，遶身回旋，还入身内，受诸苦恼，烧炙燋烂。以罪因缘，受此苦报，其罪未毕，故使不死。

After suffering for a long time in the Black Sand Hell, the beings emerge and wander in panic, seeking to save themselves. Driven by past karma, they unknowingly arrive at the Boiling Excrement Hell. In that hell, there is boiling excrement and iron balls that naturally fill before them. They are forced to embrace the iron balls, burning their bodies, hands, and even their heads and faces. They are then made to pick them up and put them in their mouths, burning their lips, tongues, and from the throat to the stomach, passing through without being burned or rotten. There are iron beak insects that peck at the skin and flesh, penetrating the bones and marrow. The suffering is bitter and painful, with immeasurable sorrow and distress. Due to their sins not yet being exhausted, they are not allowed to die.

「于此久受苦已，出黑沙地狱，慞惶驰走，求自救护，宿罪所牵，不觉忽到沸屎地狱。其地狱中有沸屎铁丸自然满前，驱迫罪人使抱铁丸，烧其身手，至其头面，无不周遍。复使探撮，举著口中，烧其唇舌，从咽至腹，通彻下过，无不燋烂。有铁［口＊（隹／乃）］虫，唼食皮肉，彻骨达髓，苦毒辛酸，忧恼无量。以罪未毕，犹复不死。

After suffering for a long time in the Boiling Excrement Hell, the beings emerge and wander in panic, seeking to save themselves. They arrive at the Iron Nail Hell. When they arrive, the prison guards throw them down and make them lie on hot iron, stretching their bodies. They nail their hands, feet, and hearts, covering their entire bodies with five hundred nails. The suffering is bitter and painful, with wailing and moaning. Due to their remaining sins not yet being exhausted, they are not allowed to die.

「于沸屎地狱久受苦已，出沸屎地狱，慞惶驰走，求自救护，到铁钉地狱。到已，狱卒扑之令堕，偃热铁上，舒展其身，以钉钉手、钉足、钉心，周遍身体，尽五百钉，苦毒辛酸，号咷呻吟。余罪未毕，犹复不死。

After suffering for a long time in the Iron Nail Hell, the beings emerge and wander in panic, seeking to save themselves. They arrive at the Starvation Hell. The prison guards come and ask, 'Why have you come here?' They reply, 'We are hungry.' The prison guards then grab them and throw them onto hot iron, stretching their bodies. They use iron hooks to pry open their mouths and put hot iron balls in their mouths, burning their lips and tongues, from the throat to the stomach, passing through without being burned or rotten. The suffering is bitter and painful, with wailing and crying. Due to their remaining sins not yet being exhausted, they are not allowed to die.

「久受苦已，出铁钉地狱，慞惶驰走，求自救护，到饥饿地狱。狱卒来问：『汝等来此，欲何所求？』报言：『我饿。』狱卒即捉扑热铁上，舒展其身，以铁钩钩口使开，以热铁丸著其口中，燋其唇舌，从咽至腹，通彻下过，无不燋烂，苦毒辛酸，悲号啼哭。余罪未尽，犹复不死。

After suffering for a long time in the Starvation Hell, the beings emerge and wander in panic, seeking to save themselves. They arrive at the Thirst Hell. The prison guards ask, 'Why have you come here?' They reply, 'We are thirsty.' The prison guards then grab them and throw them onto hot iron, stretching their bodies. They use hot iron hooks to pry open their mouths and pour molten copper into their mouths, burning their lips and tongues, from the throat to the stomach, passing through without being burned or rotten. The suffering is bitter and painful, with wailing and crying. Due to their remaining sins not yet being exhausted, they are not allowed to die.

「久受苦已，出饥地狱，慞惶驰走，求自救护，到渴地狱。狱卒问言：『汝等来此，欲何所求？』报言：『我渴。』狱卒即捉扑热铁上，舒展其身，以热铁钩钩口使开，消铜灌口，烧其唇舌，从咽至腹，通彻下过，无不燋烂，苦毒辛酸，悲号啼哭。余罪未尽，犹复不死。

After suffering for a long time in the Thirst Hell, the beings emerge and wander in panic, seeking to save themselves. Due to their past sins, they unknowingly suddenly arrive at a copper cauldron hell. The prison guards angrily grab the sinners by the feet and throw them into the cauldron, where they boil up and down, from the bottom to the mouth, from the mouth to the bottom, or in the belly of the cauldron, their bodies cooked. It is like boiling beans, boiling up and down, turning inside and out, rotten and destroyed. The sinners in the cauldron, boiling up and down with the water, are also like this, wailing and crying, with myriad sufferings reaching them. Due to their remaining sins not yet being exhausted, they are not allowed to die.

「久受苦已，出渴地狱，慞惶驰走，求自救护，宿罪所牵，不觉忽到一铜鍑地狱。狱卒怒目捉罪人足，倒投鍑中，随汤涌沸，上下回旋，从底至口，从口至底，或在鍑腹，身体烂熟。譬如煮豆，随汤涌沸，上下回转，中外烂坏，罪人在鍑，随汤上下，亦复如是，号咷悲叫，万毒普至。余罪未尽，故复不死。

After suffering for a long time in the single copper cauldron hell, the beings emerge and wander in panic, seeking to save themselves. Due to their past sins, they unknowingly suddenly arrive at the many copper cauldron hell. The many copper cauldron hell is five hundred yojanas long and wide. The prison guards angrily grab the sinners by the feet and throw them into the cauldrons, where they boil up and down, from the bottom to the mouth, from the mouth to the bottom, or in the belly of the cauldrons, their entire bodies rotten. It is like boiling beans, boiling up and down, turning inside and out, all rotten. The sinners in the cauldrons are also like this, boiling up and down, from the mouth to the bottom, from the bottom to the mouth, sometimes only hands and feet appear, sometimes only the waist and abdomen appear, sometimes only the head and face appear. The prison guards use iron hooks to pull them out and place them in other cauldrons, wailing and crying, with bitter and painful suffering. Due to their remaining sins not yet being exhausted, they are not allowed to die.

「久受苦已，出一铜鍑地狱，慞惶驰走，求自救护，宿罪所牵，不觉忽至多铜鍑地狱。多铜鍑地狱纵广五百由旬，狱鬼怒目捉罪人足，倒投鍑中，随汤涌沸，上下回旋，从底至口，从口至底，或在鍑腹，举身烂坏。譬如煑豆，随汤涌沸，上下回转，中外皆烂，罪人在鍑，亦复如是，随汤上下，从口至底，从底至口，或手足现，或腰腹现，或头面现，狱卒以铁钩钩取置余鍑中，号咷悲叫，苦毒辛酸。余罪未毕，故使不死。

After suffering for a long time in the many copper cauldron hell, the beings emerge and wander in panic, seeking to save themselves. Due to their past sins, they unknowingly suddenly arrive at the stone mill hell. The stone mill hell is five hundred yojanas long and wide. The prison guards become very angry, grab the sinners, throw them on hot stones, stretch their hands and feet, and press a large hot stone on their bodies, turning and grinding them, crushing their bones and flesh, with pus and blood flowing out. The suffering is excruciating, and they cry out in pain. Due to their remaining sins not yet being exhausted, they are not allowed to die.

「久受苦已，出多铜鍑地狱，慞惶驰走，求自救护，宿对所牵，不觉忽至石磨地狱。石磨地狱纵广五百由旬，狱卒大怒，捉彼罪人扑热石上，舒展手足，以大热石压其身上，回转揩磨，骨肉糜碎，脓血流出，苦毒切痛，悲号辛酸。余罪未尽，故使不死。

After suffering for a long time in the stone mill hell, the beings emerge and wander in panic, seeking to save themselves. Due to their past sins, they unknowingly suddenly arrive at the pus and blood hell. The pus and blood hell is five hundred yojanas long and wide. In that hell, there is naturally boiling pus and blood that surges out. The sinners run around in it, and the boiling pus and blood scalds their bodies, burning their hands, feet, head, and face. They also take the pus and blood and eat it themselves, scalding their lips, tongue, and throat, passing through the stomach and intestines, all of it rotten and destroyed. The suffering is bitter and painful, with many pains difficult to endure. Due to their remaining sins not yet being exhausted, they are not allowed to die.

「久受苦已，出石磨地狱，慞惶驰走，求自救护，宿对所牵，不觉忽至脓血地狱。脓血地狱纵广五百由旬，其地狱中有自然脓血，热沸涌出，罪人于中东西驰走，脓血沸热，汤其身体，手足头面皆悉烂坏；又取脓血而自食之，汤其唇舌，从咽至腹，通彻下过，无不烂坏，苦毒辛酸，众痛难忍。余罪未毕，故使不死。

After suffering for a long time in the pus and blood hell, the beings emerge and wander in panic, seeking to save themselves. Due to their past sins, they unknowingly suddenly arrive at the measuring fire hell. The measuring fire hell is five hundred yojanas long and wide. In that hell, there is a large mass of fire that naturally appears in front. The flames are blazing. The prison guards angrily chase the sinners, holding iron buckets, making them measure the mass of fire. When they measure the fire, it burns their hands, feet, and entire bodies. The suffering is excruciating, and they groan and cry out. Due to their remaining sins not yet being exhausted, they are not allowed to die.

「久受苦已，乃出脓血地狱，慞惶驰走，求自救护，宿罪所牵，不觉忽至量火地狱。量火地狱纵广五百由旬，其地狱中有大火聚，自然在前。其火焰炽，狱卒瞋怒驰迫罪人，手执铁斗，使量火聚，彼量火时，烧其手足，遍诸身体，苦毒热痛，呻吟号哭。余罪未毕，故使不死。

After suffering for a long time in the measuring fire hell, the beings emerge and wander in panic, seeking to save themselves. Due to their past sins, they unknowingly suddenly arrive at the ash river hell. The ash river hell is five hundred yojanas long and wide, and five hundred yojanas deep. The boiling ash water surges and boils, with evil fumes rising. The waves crash against each other, making a terrifying sound. From the bottom to the top, there are iron thorns eight inches long and wide. On the banks of the river are growing swords. On the banks there are also prison guards and foxes and wolves. On the banks there are also sword tree forests, with branches, leaves, flowers, and fruits all being swords, with blades eight inches long. When the sinners enter the river, they are carried up and down by the waves, rolling over and sinking. The iron thorns pierce them, penetrating inside and outside, with the skin and flesh rotting and pus and blood flowing out. The suffering is manifold, and they cry out in pain. Due to their remaining sins not yet being exhausted, they are not allowed to die.

「久受苦已，乃出量火地狱，慞惶驰走，自求救护，宿对所牵，不觉忽到灰河地狱。灰河地狱纵广五百由旬，深五百由旬，灰汤涌沸，恶气熢［火＊孛］，回波相搏，声响可畏，从底至上，铁刺纵广锋长八寸，其河岸边生长刀剑，其边皆有狱卒狐狼，又其岸上有剑树林，枝叶花实皆是刀剑，锋刃八寸。罪人入河，随波上下，回覆沉没，铁刺刺身，内外通彻，皮肉烂坏，脓血流出，苦痛万端，悲号酸毒。余罪未毕，故使不死。

After suffering for a long time in the ash river hell, the beings emerge and reach the other shore. On the shore, sharp swords cut and pierce their bodies, injuring their hands and feet. At that time, the prison guards ask the sinners, 'You have come here, what do you seek?' The sinners reply, 'We are hungry.' The prison guards then grab the sinners and throw them onto hot iron, stretching their bodies.
