With iron hooks, they pry open their mouths and pour molten copper into them, burning their lips and tongues, passing through their throats and stomachs, completely burning and rotting. There are also wolves with long sharp teeth that come to bite the sinners and eat their flesh raw. Then, the sinners are boiled in the ash river, pierced by sharp thorns, their mouths are poured with molten copper, and they are eaten by wolves. After that, they run up the sword trees. When they climb the sword trees, the sword blades point downward. When they descend the sword trees, the sword blades point upward. Their hands are cut off when they grasp, and their feet are cut off when they step. The sword blades pierce them, penetrating inside and outside, with the skin and flesh falling off, pus and blood flowing out, leaving only white bones connected by tendons and ligaments. At that time, there are iron birds on the sword trees that peck at their skull bones, breaking them, and eat their brains. The suffering is bitter and painful, and they cry out in distress. Due to their remaining sins not yet being exhausted, they are not allowed to die. They then return and enter the ash river hell, where they are carried up and down by the waves, rolling over and sinking. The iron thorns pierce them, penetrating inside and outside, with the skin and flesh rotting and pus and blood flowing out, leaving only white bones floating on the surface. A cold wind blows, and the flesh and skin return. They then immediately stand up, wandering in panic, seeking to save themselves. Due to their past sins, they unknowingly suddenly arrive at the iron ball hell. The iron ball hell is five hundred yojanas long and wide. When the sinners enter, there are hot iron balls that naturally appear in front of them. The prison guards drive them to grasp them, and their hands and feet rot and burn. The suffering is painful and they cry out in distress, with myriad poisons all arriving at once. Due to their remaining sins not yet being exhausted, they are not allowed to die.

「久受苦已，乃出灰河地狱至彼岸上，岸上利剑割刺身体，手足伤坏。尔时，狱卒问罪人言：『汝等来此，欲何所求？』罪人报言：『我等饥饿。』狱卒即捉罪人扑热铁上，舒展身体，以铁钩擗口，洋铜灌之，烧其唇舌，从咽至腹，通彻下过，无不燋烂。复有犲狼，牙齿长利，来啮罪人，生食其肉。于是，罪人为灰河所煮，利刺所刺，洋铜灌口，犲狼所食已，即便［马＊奔］驰走上剑树，上剑树时，剑刃下向，下剑树时，剑刃上向，手攀手绝，足蹬足绝，剑刃刺身，中外通彻，皮肉堕落，脓血流出，遂有白骨筋脉相连。时，剑树上有铁［口＊（隹／乃）］鸟，啄头骨坏，唼食其脑，苦毒辛酸，号咷悲叫。余罪未毕，故使不死。还复来入灰河狱中，随波上下，廻覆沉没，铁刺刺身，内外通彻，皮肉烂坏，脓血流出，唯有白骨浮漂于外，冷风来吹，肌肉还复，寻便起立，慞惶驰走，求自救护，宿对所牵，不觉忽至铁丸地狱。铁丸地狱纵广五百由旬，罪人入已，有热铁丸自然在前，狱鬼驱捉，手足烂坏，举身火然，苦痛悲号，万毒竝至。余罪未毕，故使不死。

After suffering for a long time in the iron ball hell, the beings emerge and wander in panic, seeking to save themselves. Due to their past sins, they unknowingly suddenly arrive at the ax and hatchet hell. The ax and hatchet hell is five hundred yojanas long and wide. When they enter the hell, the prison guards angrily grab the sinners and throw them onto hot iron. With hot iron axes and hatchets, they chop their hands, feet, ears, nose, and body. The suffering is bitter and painful, and they cry out in distress. Due to their remaining sins not yet being exhausted, they are not allowed to die. They then emerge from the ax and hatchet hell and wander in panic, seeking to save themselves. Due to their past sins, they unknowingly suddenly arrive at the saw hell. The saw hell is five hundred yojanas long and wide. When they enter the hell, the prison guards grab the sinners and stretch them on hot iron. With hot iron saws, they saw their bodies, cutting through their skin, flesh, and bones, and the saw dust flies up. The suffering is bitter and painful, and they cry out in distress. Due to their remaining sins not yet being exhausted, they are not allowed to die.

「久受苦已，乃至出铁丸地狱，慞惶驰走，求自救护，宿对所牵，不觉忽至𬬱斧地狱。𬬱斧地狱纵广五百由旬，彼入狱已，狱卒瞋怒捉此罪人扑热铁上，以热铁𬬱斧破其手足、耳鼻、身体，苦毒辛酸，悲号叫唤。余罪未尽，犹复不死。

After suffering for a long time in the ax and hatchet hell, the beings emerge and wander in panic, seeking to save themselves. Due to their past sins, they unknowingly suddenly arrive at the wolf and jackal hell. The wolf and jackal hell is five hundred yojanas long and wide. When they enter the hell, a pack of wolves and jackals come rushing to bite and drag them, tearing at their flesh and dragging them, causing the flesh to fall off and the bones to be injured. Pus and blood flow out, with myriad sufferings and bitter pain, crying out in distress. Due to their remaining sins not yet being exhausted, they are not allowed to die.

「久受罪已，出𬬱斧地狱，慞惶驰走，求自救护，宿罪所牵，不觉忽至犲狼地狱。犲狼地狱纵广五百由旬，罪人入已，有群犲狼竞来［齿＊卢］掣，［齿＊齐］啮拖抴，肉堕伤骨，脓血流出，苦痛万端，悲号酸毒。余罪未毕，故使不死。

After suffering for a long time in the wolf and jackal hell, the beings emerge and wander in panic, seeking to save themselves. Due to their past sins, they unknowingly suddenly arrive at the sword tree hell. The sword tree hell is five hundred yojanas long and wide. When they enter the hell, there is a great violent wind that blows, causing the sword tree leaves to fall onto their bodies. When they touch the hands, the hands are severed. When they touch the feet, the feet are severed. The body and head are all injured. There is an iron crow that stands on their heads and pecks out their two eyes. The suffering is myriad and bitter, crying out in distress. Due to their remaining sins not yet being exhausted, they are not allowed to die.

「久受苦已，乃出犲狼地狱，慞惶驰走，求自救护，宿对所牵，不觉忽至剑树地狱。剑树地狱纵广五百由旬，罪人入彼剑树林中，有大暴风起吹，剑树叶堕其身上，著手手绝，著足足绝，身体头面无不伤坏。有铁［口＊（隹／乃）］鸟立其头上，啄其两目，苦痛万端，悲号酸毒。余罪未毕，故使不死。

After suffering for a long time in the sword tree hell, the beings emerge and wander in panic, seeking to save themselves. Due to their past sins, they unknowingly suddenly arrive at the cold ice hell. The cold ice hell is five hundred yojanas long and wide. When they enter the hell, there is a great cold wind that blows on their bodies, causing their entire bodies to freeze and rot, with the skin and flesh falling off. The suffering is bitter and painful, crying out in distress, and then they die.

「久受苦已，乃出剑树地狱，慞惶驰走，求自救护，宿罪所牵，不觉忽至寒氷地狱。寒氷地狱纵广五百由旬，罪人入已，有大寒风来吹其身，举体冻瘃，皮肉堕落，苦毒辛酸，悲号叫唤，然后命终。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "The Black Rope Great Hell has sixteen small hells surrounding it, each of them being five hundred yojanas long and wide. From the Black Rope Hell to the Cold Ice Hell. Why is it called the Black Rope Hell? The jailers there grab the sinners and throw them on hot iron, stretching their bodies. They use hot iron ropes to straighten them and then use hot iron axes to chop along the rope lines, cutting the sinners into hundreds of thousands of pieces. It is like a craftsman using ropes to straighten wood and then using sharp axes to chop it into hundreds of thousands of pieces. The punishment of the sinners is also like this, with suffering and pain beyond description. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. This is called the Black Rope Hell.

佛告比丘：「黑绳大地狱有十六小地狱，周匝围遶，各各纵广五百由旬，从黑绳地狱至寒氷地狱。何故名为黑绳地狱？其诸狱卒捉彼罪人扑热铁上，舒展其身，以热铁绳絣之使直，以热铁斧逐绳道斫，絣彼罪人，作百千段，犹如工匠以绳絣木，利斧随斫，作百千段。治彼罪人，亦复如是，苦毒辛酸，不可称计。余罪未毕，故使不死。是名为黑绳地狱。

Furthermore, the jailers in the Black Rope Hell grab the sinners and throw them on hot iron, stretching their bodies. They use iron ropes to straighten them and then use saws to saw them, just like a craftsman using ropes to straighten wood and then using saws to saw it. The punishment of the sinners is also like this, with suffering and pain beyond description. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Black Rope Hell.

「复次，黑绳地狱狱卒捉彼罪人扑热铁上，舒展其身，以铁绳絣，以锯锯之，犹如工匠以绳絣木，以锯锯之，治彼罪人，亦复如是，苦痛辛酸，不可称计。余罪未毕，故使不死。是故名为黑绳地狱。

Furthermore, the jailers in the Black Rope Hell grab the sinners and throw them on hot iron, stretching their bodies. They use hot iron ropes to place them on their bodies, burning through the skin, flesh, bones, and marrow. The suffering and pain are beyond description. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Black Rope Hell.

「复次，黑绳地狱捉彼罪人扑热铁上，舒展其身，以热铁绳置其身上，烧皮彻肉，燋骨沸髓，苦毒辛酸，痛不可计。余罪未毕，故使不死。故名黑绳地狱。

Furthermore, the jailers in the Black Rope Hell hang countless hot iron ropes crisscrossing. They drive the sinners to walk between the ropes. A violent evil wind blows, causing the iron ropes to fall on their bodies, burning through the skin, flesh, bones, and marrow. The suffering and pain are beyond description. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Black Rope.

「复次，黑绳地狱狱卒，悬热铁绳交横无数，驱迫罪人，使行绳间，恶风暴起，吹诸铁绳，历落其身，烧皮彻肉，燋骨沸髓，苦毒万端，不可称计。余罪未毕，故使不死。故名黑绳。

Furthermore, the jailers in the Black Rope Hell force the sinners to wear hot iron rope clothes, burning through the skin, flesh, bones, and marrow. The suffering and pain are beyond description. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Black Rope.

「复次，黑绳狱卒以热铁绳衣驱罪人被之，烧皮彻肉，燋骨沸髓，苦毒万端，不可称计。余罪未毕，故使不死。故名黑绳。其彼罪人久受苦已，乃出黑绳地狱，慞惶驰走，求自救护，宿对所牵，不觉忽至黑沙地狱，乃至寒氷地狱，然后命终，亦复如是。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "The Heap-and-Crush Hell has sixteen smaller hells surrounding it, each measuring five hundred yojanas in length and width. Why is it called the Heap-and-Crush Hell? In that hell, there are large stone mountains that face each other. When the sinners enter, the mountains naturally close in, crushing their bodies, grinding their bones and flesh. The mountains then return to their original positions, just like two pieces of wood striking each other and rebounding apart. The punishment of the sinners is also like this, with suffering and pain beyond description. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Heap-and-Crush Hell.

佛告比丘：「堆压大地狱有十六小地狱，周匝围遶，各各纵广五百由旬。何故名为堆压地狱？其地狱中有大石山，两两相对，罪人入中，山自然合，堆压其身，骨肉糜碎，山还故处，犹如以木掷木，弹却还离，治彼罪人，亦复如是，苦毒万端，不可称计。余罪未毕，故使不死。是故名曰堆压地狱。

Furthermore, in the Heap-and-Crush Hell, there is a large iron elephant with a blazing body that roars and comes, trampling on the sinners and rolling over them. Their bodies are crushed and oozing with pus and blood. The suffering and pain are excruciating, with wailing and crying. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Heap-and-Crush.

「复次，堆压地狱有大铁象，举身火然，哮呼而来，蹴蹹罪人，宛转其上，身体糜碎，脓血流出，苦毒辛酸，号咷悲叫。余罪未毕，故使不死。故名堆压。

Furthermore, in the Heap-and-Crush Hell, the prison guards there seize the sinners and place them between two grindstones, grinding them. Their bones and flesh are crushed, and pus and blood flow out. The suffering and pain are beyond description. Their sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Heap-and-Crush.

「复次，堆压地狱其中狱卒。捉诸罪人置于磨石中，以磨磨之，骨肉糜碎，脓血流出，苦毒辛酸，不可称计。其罪未毕，故使不死。故名堆压。

Furthermore, in the Heap-and-Crush Hell, the prison guards seize the sinners and make them lie on a large stone, pressing down with another large stone. Their bones and flesh are crushed, and pus and blood flow out. The suffering and pain are excruciating, with all kinds of pain coming at once. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Heap-and-Crush.

「复次，堆压狱卒捉彼罪人卧大石上，以大石压，骨肉糜碎，脓血流出，苦痛辛酸，万毒竝至。余罪未毕，故使不死。故名堆压。

Furthermore, in the Heap-and-Crush Hell, the prison guards take the sinners and place them in an iron mortar, pounding them from the feet to the head with an iron pestle. Their skin and flesh are crushed, and pus and blood flow out. The suffering and pain are excruciating, with all kinds of pain coming at once. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Heap-and-Crush.

「复次，堆压狱卒取彼罪人卧铁臼中，以铁杵捣从足至头，皮肉糜碎，脓血流出，苦痛辛酸，万毒竝至。余罪未毕，故使不死。故名堆压。其彼罪人久受苦已，乃出堆压地狱，慞惶驰走，求自救护，宿罪所牵，不觉忽至黑沙地狱，乃至寒氷地狱，然后命终，亦复如是。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "The Great Howling Hell has sixteen smaller hells surrounding it, each of which is five hundred yojanas long and wide. Why is it called the Great Howling Hell? The prison guards there grab the sinners and throw them into a large cauldron of boiling hot water, cooking them. The sinners wail and howl, suffering excruciating pain, with all kinds of pain coming at once. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Great Howling Hell.

佛告比丘：「叫唤大地狱有十六小地狱，周匝围遶，各各纵广五百由旬。何故名为叫唤地狱？其诸狱卒捉彼罪人掷大镬中，热汤涌沸，煮彼罪人，号咷叫唤，苦痛辛酸，万毒竝至。余罪未毕，故使不死。故名叫唤地狱。

Furthermore, in the Great Howling Hell, the prison guards take the sinners and throw them into a large iron cauldron, boiling them in hot water. The sinners wail and howl, suffering excruciating pain, with all kinds of pain coming at once. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Great Howling.

「复次，叫唤地狱其诸狱卒，取彼罪人掷大铁瓮中，热汤涌沸而煮罪人，号咷叫唤，苦切辛酸。余罪未毕，故使不死。故名叫唤。

Furthermore, in the Great Howling Hell, the prison guards take the sinners and place them in a large iron pot, boiling them in hot water. The sinners wail and howl, suffering excruciating pain, with all kinds of pain coming at once. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Great Howling.

「复次，叫唤地狱其诸狱卒，取彼罪人置大铁鍑中，热汤涌沸，煮彼罪人，号咷叫唤，苦痛辛酸。余罪未毕，故使不死。故名叫唤。

Furthermore, in the Great Howling Hell, the prison guards take the sinners and throw them into a small pot, boiling them in hot water. The sinners wail and howl, suffering excruciating pain, with all kinds of pain coming at once. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Great Howling.

「复次，叫唤地狱其诸狱卒，取彼罪人掷小鍑中，热汤涌沸，煮彼罪人，号咷叫唤，苦痛辛酸。余罪未毕，故使不死。故名叫唤地狱。

Furthermore, in the Great Howling Hell, the prison guards take the sinners and throw them onto a large griddle, frying them back and forth, causing them to wail and howl, suffering excruciating pain, with all kinds of pain coming at once. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Great Howling.

「复次，叫唤地狱其诸狱卒，取彼罪人掷大鏊上，反复煎熬，号咷叫唤，苦痛辛酸。余罪未毕，故使不死。故名叫唤。久受苦已，乃出叫唤地狱，慞惶驰走，求自救护，宿对所牵，不觉忽至黑沙地狱，乃至寒氷地狱，尔乃至终。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: 'In the Great Howling Hell, there are sixteen smaller hells surrounding it. Why is it called the Great Howling Hell? The prison guards take the sinners and place them in a large iron cauldron, boiling them in hot water. The sinners wail and howl, suffering excruciating pain, with all kinds of pain coming at once. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Great Howling.

佛告比丘：「大叫唤地狱有十六小狱，周匝围遶。何故名为大叫唤地狱？其诸狱卒取彼罪人著大铁釜中，热汤涌沸而煮罪人，号咷叫唤、大叫唤，苦痛辛酸，万毒并至。余罪未毕，故使不死。故名大叫唤地狱。

Furthermore, in the Great Howling Hell, the prison guards take the sinners and throw them into a large iron cauldron, boiling them in hot water. The sinners wail and howl, suffering excruciating pain, with all kinds of pain coming at once. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Great Howling.

「复次，大叫唤地狱其诸狱卒，取彼罪人掷大铁瓮中，热汤涌沸而煮罪人，号咷叫唤、大叫唤，苦切辛酸，万毒并至。余罪未毕，故使不死。故名大叫唤地狱。

Furthermore, in the Great Howling Hell, the prison guards take the sinners and place them in an iron cauldron, boiling them in hot water. The sinners wail and howl, suffering excruciating pain, with all kinds of pain coming at once. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Great Howling.

「复次，大叫唤狱卒取彼罪人置铁镬中，热汤涌沸，煮彼罪人，号咷叫唤，苦毒辛酸，万毒并至。余罪未毕，故使不死。故名大叫唤地狱。

Furthermore, in the Great Howling Hell, the prison guards take the sinners and throw them into a small cauldron, boiling them in hot water. The sinners wail and howl, suffering excruciating pain, with all kinds of pain coming at once. Therefore, it is called the Great Howling.

「复次，大叫唤地狱其诸狱卒，取彼罪人掷小鍑中，热汤涌沸，煮彼罪人，号咷叫唤、大叫唤，苦痛辛酸，万毒并至，故名大叫唤。

Furthermore, in the Great Howling Hell, the prison guards take the sinners and throw them onto a large griddle, frying them back and forth. The sinners wail and howl, suffering excruciating pain, with all kinds of pain coming at once. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Great Howling.

「复次，大叫唤地狱其诸狱卒，取彼罪人掷大鏊上，反复煎熬，号咷叫唤、大叫唤，苦痛辛酸，万毒并至。余罪未毕，故使不死。故名大叫唤。久受苦已，乃出大叫唤地狱，慞惶驰走，求自救护，宿对所牵，不觉忽至黑沙地狱，乃至寒氷地狱，尔乃命终。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "The Burning Earth Hell has sixteen smaller hells surrounding it. Why is it called the Burning Earth Hell? At that time, the prison guards take the sinners and place them in an iron city, which is burning, both inside and outside, burning the sinners, scorching their skin and flesh, suffering excruciating pain, with all kinds of pain coming at once. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Burning Earth Hell.

佛告比丘：「烧炙大地狱有十六小狱，周匝围遶，何故名为烧炙大地狱？尔时，狱卒将诸罪人置铁城中，其城火然，内外俱赤，烧炙罪人，皮肉燋烂，苦痛辛酸，万毒并至。余罪未毕，故使不死。是故名为烧炙地狱。

Furthermore, in the Burning Hell, the prison guards take the sinners and place them in an iron room, which is burning, both inside and outside, burning the sinners, scorching their skin and flesh, suffering excruciating pain, with all kinds of pain coming at once. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Burning Hell.

「复次，烧炙地狱其诸狱卒，将彼罪人入铁室内，其室火然，内外俱赤，烧炙罪人，皮肉燋烂，苦痛辛酸，万毒并至。余罪未毕，故使不死。是故名为烧炙地狱。

Furthermore, in the Burning Hell, the prison guards take the sinners and place them on an iron tower, which is burning, both inside and outside, burning the sinners, scorching their skin and flesh, suffering excruciating pain, with all kinds of pain coming at once. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Burning Hell.

「复次，烧炙地狱其诸狱卒，取彼罪人著铁楼上，其楼火然，内外俱赤，烧炙罪人，皮肉燋烂，苦痛辛酸，万毒并至。余罪未毕，故使不死。是故名为烧炙地狱。

Furthermore, in the Burning Hell, the prison guards take the sinners and throw them into a large iron pot, which is burning, both inside and outside, burning the sinners, scorching their skin and flesh, suffering excruciating pain, with all kinds of pain coming at once. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Burning Hell.

「复次，烧炙地狱其诸狱卒，取彼罪人掷著大铁陶中，其陶火燃，内外俱赤，烧炙罪人，皮肉燋烂，苦痛辛酸，万毒并至。余罪未毕，故使不死。是故名为烧炙地狱。

Furthermore, in the Burning Hell, the prison guards take the sinners and throw them onto a large griddle, which is burning, both inside and outside, burning the sinners, scorching their skin and flesh, suffering excruciating pain, with all kinds of pain coming at once. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. After suffering for a long time, they emerge from the Burning Hell, wandering in panic, seeking to save themselves, but driven by their past sins, they unknowingly arrive at the Black Sand Hell, and so on, up to the Cold Ice Hell, where they finally die, also in the same way.

「复次，烧炙地狱其诸狱卒，取彼罪人掷大鏊上，其鏊火然，中外俱赤，烧炙罪人，皮肉燋烂，苦痛辛酸，万毒并至。余罪未毕，故使不死。久受苦已，乃出烧炙地狱，慞惶驰走，求自救护，宿罪所牵，不觉忽至黑沙地狱，乃至寒氷地狱，然后命终，亦复如是。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "The Great Burning Hell has sixteen smaller hells surrounding it, each of which is five hundred yojanas long and wide. What is meant by the Great Burning Hell? The prison guards take the sinners and place them in an iron city, which is burning, both inside and outside, burning the sinners, greatly burning them, scorching their skin and flesh, suffering excruciating pain, with all kinds of pain coming at once. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Great Burning Hell.

佛告比丘：「大烧炙地狱有十六小狱，周匝围遶，各各纵广五百由旬。云何名大烧炙地狱？其诸狱卒将诸罪人置铁城中，其城火然，内外俱赤，烧炙罪人，重大烧炙，皮肉燋烂，苦痛辛酸，万毒并至。余罪未毕，故使不死。是故名为大烧炙地狱。

Furthermore, in the Great Burning Hell, the prison guards take the sinners and place them in an iron chamber, which is burning, both inside and outside, burning the sinners, greatly burning them, scorching their skin and flesh, suffering excruciating pain, with all kinds of pain coming at once. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Great Burning Hell.

「复次，大烧炙地狱其诸狱卒，将诸罪人入铁室中，其室火燃，内外俱赤，烧炙罪人，重大烧炙，皮肉燋烂，苦痛辛酸，万毒并至。余罪未毕，故使不死。是故名为大烧炙地狱。

Furthermore, in the Great Burning Hell, the prison guards take the sinners and place them on an iron tower, which is burning, both inside and outside, burning the sinners, greatly burning them, scorching their skin and flesh, suffering excruciating pain, with all kinds of pain coming at once. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Great Burning Hell.

「复次，大烧炙地狱其诸狱卒，取彼罪人著铁楼上，其楼火燃，内外俱赤，烧炙罪人，重大烧炙，皮肉燋烂，苦痛辛酸，万毒并至。余罪未毕，故使不死。是故名曰大烧炙地狱。

Furthermore, in the Great Burning Hell, the prison guards take the sinners and place them in a large iron pot, which is burning, both inside and outside, burning the sinners, greatly burning them, suffering excruciating pain, with all kinds of pain coming at once. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Great Burning Hell.

「复次，大烧炙地狱其诸狱卒，取彼罪人著大铁陶中，其陶火然，内外俱赤，烧炙罪人，重大烧炙，苦痛辛酸，万毒并至。余罪未毕，故使不死。是故名为大烧炙地狱。

Furthermore, in the Great Burning Hell, there is a naturally occurring large fire pit with blazing flames. On both sides of the pit are large volcanic mountains. The prison guards take the sinners, impale them on iron forks, and stand them in the fire, burning their bodies, greatly burning them, scorching their skin and flesh, suffering excruciating pain, with all kinds of pain coming at once. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. After suffering for a long time, they then emerge from the Great Burning Hell, wandering in panic, seeking self-protection, but driven by past karma, they unknowingly arrive at the Black Sand Hell, and so on, up to the Cold Ice Hell, where they finally die, also in the same way.

「复次，大烧炙地狱中自然有大火坑，火焰炽盛，其坑两岸有大火山，其诸狱卒捉彼罪人贯铁叉上，竖著火中，烧炙其身，重大烧炙，皮肉燋烂，苦痛辛酸，万毒并至。余罪未毕，故使不死。久受苦已，然后乃出大烧炙地狱，慞惶驰走，求自救护，宿对所牵，不觉忽至黑沙地狱，乃至寒氷地狱，尔乃命终，亦复如是。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "The Avīci Hell has sixteen smaller hells surrounding it, each of which is five hundred yojanas long and wide. What is meant by the Avīci Hell? The prison guards there grab the sinners and flay their skin from their feet to the top of their heads. They then wrap the sinners' bodies in their own skin and put them on a burning wheel. They drive the burning cart over the hot iron ground, going back and forth, crushing their bodies into pieces. Their skin and flesh fall off, and they suffer excruciating pain, with all kinds of pain coming at once. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Avīci Hell.

佛告比丘：「无间大地狱有十六小狱，周匝围遶，各各纵广五百由旬。云何名无间地狱？其诸狱卒捉彼罪人剥其皮，从足至顶，即以其皮缠罪人身，著火车轮，疾驾火车，辗热铁地，周行往返，身体碎烂，皮肉堕落，苦痛辛酸，万毒并至。余罪未毕，故使不死。是故名为无间地狱。

Furthermore, in the Avīci Hell there is a large iron city. On all four sides of the city, a great fire arises. The eastern flames reach the west, the western flames reach the east, the southern flames reach the north, the northern flames reach the south, the upper flames reach the lower, and the lower flames reach the upper. The flames blaze and swirl, leaving no empty space. The sinners run back and forth in the middle, burning their bodies, scorching their skin and flesh. They suffer excruciating pain, with all kinds of pain coming at once. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Avīci Hell.

「复次，无间大地狱有大铁城，其城四面有大火起，东焰至西，西焰至东，南焰至北，北焰至南，上焰至下，下焰至上，焰炽回遑，无间空处，罪人在中，东西驰走，烧炙其身，皮肉燋烂，苦痛辛酸，万毒并至。余罪未毕，故使不死。是故名为无间地狱。

Furthermore, in the Avīci Hell there is an iron city. A fire arises and blazes. The sinners are inside, and the flames burn their bodies, scorching their skin and flesh. They suffer excruciating pain, with all kinds of pain coming at once. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Avīci Hell.

「复次，无间大地狱中有铁城，火起洞然，罪人在中，火焰燎身，皮肉燋烂，苦痛辛酸，万毒并至。余罪未毕，故使不死。是故名为无间地狱。

Furthermore, in the Avīci Hell, the sinners are inside for a long time before the door opens. When they rush towards it, flames come out from all their limbs and joints. It is like a strong man holding a large torch against the wind and running. The flames are blazing. When the sinners run, it is also like this. When they run to the door, the door naturally closes. The sinners jump and crawl on the hot iron ground, burning their bodies, scorching their skin and flesh. They suffer excruciating pain, with all kinds of pain coming at once. Their remaining sins have not yet been exhausted, so they are not allowed to die. Therefore, it is called the Avīci Hell.

「复次，大无间地狱罪人在中，久乃门开，其诸罪人［马＊奔］走往趣。彼当走时，身诸肢节，皆火焰出，犹如力士执大草炬逆风而走，其焰炽然。罪人走时，亦复如是。走欲至门，门自然闭，罪人［跳－兆＋匍］蹈，伏热铁地，烧炙其身，皮肉燋烂，苦痛辛酸，万毒并至。余罪未毕，故使不死。是故名为无间地狱。

Furthermore, in the Avīci Hell, the sinners only see evil sights when they raise their eyes, only hear evil sounds when they hear, only smell evil odors when they smell, only touch painful sensations when they touch, and only think of evil dharmas when they think. Moreover, for the sinners, there is no time without suffering even for the duration of a finger snap. Therefore, it is called the Avīci Hell. After the beings there have suffered for a long time, they emerge from Avīci and flee in panic, seeking to save themselves. Pulled by their past karma, they unknowingly suddenly arrive at the Black Sand Hell, and so on, up to the Cold Ice Hell, where they then die. It is also like this.

「复次，无间地狱其中罪人，举目所见，但见恶色，耳有所闻，但闻恶声，鼻有所闻，但闻臭恶，身有所触，但触苦痛，意有所念，但念恶法。又其罪人弹指之顷，无不苦时，故名无间地狱。其中众生久受苦已，从无间出，慞惶驰走，求自救护，宿对所牵，不觉忽到黑沙地狱，乃至寒氷地狱，尔乃命终，亦复如是。」

At that time, the World-Honored One spoke a verse, saying:

尔时，世尊即说颂曰：

The body commits unwholesome actions, the mouth and mind are also
unwholesome. One falls into the Hell of Thought, fearful and hair-raising
Evil intentions towards parents, the Buddha, and the Shravakas, one falls
into the Black Rope Hell, with suffering beyond measure. Only creating
the three unwholesome actions, not cultivating the three wholesome practices, one
falls into the Hell of Crushing, with suffering beyond measure. With
anger and malice, killing and blood on the hands, creating various
evil actions, one falls into the Hell of Screaming. Always practicing
various wrong views, covered by the net of desire, creating these
base and lowly actions, one falls into the Great Hell of
Screaming. Always practicing burning and scorching, burning and scorching sentient beings
one falls into the Hell of Burning, suffering burning for a
long time. Abandoning wholesome fruit actions, the pure path of wholesome
fruit, creating various evil actions, one falls into the Great Hell
of Burning. For extremely heavy evil actions, definitely giving rise to
evil destinies, one falls into the Hell of No Intermission, with
suffering beyond measure. The Hell of Thought and the Black Rope
Hell, the two Crushing Hells and the two Screaming Hells, the
Burning and the Great Burning, the Hell of No Intermission as
the eighth. These eight great hells, blazing with fiery light, are
due to past evil retribution. The minor hells have sixteen.

「身为不善业，　　口意亦不善，斯堕想地狱，　　怖惧衣毛竖。恶意向父母，　　佛及诸声闻，则堕黑绳狱，　　苦痛不可称。但造三恶业，　　不修三善行，堕堆压地狱，　　苦痛不可称。瞋恚怀毒害，　　杀生血污手，造诸杂恶行，　　堕叫唤地狱。常习众邪见，　　为爱网所覆，造此卑陋行，　　堕大叫唤狱。常为烧炙行，　　烧炙诸众生，堕烧炙地狱，　　长夜受烧炙。舍于善果业，　　善果清净道，为众弊恶行，　　堕大烧炙狱。为极重罪行，　　必生恶趣业，堕无间地狱，　　受罪不可称。想及黑绳狱，　　堆压二叫唤，烧炙大烧炙，　　无间为第八。此八大地狱，　　洞然火光色，斯由宿恶殃，　　小狱有十六。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "Between those two great vajra mountains, a great wind arises, called 'increasing'. If this wind were to come to this four-continent world and the eight thousand worlds, it would blow this great earth and all the famous mountains, Mount Sumeru, ten miles or even a hundred miles away from the ground, and scatter them in the air, all pulverized. It would be like a strong man scattering light chaff in the air with his hand. If that great wind were to come, it would blow this world in the same way. It is because there are two great vajra mountains blocking this wind that it does not come. Bhikṣus! You should know that these vajra mountains are of great benefit, and it is also due to the karmic retribution of sentient beings.

佛告比丘：「彼二大金刚山间有大风起，名为增佉，若使此风来至此四天下及八千天下者，吹此大地及诸名山须弥山王去地十里，或至百里，飞飏空中，皆悉糜碎。譬如壮士，手把轻糠散于空中。彼大风力，若使来者，吹此天下，亦复如是。由有二大金刚山遮止此风，故使不来。比丘！当知此金刚山多所饶益，亦是众生行报所致。

Moreover, the wind between those two mountains is blazing and fierce. If that wind were to come to this four-continent world, the sentient beings, mountains, rivers, oceans, grasses, trees, and forests would all be scorched and withered. It would be like cutting fresh grass in the hot summer and placing it in the sun, which would immediately wither. That wind would be like this. If it were to come to this world, the heat would burn and scorch it in the same way. It is because these two vajra mountains block this wind that it does not come. Bhikṣus! You should know that these vajra mountains are of great benefit, and it is also due to the karmic retribution of sentient beings.

「又彼二山间风，焰炽猛热，若使彼风来至此四天下者，其中众生、山河、江海、草木、丛林皆当燋枯。犹如盛夏断生濡草，置于日中，寻时萎枯。彼风如是，若使来至此世界，热气烧炙，亦复如是。由此二金刚山遮止此风，故使不来。比丘！当知此金刚山多所饶益，亦是众生行报所致。

Moreover, the wind between those two mountains is foul-smelling, impure, and extremely putrid. If it were to come to this four-continent world, it would make the sentient beings here all lose their eyesight. It is because these two great vajra mountains block this wind that it does not come. Bhikṣus! You should know that these vajra mountains are of great benefit, and it is also due to the karmic retribution of sentient beings.

「又彼二山间风，臭处不净，腥秽酷烈，若使来至此天下者，熏此众生皆当失目。由此二大金刚山遮止此风，故使不来。比丘！当知此金刚山多所饶益，亦是众生行报所致。

"Moreover, between those two mountains there are ten hells: the first is called Thick Clouds, the second is called Cloudless, the third is called Ha Ha, the fourth is called Alas, the fifth is called Sheep's Cry, the sixth is called Sukhandi, the seventh is called Utpala, the eighth is called Kumuda, the ninth is called Pundarika, and the tenth is called Paduma. What is the Thick Clouds Hell? The bodies of the sinners born in that hell are like thick clouds, hence the name Thick Clouds. What is meant by Cloudless? The bodies of the sentient beings suffering in that hell are like pieces of meat, hence the name Cloudless. What is meant by Ha Ha? The sentient beings suffering in that hell cry out in pain, hence the name Ha Ha. What is meant by Alas? The sentient beings suffering in that hell cry out in pain, having nowhere to turn, hence the name Alas. What is meant by Sheep's Cry? The sentient beings suffering in that hell cry out in pain, unable to turn their tongues, just like sheep, hence the name Sheep's Cry. What is meant by Sukhandi? The entire hell is black, like the color of Sukhandi flowers, hence the name Sukhandi. What is meant by Utpala? The entire hell is blue, like Utpala flowers, hence the name Utpala. What is meant by Kumuda? The entire hell is red, like the color of Kumuda flowers, hence the name Kumuda. What is meant by Pundarika? The entire hell is white, like the color of Pundarika flowers, hence the name Pundarika. What is meant by Paduma? The entire hell is red, like the color of Paduma flowers, hence the name Paduma."

「又彼二山中间复有十地狱：一名厚云，二名无云，三名呵呵，四名奈何，五名羊鸣，六名须干提，七名优钵罗，八名拘物头，九名分陀利，十名钵头摩。云何厚云地狱？其狱罪人自然生身，譬如厚云，故名厚云。云何名曰无云？其彼狱中受罪众生，自然生身，犹如段肉，故名无云。云何名呵呵？其地狱中受罪众生，苦痛切身，皆称呵呵，故名呵呵。云何名奈何？其地狱中受罪众生，苦痛酸切，无所归依，皆称奈何，故名奈何。云何名羊鸣？其地狱中受罪众生，苦痛切身，欲举声语，舌不能转，直如羊鸣，故名羊鸣。云何名须干提？其地狱中举狱皆黑，如须干提华色，故名须干提。云何名优钵罗？其地狱中举狱皆青，如优钵罗华，故名优钵罗。云何名俱物头？其地狱中举狱皆红，如俱物头华色，故名俱物头。云何名分陀利？其地狱中举狱皆白，如分陀利华色，故名分陀利。云何名钵头摩？其地狱中举狱皆赤，如钵头摩华色，故名钵头摩。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "Suppose there is a basket holding sixty-four bushels of sesame seeds, and a person takes one sesame seed every hundred years. In this way, until it is emptied, the suffering in the Thick Clouds Hell is not yet over. The lifespan in twenty Thick Clouds Hells is equal to the lifespan in one Cloudless Hell. The lifespan in twenty Cloudless Hells is equal to the lifespan in one Ha Ha Hell. The lifespan in twenty Ha Ha Hells is equal to the lifespan in one Alas Hell. The lifespan in twenty Alas Hells is equal to the lifespan in one Sheep's Cry Hell. The lifespan in twenty Sheep's Cry Hells is equal to the lifespan in one Sukhandi Hell. The lifespan in twenty Sukhandi Hells is equal to the lifespan in one Utpala Hell. The lifespan in twenty Utpala Hells is equal to the lifespan in one Kumuda Hell. The lifespan in twenty Kumuda Hells is equal to the lifespan in one Pundarika Hell. The lifespan in twenty Pundarika Hells is equal to the lifespan in one Paduma Hell. The lifespan in twenty Paduma Hells is called one intermediate kalpa. Twenty intermediate kalpas are called one great kalpa. The flames in the Paduma Hell are extremely hot and blazing. The sinners are a hundred yojanas away from the fire, and they are already burned. Sixty yojanas away, their ears are already deaf and they can no longer hear. Fifty yojanas away, their eyes are already blind and they can no longer see. The bhikṣu Gautama Pari has already harbored evil intentions and slandered Śāriputra and Maudgalyāyana. When his body perishes and his life ends, he will fall into this Paduma Hell.

佛告比丘：「喻如有篅受六十四斛，满中胡麻，有人百岁持一麻去，如是至尽，厚云地狱受罪未竟，如二十厚云地狱寿与一无云地狱寿等，如二十无云地狱寿与一呵呵地狱寿等，如二十呵呵地狱寿与一奈何地狱寿等，如二十奈何地狱寿与一羊鸣地狱寿等，如二十羊鸣地狱寿与一须干提地狱寿等，如二十须干提地狱寿与一优钵罗地狱寿等，如二十优钵罗地狱寿与一拘物头地狱寿等，如二十拘物头地狱寿与一分陀利地狱寿等，如二十分陀利地狱寿与一钵头摩地狱寿等，如二十钵头摩地狱寿，名一中劫，如二十中劫，名一大劫。钵头摩地狱中火焰热炽盛，罪人去火一百由旬，火已烧炙；去六十由旬，两耳已聋，无所闻知；去五十由旬，两目已盲，无所复见。瞿波梨比丘已怀恶心，谤舍利弗、目犍连，身坏命终，堕此钵头摩地狱中。

At that time, the Brahma King spoke this verse:

「尔时，梵王说此偈言：

The man's life is like an axe in his mouth, which cuts
his own body because of his evil speech. He should praise those
who deserve praise, but he slanders them; he should slander those who
deserve slander, but he praises them. The evil karma of his mouth
causes his body to suffer. Although earning wealth through skills is a
minor fault, slandering the sages is a grave offense. The lifespan in
a hundred thousand Cloudless Hells is equal to forty-one Cloud Hells. Slandering
the sages brings this retribution, caused by the evil of mind and mouth.

「『夫士之生，　　斧在口中，所以斩身，　　由其恶口。应毁者誉，　　应誉者毁，口为恶业，　　身受其罪。技术取财，　　其过薄少，毁谤贤圣，　　其罪甚重。百千无云寿，　　四十一云寿，谤圣受斯殃，　　由心口为恶。』」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "The Brahma Heaven spoke these verses, which are true words approved by the Buddha. Why is this so? I, the Tathāgata, Arhat, Perfectly Enlightened One, also speak of this meaning.

佛告比丘：「彼梵天说如是偈，为真正言，佛所印可。所以者何？我今如来、至真、等正觉亦说此义。

The man's life is like an axe in his mouth, which cuts
his own body because of his evil speech. He should praise those
who deserve praise, but he slanders them; he should slander those who
deserve slander, but he praises them. The evil karma of his mouth
causes his body to suffer. Although earning wealth through skills is a
minor fault, slandering the sages is a grave offense. The lifespan in
a hundred thousand Cloudless Hells is equal to forty-one Cloud Hells. Slandering
the sages brings this retribution, caused by the evil of mind and mouth.

「夫士之生，　　斧在口中，所以斩身，　　由其恶言。应毁者誉，　　应誉者毁，口为恶业，　　身受其罪。技术取财，　　其过薄少，毁谤贤圣，　　其罪甚重。百千无云寿，　　四十一云寿，谤圣受斯殃，　　由心口为恶。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "Inside the great diamond mountain south of Jambudvīpa is the palace of King Yama. The place he governs is six thousand yojanas long and wide. The city has seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees, and so on, with countless birds singing harmoniously, also like this. However, King Yama has three times a day when a large copper cauldron appears before him. If the cauldron appears inside the palace, the king, seeing it, is afraid and leaves the palace. If the cauldron appears outside the palace, the king, seeing it, is afraid and enters the palace. A great jailer seizes King Yama and lays him on a hot iron bed, opens his mouth with an iron hook, and pours molten copper into it, burning his lips and tongue, passing through his throat and stomach, and burning everything below. After suffering the punishment, he again enjoys himself with the palace ladies. The ministers who share his merit also experience this.

佛告比丘：「阎浮提南大金刚山内，有阎罗王宫，王所治处纵广六千由旬，其城七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，乃至无数众鸟相和悲鸣，亦复如是。然彼阎罗王昼夜三时，有大铜镬自然在前。若镬出宫内，王见畏怖，舍出宫外。若镬出宫外，王见畏怖，舍入宫内。有大狱卒，捉阎罗王卧热铁上，以铁钩擗口使开，洋铜灌之，烧其唇舌，从咽至腹，通彻下过，无不燋烂。受罪讫已，复与诸婇女共相娱乐。彼诸大臣同受福者，亦复如是。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "There are three messengers. What are the three? First, old age; second, sickness; third, death. If sentient beings commit evil deeds with their bodies, speak evil words, and think evil thoughts, when their bodies perish and their lives end, they fall into hell. The jailers take these sinners to King Yama. Upon arrival, they say, 'This is the one summoned by the messengers. May the great king kindly question him.' The king asks the sinner, 'Did you not see the first messenger?' The sinner replies, 'I did not see.' The king further says, 'When you were among humans, did you ever see an old person with white hair, falling teeth, blurred vision, loose skin, and a hunched back, leaning on a cane, groaning as they walk, with a trembling body and waning strength? Did you see such a person?' The sinner says, 'I saw.' The king further says, 'Why did you not think to yourself, "I am also like this"?' The person replies, 'At that time, I was heedless and did not realize it.' The king further says, 'It is because you were heedless that you could not cultivate your body, speech, and mind, change evil and follow goodness. Now I will let you know the suffering of heedlessness.' The king further says, 'The suffering you now experience is not the fault of your parents, siblings, the Heavenly Emperor, ancestors, friends, servants, or śramaṇas and brāhmaṇas. It is your own evil that you now experience.

佛告比丘：「有三使者，云何为三？一者老，二者病，三者死。有众生身行恶，口言恶，心念恶，身坏命终，堕地狱中。狱卒将此罪人诣阎罗王所，到已，白言：『此是天使所召也，唯愿大王善问其辞。』王问罪人言：『汝不见初使耶？』罪人报言：『我不见也。』王复告曰：『汝在人中时，颇见老人头白齿落，目视蒙蒙，皮缓肌［月＊曷］，偻脊柱杖，呻吟而行，身体战掉，气力衰微。见此人不？』罪人言：『见。』王复告曰：『汝何不自念：「我亦如是。」』彼人报言：『我时放逸，不自觉知。』王复语言：『汝自放逸，不能修身、口、意，改恶从善，今当令汝知放逸苦。』王又告言：『今汝受罪，非父母过，非兄弟过，亦非天帝，亦非先祖，亦非知识、僮仆、使人，亦非沙门、婆罗门过。汝自有恶，汝今自受。』

"At that time, King Yama, having questioned the sinner with the first messenger, further questioned the sinner with the second messenger, saying, 'How is it that you did not see the second messenger?' The sinner replied, 'I did not see.' The king further asked, 'When you were a human, did you ever see a sick person, gravely ill, lying on a bed, in a place of filth and urine, unable to get up, needing others to feed them, with aching limbs, tears streaming, groaning, unable to speak? Did you see this?' The sinner replied, 'I saw.' The king further said, 'Why did you not think to yourself, "Such sickness and suffering, I will also be like this"?" The sinner replied, 'At that time, I was heedless and did not realize it.' The king further said, 'It is because you were heedless that you could not cultivate your body, speech, and mind, change evil and follow goodness. Now I will let you know the suffering of heedlessness.' The king further said, 'The suffering you now experience is not the fault of your parents, siblings, the Heavenly Emperor, ancestors, friends, servants, or śramaṇas and brāhmaṇas. It is your own evil that you now experience.

「时，阎罗王以第一天使问罪人已，复以第二天使问罪人言：『云何汝不见第二天使耶？』对曰：『不见。』王又问言：『汝本为人时，颇见人疾病困笃，卧著床褥，屎尿臭处，身卧其上，不能起居，饮食须人，百节酸疼，流泪呻吟，不能言语。汝见是不？』答曰：『见。』王又报言：『汝何不自念：「如此病苦，我亦当尔？」』罪人报言：『我时放逸，不自觉知。』王又语言：『汝自放逸，不能修身、口、意，改恶从善，今当令汝知放逸苦。』王又告言：『今汝受罪，非父母过，非兄弟过，亦非天帝过，亦非先祖，亦非知识、僮仆、使人，亦非沙门、婆罗门过。汝自为恶，汝今自受。』

"At that time, King Yama, having questioned the sinner with the second messenger, further questioned the sinner with the third messenger, saying, 'How is it that you did not see the third messenger?' The sinner replied, 'I did not see.' The king further asked, 'When you were a human, did you ever see a dead person, with their body destroyed and life ended, with all faculties forever extinguished, their body straight like a withered tree, abandoned in a charnel ground, eaten by birds and beasts, or wrapped in a coffin, or burned by fire. Did you see this?' The sinner replied, 'Indeed I saw.' The king further said, 'Why did you not think to yourself, "I will also die, no different from them"?" The sinner replied, 'At that time, I was heedless and did not realize it.' The king further said, 'It is because you were heedless that you could not cultivate your body, speech, and mind, change evil and follow goodness. Now I will let you know the suffering of heedlessness.' The king further said, 'The suffering you now experience is not the fault of your parents, siblings, the Heavenly Emperor, ancestors, friends, servants, or śramaṇas and brāhmaṇas. It is your own evil that you now experience.

「时，阎罗王以第二天使问罪人已，复以第三天使问罪人言：『云何汝不见第三天使耶？』答言：『不见。』王又问言：『汝本为人时，颇见人死，身坏命终，诸根永灭，身体挺直，犹如枯木，捐弃冢间，鸟兽所食，或衣棺椁，或以火烧。汝见是不？』罪人报曰：『实见。』王又报言：『汝何不自念：「我亦当死，与彼无异。」』罪人报言：『我时放逸，不自觉知。』王复语言：『汝自放逸，不能修身、口、意，改恶从善，今当令汝知放逸苦。』王又告言：『汝今受罪，非父母过，非兄弟过，亦非天帝，亦非先祖，亦非知识、僮仆、使人，亦非沙门、婆罗门过。汝自为恶，汝今自受。』时，阎罗王以三天使具诘问已，即付狱卒。时，彼狱卒即将罪人诣大地狱，其大地狱纵广百由旬，下深百由旬。」

At that time, the World-Honored One spoke a verse, saying:

尔时，世尊即说偈言：

There are four gates in the four directions, the streets are all
corresponding, with iron walls as the prison walls, covered above with an
iron net. The ground below is made of iron, with natural flames
rising up. It is a hundred yojanas long and wide, firmly established
and immovable. Black flames rise up, blazing fiercely, difficult to look at
There are sixteen smaller hells, with raging fires due to evil deeds.

「四方有四门，　　巷陌皆相当，以铁为狱墙，　　上覆铁罗网。以铁为下地，　　自然火焰出，纵广百由旬，　　安住不倾动。黑焰熢［火＊孛］起，　　赫烈难可覩，小狱有十六，　　火炽由行恶。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "At that time, King Yama had this thought: 'The sentient beings in the world are deluded and ignorant. Those who do evil with their bodies, speech, and minds, after their lives end, few do not experience this suffering. If the sentient beings in the world can change their evil ways and cultivate good conduct with their bodies, speech, and minds, after their lives end they will experience happiness like those heavenly beings. If I am reborn as a human after my life ends, if I encounter the Tathāgata, I will shave my head and beard, wear the three Dharma robes, leave home to cultivate the path, practice pure and chaste conduct with pure faith, accomplish what is to be done, cut off birth and death, and in this very life realize it for myself, not experiencing future existence.'"

佛告比丘：「时，阎罗王自生念言：『世间众生迷惑无识，身为恶行，口、意为恶，其后命终，少有不受此苦。世间众生若能改恶，修身、口、意为善行者，命终受乐，如彼天神。我若命终生人中者，若遇如来，当于正法中剃除须发，服三法衣，出家修道，以清净信修净梵行，所作已办，断除生死，于现法中自身作证，不受后有。』」

At that time, the World-Honored One spoke in verse:

尔时，世尊以偈颂曰：

Although they see the messengers, they still indulge in carelessness. Such people
are always anxious and are born in lowly places. If there are
wise people who see the messengers, they will be close to the
Dharma of the sages and not indulge in carelessness. Seeing the fear
of birth, due to birth, old age, sickness, and death, without birth
there is liberation, and birth, old age, sickness, and death are exhausted
They attain a place of peace and tranquility, and in the present
life attain the unconditioned. Having crossed all fears and worries, they will
definitely attain parinirvāṇa.

「虽见天使者，　　而犹为放逸，其人常怀忧，　　生于卑贱处。若有智慧人，　　见于天使者，亲近贤圣法，　　而不为放逸。见受生恐畏，　　由生老病死，无受则解脱，　　生老病死尽。彼得安隐处，　　现在得无为，已渡诸忧畏，　　决定般涅槃。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "There are four kinds of dragons. What are the four? First, those born from eggs, second, those born from wombs, third, those born from moisture, and fourth, those born miraculously. These are the four kinds. There are four kinds of garuḍas. What are the four? First, those born from eggs, second, those born from wombs, third, those born from moisture, and fourth, those born miraculously. These are the four kinds. At the bottom of the great ocean is the palace of the dragon king Sāgara, which is eighty thousand yojanas long and wide. The palace walls are sevenfold, with sevenfold railings, sevenfold nets, and sevenfold rows of trees, all adorned with the seven treasures, and so on, up to countless birds singing harmoniously, also like this. Between Mount Sumeru and Mount Khadira is the palace of the two dragon kings Nanda and Upananda, each sixty thousand yojanas long and wide. The palace walls are sevenfold, with sevenfold railings, sevenfold nets, and sevenfold rows of trees, all adorned with the seven treasures, and so on, up to countless birds singing harmoniously, also like this.

佛告比丘：「有四种龙。何等为四？一者卵生，二者胎生，三者湿生，四者化生，是为四种。有四种金翅鸟。何等为四？一者卵生，二者胎生，三者湿生，四者化生，是为四种。大海水底有娑竭龙王宫，纵广八万由旬，宫墙七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝严饰，皆七宝成，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。须弥山王与佉陀罗山二山中间，有难陀、婆难陀二龙王宫，各各纵广六千由旬，宫墙七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。

On the northern shore of the great ocean is a large tree called Jūlaśāmalā, which is shared by the dragon kings and garuḍas. The tree is seven yojanas in circumference at the base, one hundred yojanas tall, and its branches and leaves spread out fifty yojanas. To the east of this great tree are the palaces of the egg-born dragon kings and egg-born garuḍas, each palace being six thousand yojanas long and wide. The palace walls are sevenfold, with sevenfold railings, sevenfold nets, and sevenfold rows of trees, all adorned with the seven treasures, and so on, up to countless birds singing harmoniously, also like this. To the south of the Jūlaśāmalā tree are the palaces of the womb-born dragon kings and womb-born garuḍas, each palace being six thousand yojanas long and wide. The palace walls are sevenfold, with sevenfold railings, sevenfold nets, and sevenfold rows of trees, all adorned with the seven treasures, and so on, up to countless birds singing harmoniously, also like this. To the west of the Jūlaśāmalā tree are the palaces of the moisture-born dragons and moisture-born garuḍas, each palace being six thousand yojanas long and wide. The palace walls are sevenfold, with sevenfold railings, sevenfold nets, and sevenfold rows of trees, all adorned with the seven treasures, and so on, up to countless birds singing harmoniously, also like this. To the north of the Jūlaśāmalā tree are the palaces of the magically-born dragon kings and magically-born garuḍas, each palace being six thousand yojanas long and wide. The palace walls are sevenfold, with sevenfold railings, sevenfold nets, and sevenfold rows of trees, all adorned with the seven treasures, and so on, up to countless birds singing harmoniously, also like this.

「大海北岸有一大树，名究罗睒摩罗，龙王、金翅鸟共有此树。其树下围七由旬，高百由旬，枝叶四布五十由旬。此大树东有卵生龙王宫、卵生金翅鸟宫，其宫各各纵广六千由旬，宫墙七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成，乃至无数众鸟相和悲鸣，亦复如是。其究罗睒摩罗树南有胎生龙王宫、胎生金翅鸟宫，其宫各各纵广六千由旬，宫墙七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成，乃至无数众鸟相和悲鸣，亦复如是。究罗睒摩罗树西有湿生龙宫、湿生金翅鸟宫，其宫各各纵广六千由旬，宫墙七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。究罗睒摩罗树北有化生龙王宫、化生金翅鸟宫，其宫各各纵广六千由旬，宫墙七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成，乃至无数众鸟相和悲鸣，亦复如是。

When an egg-born garuḍa wants to catch and eat a dragon, it flies down from the eastern branch of the Jūlaśāmalā tree and beats the great ocean with its wings. The sea water parts for two hundred yojanas, and it takes an egg-born dragon to eat it, as it pleases. But it cannot take womb-born, moisture-born, or magically-born dragons.

「若卵生金翅鸟欲搏食龙时，从究罗睒摩罗树东枝飞下，以翅搏大海水，海水两披] cf.【丽】二百由旬，取卵生龙食之，随意自在，而不能取胎生、湿生、化生诸龙。

When a womb-born garuḍa wants to catch and eat an egg-born dragon, it flies down from the eastern branch of the tree and beats the great ocean with its wings. The sea water parts for two hundred yojanas, and it takes an egg-born dragon to eat it, as it pleases. When a womb-born garuḍa wants to eat a womb-born dragon, it flies down from the southern branch of the tree and beats the great ocean with its wings. The sea water parts for four hundred yojanas, and it takes a womb-born dragon to eat it, as it pleases. But it cannot take moisture-born or magically-born dragons to eat.

「若胎生金翅鸟欲搏食卵生龙时，从树东枝飞下，以翅搏大海水，海水两披二百由旬，取卵生龙食之，自在随意。若胎生金翅鸟欲食胎生龙时，从树南枝飞下，以翅搏大海水，海水两披四百由旬，取胎生龙食之，随意自在，而不能取湿生、化生诸龙食也。

When a moisture-born garuḍa wants to eat an egg-born dragon, it flies down from the eastern branch of the tree and beats the great ocean with its wings. The sea water parts for two hundred yojanas, and it takes an egg-born dragon to eat it, as it pleases. When a moisture-born garuḍa wants to eat a womb-born dragon, it flies down from the southern branch of the tree and beats the great ocean with its wings. The sea water parts for four hundred yojanas, and it takes a womb-born dragon to eat it, as it pleases. When a moisture-born garuḍa wants to eat a moisture-born dragon, it flies down from the western branch of the tree and beats the great ocean with its wings. The sea water parts for eight hundred yojanas, and it takes a moisture-born dragon to eat it, as it pleases. But it cannot take a magically-born dragon to eat.

「湿生金翅鸟欲食卵生龙时，从树东枝飞下，以翅搏大海水，海水两披二百由旬，取卵生龙食之，自在随意。湿生金翅鸟欲食胎生龙时，于树南枝飞下，以翅搏大海水，海水两披四百由旬，取胎生龙食之，自在随意。湿生金翅鸟欲食湿生龙时，于树西枝飞下，以翅搏大海水，海水两披八百由旬，取湿生龙食之，自在随意，而不能取化生龙食。

When a magically-born garuḍa wants to eat an egg-born dragon, it flies down from the eastern branch of the tree and beats the great ocean with its wings. The sea water parts for two hundred yojanas, and it takes an egg-born dragon to eat it, as it pleases. When a magically-born garuḍa wants to eat a womb-born dragon, it flies down from the southern branch of the tree and beats the great ocean with its wings. The sea water parts for four hundred yojanas, and it takes a womb-born dragon to eat it, as it pleases. When a magically-born garuḍa wants to eat a moisture-born dragon, it flies down from the western branch of the tree and beats the great ocean with its wings. The sea water parts for eight hundred yojanas, and it takes a moisture-born dragon to eat it. When a magically-born garuḍa wants to eat a magically-born dragon, it flies down from the northern branch of the tree and beats the great ocean with its wings. The sea water parts for one thousand six hundred yojanas, and it takes a magically-born dragon to eat it, as it pleases. These are the dragons eaten by the garuḍas.

「化生金翅鸟欲食卵生龙时，从树东枝飞下，以翅搏大海水，海水两披二百由旬，取卵生龙食之，自在随意。化生金翅鸟欲食胎生龙时，从树南枝飞下，以翅搏大海水，海水两披四百由旬，取胎生龙食之，随意自在。化生金翅鸟欲食湿生龙时，从树西枝飞下，以翅搏大海水，海水两披八百由旬，取湿生龙食之。化生金翅鸟欲食化生龙时，从树北枝飞下，以翅搏大海水，海水两披千六百由旬，取化生龙食之，随意自在。是为金翅鸟所食诸龙。

There are also great dragons that the garuḍas cannot get. Who are they? The dragon kings Sāgara, Nanda, Upananda, Anavatapta, Virūḍhaka, Sudarśana, Aruṇa, Kakudha, Kapila, Aparājita, Kakudha, Kukkuṭa, Anavatapta, Sudarśana, Uśīragiri, Takṣaka, these great dragon kings are all not eaten by the garuḍas. Those dragons who live near them are also not eaten by the garuḍas.

「复有大龙，金翅鸟所不能得。何者是？娑竭龙王、难陀龙王、跋难陀龙王、伊那婆罗龙王、提头赖咤龙王、善见龙王、阿卢龙王、伽拘罗龙王、伽毗罗龙王、阿波罗龙王、伽［少／兔］龙王、瞿伽［少／兔］龙王、阿耨达龙王、善住龙王、优睒伽波头龙王、得叉伽龙王，此诸大龙王皆不为金翅鸟之所搏食，其有诸龙在近彼住者，亦不为金翅鸟之所搏食。」

The Buddha told the monks: "If there are sentient beings who uphold the dragon precepts, have a mind towards dragons, and possess the dragon Dharma, they will be reborn among dragons. If there are sentient beings who uphold the garuḍa precepts, have a mind towards garuḍas, and possess their Dharma, they will be reborn among garuḍas. If there are sentient beings who uphold the rabbit or owl precepts, have a mind towards rabbits or owls, and possess their Dharma, they will fall into the state of rabbits or owls. If there are sentient beings who uphold the dog precepts, or the cow precepts, or the deer precepts, or the mute precepts, or the maṇibhaṭa precepts, or the fire precepts, or the moon precepts, or the sun precepts, or the water precepts, or the fire-worship precepts, or the precepts of ascetic defilement, they think: 'I uphold this mute Dharma, maṇibhaṭa Dharma, fire Dharma, sun and moon Dharma, water Dharma, fire-worship Dharma, and various ascetic Dharmas. With these merits, I wish to be reborn in heaven.' This is wrong view.

佛告比丘：「若有众生奉持龙戒，心意向龙，具龙法者，即生龙中。若有众生奉持金翅鸟戒，心向金翅鸟，具其法者，便生金翅鸟中。或有众生持兔枭戒者，心向兔枭，具其法者，堕兔枭中。若有众生奉持狗戒，或持牛戒，或持鹿戒，或持痖戒，或持摩尼婆陀戒，或持火戒，或持月戒，或持日戒，或持水戒，或持供养火戒，或持苦行秽污法，彼作是念：『我持此痖法、摩尼婆陀法、火法、日月法、水法、供养火法、诸苦行法，我持此功德，欲以生天。』此是邪见。」

The Buddha said: "I say that these people with wrong views will definitely go to two places, either to hell or to the four kinds of birth. There are some śramaṇas and brāhmaṇas who have such theories and views: 'The self and the world are permanent, this is true and the rest is false; the self and the world are impermanent, this is true and the rest is false; the self and the world are both permanent and impermanent, this is true and the rest is false; the self and the world are neither permanent nor impermanent, this is true and the rest is false. The self and the world have an end, this is true and the rest is false; the self and the world have no end, this is true and the rest is false; the self and the world both have an end and no end, this is true and the rest is false; the self and the world neither have an end nor no end, this is true and the rest is false. The self and life are the same, this is true and the rest is false; the self and life are different, this is true and the rest is false; there is neither self nor life, this is true and the rest is false; there is no self and no life, this is true and the rest is false.' Some say: 'There is such a thing as death of another, this is true and the rest is false.' Some say: 'There is no such thing as death of another, this is true and the rest is false.' Some say: 'There is such a thing and there is no such thing as death of another, this is true and the rest is false.' Some say: 'There is neither such a thing nor no such thing as death of another, this is true and the rest is false.'

佛言：「我说此邪见人必趣二处，若生地狱，有堕四生。或有沙门、婆罗门有如是论、如是见：『我、世间有常，此实余虚；我及世间无常，此实余虚；我及世间有常无常，此实余虚；我及世间非有常非无常，此实余虚。我、世有边，此实余虚；我、世无边，此实余虚；我、世有边无边，此实余虚；我、世非有边非无边，此实余虚。是命是身，此实余虚；是命异身异，此实余虚；非有命非无命，此实余虚；无命无身，此实余虚。』或有人言：『有如是他死，此实余虚。』有言：『无如是他死，此实余虚。』或言：『有如是无如是他死，此实余虚。』又言：『非有非无如是他死，此实余虚。』

Those śramaṇas and brāhmaṇas who make such theories and have such views, saying that the world is permanent, this is true and the rest is false, they have the view of self, the view of life, the view of body, and the view of world in their practices. Therefore, they say: 'The self and the world are permanent.' Those who say it is impermanent, they have the view of self, the view of life, the view of body, and the view of world in their practices. Therefore, they say: 'The self and the world are impermanent.' Those who say it is both permanent and impermanent, they have the view of self, the view of life, the view of body, and the view of world in their practices. Therefore, they say: 'The self and the world are both permanent and impermanent.' Those who say it is neither permanent nor impermanent, they have the view of self, the view of life, the view of body, and the view of world in their practices. Therefore, they say: 'The self and the world are neither permanent nor impermanent.'

「彼沙门、婆罗门若作如是论、如是见者，言世是常，此实余虚者，彼于行有我见、命见、身见、世间见，是故彼作是言：『我、世间有常。』彼言无常者，于行有我见、命见、身见、世间见，是故彼言：『我、世间无常。』彼言有常无常者，彼行于有我见、命见、身见、世间见，故言：『世间有常无常。』彼言非有常非无常者，于行有我见、命见、身见、世间见，故言：『我、世间非有常非无常。』

Those who say that the self and the world have an end, they have the view of self, the view of life, the view of body, and the view of world in their practices. They say: 'Life has an end, body has an end, the world has an end. From the initial conception until the charnel ground, the four great elements of the body continue in this way, up to seven lives. When the body and life are exhausted, I enter the pure aggregate.' Therefore, they say: 'I have an end.' Those who say that the self and the world are endless, they have the view of self, the view of life, the view of body, and the view of world in their practices. They say: 'Life is endless, body is endless. The world is endless. From the initial conception until the charnel ground, the four great elements of the body continue in this way, up to seven lives. When the body and life are exhausted, I enter the pure aggregate.' They say: 'I and the world are endless.' Those who say that this world is both finite and infinite, they have the view of self, the view of life, the view of body, and the view of world in their practices. They say: 'Life is both finite and infinite. From the initial conception until the charnel ground, the four great elements of the body continue in this way, up to seven lives. When the body and life are exhausted, I enter the pure aggregate.' Therefore, they say: 'I am both finite and infinite.' Those who say that the self and the world are neither finite nor infinite, they have the view of self, the view of life, the view of body, and the view of world in their practices. They say: 'Life and body are neither finite nor infinite. From the initial conception until the charnel ground, the four great elements of the body continue in this way, up to seven lives. When the body and life are exhausted, I enter the pure aggregate.' Therefore, they say: 'I am neither finite nor infinite.'

「彼言我、世间有边者，于行有我见、命见、身见、世间见，言：『命有边，身有边，世间有边，从初受胎至于冢间，所有四大身如是展转，极至七生，身、命行尽，我入清净聚。』是故彼言：『我有边。』彼言我、世间无边者，于行有我见、命见、身见、世间见，言：『命无边，身无边。世间无边，从初受胎至于冢间，所有四大身如是展转，极至七生，身、命行尽，我入清净聚。』是言：『我、世间无边。』彼作是言：『此世间有边无边。』彼于行有我见、命见、身见、世间见：『命有边无边，从初受胎至于冢间，所有四大身如是展转，极至七生，身、命行尽，我入清净聚。』是故言：『我有边无边。』彼作是言：『我、世间非有边非无边。』于行有我见、命见、身见、世间见：『命身非有边非无边，从初受胎至于冢间，所有四大身如是展转，极至七生，身、命行尽，我入清净聚。』是故言：『我非有边非无边。』

"Those who say that this is life and this is body, they have the view of life in this body and the view of life in other bodies. Therefore, they say: 'This is life and this is body.' Those who say that life is different from body, they have the view of life in this body and no view of life in other bodies. Therefore, they say: 'Life is different from body.' Those who say that body and life are neither existent nor nonexistent, they have no view of life in this body and the view of life in other bodies. Therefore, they say: 'Neither existent nor nonexistent.' Those who say that there is no body and life, they have no view of life in this body and no view of life in other bodies. Therefore, they say: 'No life, no body.' Those who say that there is another life after death, they see that there is life now and that there will be another body and life wandering about in the future. Therefore, they say: 'There is another life after death.' Those who say that there is no other life after death, they say that there is life in this world but no life in the next world. Therefore, they say: 'There is no other life after death.' Those who say that there is another life after death and that there is no other life after death, they say that life is cut off and extinguished in this world but that life wanders about in the next world. Therefore, they say: 'There is another life after death and there is no other life after death.' Those who say that there is neither another life after death nor no other life after death, they say that the body and life are cut off and extinguished in this world and that the body and life are cut off and extinguished in the next world. Therefore, they say: 'Neither another life after death nor no other life after death.'"

「彼言是命是身者，于此身有命见，于余身有命见，是故言：『是命是身。』言命异身异者，于此身有命见，于余身无命见，是故言：『命异身异。』彼言身命非有非无者，于此身无命见，于余身有命见，是故言：『非有非无。』彼言无身命者，此身无命见，余身无命见，是故言：『无命无身。』彼言有如是他死者，其人见今有命，后更有身、命游行，是故言：『有如是他死。』无如是他死者，彼言今世有命，后世无命，是故言：『无如是他死。』有如是他死无如是他死者，彼言今世命断灭，后世命游行，是故言：『有如是他命无如是他命。』非有非无如是他死者，彼言今身、命断灭，后身、命断灭，是故言：『非有非无如是他死。』」

At that time, the World Honored One told the bhikṣus: "In the past, there was a king named Mirror Face. He gathered a group of blind people together and asked them, 'You blind people, do you know what an elephant is?' They replied, 'Great King! We do not know or understand.' The king then said, 'Do you want to know what it looks like?' They replied, 'We want to know.' The king then ordered his attendants to bring an elephant and let the blind people touch it with their hands. Some touched the elephant's trunk and the king said, 'This is an elephant.' Some touched the elephant's tusk, some touched its ear, some touched its head, some touched its back, some touched its belly, some touched its thigh, some touched its arm, some touched its foot, some touched its tail, and the king said in each case, 'This is an elephant.'

尔时，世尊告诸比丘言：「乃往过去有王名镜面，时，集生盲人聚在一处，而告之曰：『汝等生盲，宁识象不？』对曰：『大王！我不识、不知。』王复告言：『汝等欲知彼形类不？』对曰：『欲知。』时，王即勅侍者，使将象来，令众盲子手自扪象。中有摸象得鼻者，王言此是象，或有摸象得其牙者，或有摸象得其耳者，或有摸象得其头者，或有摸象得其背者，或有摸象得其腹者，或有摸象得其髀者，或有摸象得其膊者，或有摸象得其迹者，或有摸象得其尾者，王皆语言：『此是象也。』

At that time, King Mirror Face then removed the elephant and asked the blind children, 'What is the elephant like?' The blind children who touched the elephant's trunk said, 'The elephant is like a curved yoke.' Those who touched the elephant's tusk said, 'The elephant is like a pestle.' Those who touched the elephant's ear said, 'The elephant is like a winnowing basket.' Those who touched the elephant's head said, 'The elephant is like a tripod.' Those who touched the elephant's back said, 'The elephant is like a hill.' Those who touched the elephant's belly said, 'The elephant is like a wall.' Those who touched the elephant's thigh said, 'The elephant is like a tree.' Those who touched the elephant's arm said, 'The elephant is like a pillar.' Those who touched the elephant's foot said, 'The elephant is like a mortar.' Those who touched the elephant's tail said, 'The elephant is like a rope.' They each argued with each other, saying this and that, not agreeing with each other. The king saw this and laughed happily.

「时，镜面王即却彼象，问盲子言：『象何等类？』其诸盲子，得象鼻者，言象如曲辕，得象牙者，言象如杵，得象耳者，言象如箕，得象头者，言象如鼎，得象背者，言象如丘阜，得象腹者，言象如壁，得象髀者，言象如树，得象膊者，言象如柱，得象迹者，言象如臼，得象尾者，言象如𫄠。各各共诤，互相是非，此言如是，彼言不尔，云云不已，遂至鬪诤。时，王见此，欢喜大笑。

At that time, King Mirror Face then spoke a verse, saying:

「尔时，镜面王即说颂曰：

The blind people gathered here, arguing and disputing. The elephant's body
is originally one, but different characteristics give rise to right and wrong.

「『诸盲人群集，　　于此竞诤讼，象身本一体，　　异相生是非。』」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "The non-Buddhist practitioners are also like this. They do not know the truth of suffering, the truth of the origin of suffering, the truth of the cessation of suffering, and the truth of the path. They each give rise to different views and argue with each other, saying that their own is right and start disputes. If there are śramaṇas and brāhmaṇas who can truly know the noble truth of suffering, the noble truth of the origin of suffering, the noble truth of the cessation of suffering, and the noble truth of the path, they will contemplate and harmonize with each other, have the same understanding, the same teacher, and be like water and milk. They will vigorously promote the Buddha's teachings and ensure their long-lasting peace and happiness."

佛告比丘：「诸外道异学亦复如是，不知苦谛，不知习谛、尽谛、道谛，各生异见，互相是非，谓己为是，便起诤讼。若有沙门、婆罗门能如实知苦圣谛、苦习圣谛、苦灭圣谛、苦出要谛，彼自思惟，相共和合，同一受，同一师，同一水乳，炽然佛法，安乐久住。」

At that time, the World-Honored One spoke a verse, saying:

尔时，世尊而说偈言：

If one does not know suffering, the origin
of suffering, the cessation of suffering, and the
path to the cessation of suffering, one loses
mental liberation and wisdom liberation. One cannot investigate
the root of suffering, the source of birth
old age, sickness, and death. If one can
truly know suffering, the cause of suffering, the
cessation of suffering, and the path to the
cessation of suffering, one will attain mental liberation
and wisdom liberation. Such a person can thoroughly
understand the root of the aggregates of suffering
and the source of birth, old age, sickness and death.

「若人不知苦，　　不知苦所起，亦复不知苦，　　所可灭尽处，亦复不能知，　　灭于苦集道，失于心解脱，　　慧解脱亦失，不能究苦本，　　生老病死源。若] cf.【丽】能谛知苦，　　知苦所起因，亦能知彼苦，　　所可灭尽处，又能善分别，　　灭苦集圣道，则得心解脱，　　慧解脱亦然。斯人能究竟，　　苦阴之根本，尽生老病死，　　受有之根原。

"Bhikṣus! Therefore, you should diligently cultivate and contemplate the noble truth of suffering, the noble truth of the origin of suffering, the noble truth of the cessation of suffering, and the noble truth of the path to the cessation of suffering."

「诸比丘！是故汝等当勤方便思惟苦圣谛、苦集圣谛、苦灭圣谛、苦出要谛。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "Under the sea north of Mount Sumeru is the city of the Rāhu asuras, which is 80,000 yojanas long and wide. The city has seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding it, all adorned with the seven treasures. The city is 3,000 yojanas high and 2,000 yojanas wide. The city gates are 1,000 yojanas high and 1,000 yojanas wide. The golden city has silver gates, and the silver city has golden gates. There are also countless birds singing harmoniously together, just like that. The small city ruled by the asura king is called Lunshuomobata, which is 60,000 yojanas long and wide. The city has seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding it, all adorned with the seven treasures. The city is 3,000 yojanas high and 2,000 yojanas wide. The city gates are 2,000 yojanas high and 1,000 yojanas wide. The golden city has silver gates, and the silver city has golden gates. There are also countless birds singing harmoniously together, just like that.

佛告比丘：「须弥山北大海水底有罗呵阿须伦城，纵广八万由旬，其城七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成，城高三千由旬，广二千由旬。其城门高一千由旬，广千由旬，金城银门，银城金门，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。其阿须伦王所治小城，当大城中，名轮输摩跋咤，纵广六万由旬，其城七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，七宝所成，城高三千由旬，广二千由旬。其城门高二千由旬，广千由旬，金城银门，银城金门，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。

Within the city, there is a separate council hall called Shesheli Sha. The walls of the hall are seven layers, with seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding it, all adorned with the seven treasures. The foundation of the hall is made entirely of beryl. The pillars and beams are made entirely of the seven treasures. The central pillar of the hall is 1,000 yojanas in circumference and 10,000 yojanas high. Under this pillar is a Dharma seat, 700 yojanas long and wide, carved and inlaid with the seven treasures. The hall has four doors, surrounded by railings. The steps and pavilions are seven layers, with seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding them, all adorned with the seven treasures. There are also countless birds singing harmoniously together, just like that. To the north of the council hall is the palace of the asuras, which is 10,000 yojanas long and wide. The palace walls are seven layers, with seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding them, all adorned with the seven treasures. There are also countless birds singing harmoniously together, just like that. To the east of the council hall is a garden called Shara, which is 10,000 yojanas long and wide. The garden walls are seven layers, with seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding them, all adorned with the seven treasures. There are also countless birds singing harmoniously together, just like that. To the south of the council hall is a garden called Jiemiao, which is 10,000 yojanas long and wide, just like the Shara garden. To the west of the council hall is a garden called Shanmo, which is 10,000 yojanas long and wide, also like the Shara garden. To the north of the council hall is a garden called Le Lin, which is 10,000 yojanas long and wide, also like the Shara garden.

「于其城内别立议堂，名曰七尸利沙，堂墙七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，七宝所成，议堂下基纯以车璩，其柱梁纯以七宝，其堂中柱围千由旬，高万由旬，当此柱下有正法座，纵广七百由旬，雕文刻镂，七宝所成。堂有四户，周匝栏楯，阶亭七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，七宝所成，乃至众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。其议堂北有阿须伦宫殿，纵广万由旬，宫墙七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成，乃至无数众鸟相和悲鸣，亦复如是。其议堂东有一园林，名曰娑罗，纵广万由旬，园墙七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成，乃至无数众鸟相和悲鸣，亦复如是。其议堂南有一园林，名曰极妙，纵广万由旬，如娑罗园。其议堂西有一园林，名曰睒摩，纵广万由旬，亦如娑罗园林。其议堂北有一园林，名曰乐林，纵广万由旬，亦如娑罗园林。

Between the Shara and Jiemiao gardens is a day-degree tree, which is 7 yojanas in circumference at the base, 100 yojanas high, and its branches and leaves spread out for 50 yojanas. The tree walls are seven layers, with seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding them, all adorned with the seven treasures. There are also countless birds singing harmoniously together, just like that. Between the Shanmo and Le Lin gardens is a pond called Balantan, whose water is clear and cool, without any impurities. The pond is surrounded by seven layers of precious moats, with seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding them, all adorned with the seven treasures. In the pond grow four kinds of flowers, whose petals are 1 yojana long and wide, and their fragrance spreads for 1 yojana. Their roots are like chariot hubs, and their sap flows out, white in color like milk, and sweet in taste like honey. There are countless birds singing harmoniously together. Also, along the pond are seven layers of steps and pavilions, with seven layers of gates and walls, seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding them, all adorned with the seven treasures. There are also countless birds singing harmoniously together, just like that.

「娑罗、极妙二园中间生昼度树，下围七由旬，高百由旬，枝叶四布五十由旬。树墙七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。又其睒摩、乐林二园中间有跋难陀池，其水清凉，无有垢秽。宝堑七重，周匝砌厕，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，七宝所成。于其池中生四种华，华叶纵广一由旬，香气流布亦一由旬，根如车毂，其汁流出，色白如乳，味甘如蜜，无数众鸟相和而鸣。又其池边有七重阶亭，门墙七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，七宝所成，乃至无数众鸟相和悲鸣，亦复如是。

The palaces of the Asura kings and their ministers are of various sizes. Some are 10,000 yojanas long and wide, some are 9,000 or 8,000 yojanas. The smallest palace is 1,000 yojanas. The palace walls are seven layers, with seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding them, all adorned with the seven treasures. There are also countless birds singing harmoniously together, just like that. The palaces of the lesser Asuras are of various sizes. Some are 1,000 yojanas long and wide, some are 900 or 800 yojanas. The smallest palace is 100 yojanas. They all have seven layers of palace walls, seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding them, all adorned with the seven treasures. There are also countless birds singing harmoniously together, just like that.

「其阿须伦王臣下宫殿，有纵广万由旬者，有九千、八千，极小宫殿至千由旬，宫墙七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。其小阿须伦宫殿有纵广千由旬、九百、八百，极小宫殿至百由旬，皆宫墙七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，七宝所成，乃至无数众鸟相和悲鸣，亦复如是。

To the north of the assembly hall is a staircase made of the seven treasures leading into the palace. There are also staircases leading to the Shara garden, the Jiemiao garden, the Shanmo garden, the Le Lin garden, the Dayu tree, the Balantan pond, the ministers' palaces, and the lesser Asura palaces. When the Asura king wants to go to the Shara garden for sightseeing, he thinks of the Asura king Vimati. The Asura king Vimati also thinks to himself, 'The Asura king Luohe is thinking of me.' He then adorns himself, rides a jeweled carriage, and is surrounded by countless great multitudes as attendants. He goes before the Asura king Luohe and stands to one side. At that time, the Asura king Luohe also thinks of the Asura king Boluohe. The Asura king Boluohe also thinks to himself, 'The king is now thinking of me.' He then adorns himself, rides a jeweled carriage, and is surrounded by countless great multitudes as attendants. He goes before King Luohe and stands to one side.

「其议堂北有七宝阶道入于宫中，复有阶道趣娑罗园，复有阶道趣极妙园，复有阶道趣睒摩园，复有阶道趣乐林园，复有阶道趣昼度树，复有阶道趣跋难陀池，复有阶道趣大臣宫殿，复有阶道趣小阿须伦宫殿。若阿须伦王欲诣娑罗园游观时，即念毗摩质多阿须伦王，毗摩质多阿须伦王复自念言：『罗呵阿须伦王念我。』即自庄严驾乘宝车，无数大众侍从围遶，诣罗呵阿须伦王前，于一面立。时，阿须伦王复念波罗呵阿须伦王，波罗呵阿须伦王复自念言：『王今念我。』即自庄严驾乘宝车，无数大众侍从围遶，诣 罗呵王前，于一面立。

At that time, the Asura king Luohe also thinks of the Asura king Shanmolu. The Asura king Shanmolu also thinks to himself, 'The king is now thinking of me.' He then adorns himself, rides a jeweled carriage, and is surrounded by countless great multitudes as attendants. He goes before King Luohe and stands to one side. At that time, the king also thinks of the Asura minister. The Asura minister also thinks to himself, 'The king is now thinking of me.' He then adorns himself, rides a jeweled carriage, and is surrounded by countless great multitudes as attendants. He goes before King Luohe and stands to one side. At that time, the king also thinks of the lesser Asuras. The lesser Asuras also think to themselves, 'The king is now thinking of us.' They then adorn themselves and, together with the great multitudes, go before King Luohe and stand to one side.

「时，阿须伦王复念睒摩罗阿须伦王，睒摩罗阿须伦王复自念言：『今王念我。』即自庄严驾乘宝车，无数大众侍从围遶，诣罗呵王前，于一面立。时，王复念大臣阿须伦，大臣阿须伦复自念言：『今王念我。』即自庄严驾乘宝车，无数大众侍从围遶，诣罗呵王前，于一面立。时，王复念小阿须伦，小阿须伦复自念言：『今王念我。』即自庄严，与诸大众诣罗呵王前，于一面立。

At that time, King Luohe put on jeweled garments, rode a jeweled carriage, and was surrounded by countless great multitudes in front and behind. He went to the Shara forest. There was a natural wind that blew the gate open by itself. There was a natural wind that blew the ground clean. There was a natural wind that blew flowers and scattered them on the ground, the flowers reaching up to the knees. When King Luohe entered the garden, he enjoyed himself with them for one day, two days, up to seven days. After enjoying himself, he returned to his palace. Later, he also went to visit the Jiemiao garden, the Shanmo garden, and the Le garden, in the same way. King Luohe always had five great Asuras guarding him on the left and right: the first was named Ti Chi, the second was named Xiong Li, the third was named Wu Yi, the fourth was named Tou Shou, and the fifth was named Cui Fu. These five great Asuras always guarded him on the left and right. The palace of King Luohe was located under the great ocean, with the ocean above it. It was supported by four winds: the first was named Zhu Feng, the second was named Chi Feng, the third was named Bu Dong, and the fourth was named Jian Gu. The great ocean was held up in the sky, like floating clouds, one thousand yojanas away from the Asura palace, and would not fall.

「时，罗呵王身著宝衣，驾乘宝车，与无数大众前后围遶，诣娑罗林中，有自然风，吹门自开；有自然风，吹地令净；有自然风，吹花散地，花至于膝。时，罗呵王入此园已，共相娱乐，一日、二日，乃至七日，娱乐讫已，便还本宫。其后游观极妙园林、睒摩园林、乐园林，亦复如是。时，罗呵王常有五大阿须伦侍卫左右：一名提持，二名雄力，三名武夷，四名头首，五名摧伏。此五大阿须伦常侍卫左右。其罗呵王宫殿在大海水下，海水在上，四风所持：一名住风，二名持风，三名不动，四者坚固。持大海水，悬处虚空，犹如浮云，去阿须伦宫一万由旬终不堕落。阿须伦王福报、功德、威神如是。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "One thousand yojanas east of Mount Sumeru is the city of the Heavenly King Dhṛtarāṣṭra, named Xian Shang, with a length and width of six thousand yojanas. The city has seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding it, decorated with the seven treasures, up to countless birds singing harmoniously, also like this. One thousand yojanas south of Mount Sumeru is the city of the Heavenly King Virūḍhaka, named Shan Jian, with a length and width of six thousand yojanas. The city has seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding it, decorated with the seven treasures, up to countless birds singing harmoniously, also like this. One thousand yojanas west of Mount Sumeru is the city of the Heavenly King Virūpākṣa, named Zhou Luo Shan Jian, with a length and width of six thousand yojanas. The city has seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding it, decorated with the seven treasures, up to countless birds singing harmoniously, also like this. One thousand yojanas north of Mount Sumeru is the Heavenly King Vaiśravaṇa, with three cities: the first is named Ke Wei, the second is named Tian Jing, and the third is named Zhong Gui. Each has a length and width of six thousand yojanas. The cities have seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding them, decorated with the seven treasures, up to countless birds singing harmoniously, also like this.

佛告比丘：「须弥山王东千由旬提头赖咤天王城，名贤上，纵广六千由旬，其城七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。须弥山南千由旬有毗楼勒天王城，名善见，纵广六千由旬，其城七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。须弥山西千由旬有毗楼婆叉天王城，名周罗善见，纵广六千由旬，其城七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。须弥山北千由旬有毗沙门天王，王有三城：一名可畏，二名天敬，三名众归。各各纵广六千由旬，其城七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。

To the north of the city of Zhong Gui is a garden named Jiapi Yan Tou, with a length and width of four thousand yojanas. The garden wall has seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding it, decorated with the seven treasures, up to countless birds singing harmoniously, also like this. In the middle of the garden and city is a pond named Nalinini, with a length and width of forty yojanas. The water is clear and pure, without any impurities. It is lined with seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding it, decorated with the seven treasures. In the middle grow lotus flowers in blue, yellow, red, white, and various colors, shining half a yojana. The fragrance spreads and is smelled for half a yojana. The flower roots are as big as chariot hubs. The sap flows out, white in color like milk, and sweet in taste like honey. Up to countless birds sing harmoniously, also like this.

「众归城北有园林，名伽毗延头，纵广四千由旬，园墙七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。园城中间有池名那隣尼，纵广四十由旬，其水清澄，无有垢秽，以七宝堑厕砌其边，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，七宝所成，中生莲花，青、黄、赤、白、杂色，光照半由旬，其香芬薰闻半由旬，又其花根大如车毂，其汁流出，色白如乳，味甘如蜜，乃至无数众鸟相和悲鸣，亦复如是。

Except for the palaces of the sun and moon, the palaces of the Four Heavenly Kings are forty yojanas long and wide. The palace walls have seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding them, decorated with the seven treasures, up to countless birds singing harmoniously, also like this. The various palaces are forty yojanas, twenty yojanas, and the smallest is five yojanas long and wide. From the city of Zhong Gui, there is a jeweled staircase leading to the city of Xian Shang. There is also a staircase leading to the city of Shan Jian. There is also a staircase leading to the city of Zhou Luo Shan Jian. There is also a staircase leading to the city of Ke Wei and Tian Jing. There is also a staircase leading to the garden of Jiapi Yan Tou. There is also a staircase leading to the pond of Nalinini. There is also a staircase leading to the palaces of the ministers of the Four Heavenly Kings.

「除日月宫殿，诸四天王宫殿纵广四十由旬，宫墙七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。其诸宫殿有四十由旬、二十由旬，极小纵广五由旬。从众归城有宝阶道至贤上城，复有阶道至善见城，复有阶道至周罗善见城，复有阶道至可畏城、天敬城，复有阶道至伽毗延头园，复有阶道至那隣尼池，复有阶道至四天王大臣宫殿。

When the Heavenly King Virudhaka wishes to go to the Jiapi Yan Tou garden to enjoy the view, he thinks of the Heavenly King Dhṛtarāṣṭra. The Heavenly King Dhṛtarāṣṭra also thinks to himself: 'Now the Heavenly King Virudhaka is thinking of me.' He then adorns himself, rides a jeweled carriage, and is surrounded by countless Kumbhāṇḍa spirits in front and behind. He goes to the Heavenly King Virudhaka and stands to one side. At that time, the Heavenly King Virudhaka also thinks of the Heavenly King Virūpākṣa. The Heavenly King Virūpākṣa also thinks to himself: 'Now the Heavenly King Virudhaka is thinking of me.' He then adorns himself, rides a jeweled carriage, and is surrounded by countless Yakṣa spirits in front and behind. He goes to the Heavenly King Virudhaka and stands to one side. The Heavenly King Virudhaka also thinks of the Heavenly King Virūpākṣa. The Heavenly King Virūpākṣa also thinks to himself: 'Now the Heavenly King Virudhaka is thinking of me.' He then adorns himself, rides a jeweled carriage, and is surrounded by countless Nāga spirits in front and behind. He goes to the Heavenly King Virudhaka and stands to one side. The Heavenly King Virudhaka also thinks of the four great ministers of the Four Heavenly Kings. The four great ministers of the Four Heavenly Kings also think to themselves: 'Now the Heavenly King Virudhaka is thinking of us.' They then adorn themselves, ride jeweled carriages, and are led and followed by countless gods in front and behind. They go to the Heavenly King Virudhaka and stand to one side.
