「若毘沙门天王欲诣伽毘延头园游观时，即念提头赖天王，提头赖天王复自念言：『今毘沙门王念我。』即自庄严驾乘宝车，与无数干沓和神前后围遶，诣毘沙门天王前，于一面立。时，毘沙门王复念毘楼勒天王，毘楼勒天王复自念言：『今毘沙门王念我。』即自庄严驾乘宝车，与无数究槃荼神前后围遶，诣毘沙门天王前，于一面立。毘沙门王复念毘楼婆叉，毘楼婆叉复自念言：『今毘沙门王念我。』即自庄严驾乘宝车，无数龙神前后围遶，诣毘沙门王前，于一面立。毘沙门王复念四天王大臣，四天王大臣复自念言：『今毘沙门王念我。』即自庄严驾乘宝车，无数诸天前后导从，诣毘沙门天王前，于一面立。

"At that time, the Heavenly King Virudhaka immediately adorned himself, put on jeweled garments, rode a jeweled carriage, and went to the Jiapi Yan Tou garden with countless hundreds of thousands of heavenly beings. There was a natural wind that blew the gate open by itself; there was a natural wind that blew the ground to make it clean; there was a natural wind that blew flowers to scatter on the ground, the flowers reaching up to the knees. At that time, the king was in the garden enjoying himself together, for one day, two days, up to seven days, after enjoying the view, he returned to his palace. The Heavenly King Virudhaka always had five great ghosts and spirits guarding him on the left and right: one named Pancha Lou, two named Dan Dala, three named Himala, four named Ti Jie La, and five named Xiu Yi Lu Mo. These five ghosts and spirits always followed and guarded him. The Heavenly King Virudhaka's blessings, merits, and spiritual powers are like this."

「时，毘沙门天王即自庄严，著宝饰衣，驾乘宝车，与无数百千天神诣伽毘延头园。有自然风，吹门自开；有自然风，吹地令净；有自然风，吹花散地，花至于膝。时，王在园共相娱乐，一日、二日，乃至七日，游观讫已，还归本宫。毘沙门王常有五大鬼神侍卫左右：一名般阇楼，二名檀陀罗，三名醯摩跋陀，四名提偈罗，五名修逸路摩。此五鬼神常随侍卫。毘沙门王福报、功德、威神如是。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "On the summit of Mount Sumeru is the city of the Thirty-three Heavens, eighty thousand yojanas long and wide. The city has seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding it, adorned with the seven treasures. The city is one hundred yojanas high and sixty yojanas wide. The city gates are sixty yojanas high and thirty yojanas wide, and they are five hundred yojanas apart. Each gate is guarded by five hundred ghosts and spirits who protect the Thirty-three Heavens. The golden city has silver gates, the silver city has golden gates, and so on. The countless birds sing harmoniously, also like this. Inside the great city is another smaller city, sixty thousand yojanas long and wide. The city has seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding it, adorned with the seven treasures. The city is one hundred yojanas high and sixty yojanas wide. The city gates are five hundred yojanas apart, sixty yojanas high, and thirty yojanas wide. Each city gate is guarded by five hundred ghosts and spirits who guard the Thirty-three Heavens. The golden city has silver gates, the silver city has golden gates, the crystal city has lapis lazuli gates, the lapis lazuli city has crystal gates, the red pearl city has agate gates, the agate city has red pearl gates, and the vehicle jade city has gates made of various treasures.

佛告比丘：「须弥山王顶上有三十三天城，纵广八万由旬，其城七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成，城高百由旬，上广六十由旬。城门高六十由旬，广三十由旬，相去五百由旬有一门，其一一门有五百鬼神守侍卫护三十三天，金城银门，银城金门，乃至无数众鸟相和悲鸣，亦复如是。其大城内复有小城，纵广六万由旬，其城七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成，城高百由旬，广六十由旬，城门相去五百由旬，高六十由旬，广三十由旬，一一城门有五百鬼神侍卫门侧，守护三十三天。金城银门，银城金门，水精城琉璃门，琉璃城水精门，赤珠城马瑙门，马瑙城赤珠门，车璩城众宝门。

The railings are made of gold with silver crossbars, silver with gold crossbars, crystal with lapis lazuli crossbars, lapis lazuli with crystal crossbars, red pearls with agate crossbars, agate with red pearl crossbars, and vehicle jade with various treasure crossbars. Above the railings are jeweled nets, with golden nets hanging silver bells, silver nets hanging golden bells, lapis lazuli nets hanging crystal bells, crystal nets hanging lapis lazuli bells, red pearl nets hanging agate bells, agate nets hanging red pearl bells, and vehicle jade nets hanging various treasure bells. The golden trees have golden roots and branches with silver leaves and flowers, the silver trees have silver roots and branches with golden leaves and flowers, the crystal trees have crystal roots and branches with lapis lazuli flowers and leaves, the lapis lazuli trees have lapis lazuli roots and branches with crystal flowers and leaves, the red pearl trees have red pearl roots and branches with agate flowers and leaves, the agate trees have agate roots and branches with red pearl flowers and leaves, and the vehicle jade trees have vehicle jade roots and branches with various treasure flowers and leaves.

「其栏楯者，金栏银桄，银栏金桄，水精栏琉璃桄，琉璃栏水精桄，赤珠栏马瑙桄，马瑙栏赤珠桄，车璩栏众宝桄。其栏楯上有宝罗网，其金罗网下悬银铃，其银罗网下悬金铃，琉璃罗网悬水精铃，水精罗网悬琉璃铃，赤珠罗网悬马瑙铃，马瑙罗网悬赤珠铃，车璩罗网悬众宝铃。其金树者金根金枝银叶花实，其银树者银根银枝金叶花实，其水精树水精根枝琉璃花叶，其琉璃树琉璃根枝水精花叶，其赤珠树赤珠根枝马瑙花叶，马瑙树者马瑙根枝赤珠花叶，车璩树者车璩根枝众宝花叶。

The seven-layered city has four gates, with railings at the gates. On top of the seven-layered city are all surrounded by towers, pavilions, and terraces. There are gardens, forests, and bathing pools, with various colored precious flowers blooming, and rows of jeweled trees with abundant flowers and fruits. Fragrant breezes blow in all directions, pleasing the minds of people. There are countless thousands of ducks, geese, mandarin ducks, and other exotic birds singing harmoniously together. Outside the small city is the palace of the Irapat dragon, sixty thousand yojanas long and wide. The palace walls are seven layers, with seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding them, adorned with the seven treasures. There are also countless birds singing harmoniously together, also like this.

「其七重城，城有四门，门有栏楯，七重城上皆有楼阁台观周匝围遶，有园林浴池，生众宝花，杂色参间，宝树行列，华果繁茂，香风四起，悦可人心，凫雁、鸳鸯、异类奇鸟，无数千种，相和而鸣。其小城外中间有伊罗钵龙宫，纵广六千由旬，宫墙七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成，乃至无数众鸟相和悲鸣，亦复如是。

Within the city of Good View is the Hall of Good Dharma, one hundred yojanas long and wide, with seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding it, adorned with the seven treasures. The foundation of the hall is made entirely of pure gold, covered with lapis lazuli. The pillars in the hall are ten yojanas in circumference and one hundred yojanas high. Under the pillars are laid the heavenly emperor's seats, one yojana long and wide, with various colors interspersed, made of the seven treasures. The seats are soft, as soft as heavenly garments. On both sides of the seats are sixteen seats.

「其善见城内有善法堂，纵广百由旬，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成。其堂下基纯以真金，上覆琉璃，其堂中柱围十由旬，高百由旬，当其柱下敷天帝御座，纵广一由旬，杂色间厕，以七宝成，其座柔软，软若天衣，夹座两边左右十六座。

The hall has four gates, surrounded by railings made of the seven treasures. The steps of the hall are five hundred yojanas long and wide. The gates are seven layers, with seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding them, adorned with the seven treasures. There are also countless birds singing harmoniously together, also like this. To the north of the Hall of Good Dharma is the palace of the Heavenly Emperor, one thousand yojanas long and wide. The palace walls are seven layers, with seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding them, adorned with the seven treasures. There are also countless birds singing harmoniously together, also like this. To the east of the Hall of Good Dharma is a garden called Rough, one thousand yojanas long and wide. The garden walls are seven layers, with seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding them, adorned with the seven treasures. There are also countless birds singing harmoniously together, also like this. In the Rough Garden are two stone mounds decorated with heavenly gold, one called Wise and the other called Very Wise, each fifty yojanas long and wide. The stones are soft, as soft as heavenly garments.

「堂有四门，周匝栏楯，以七宝成，其堂阶道纵广五百由旬，门郭七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。善见堂北有帝释宫殿，纵广千由旬，宫墙七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成，乃至无数众鸟相和悲鸣，亦复如是。善见堂东有园林，名曰麤澁，纵广千由旬，园墙七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰以七宝成，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。麤澁园中有二石垛，天金校饰，一名贤，二名善贤，纵广各五十由旬，其石柔软，软若天衣。

To the south of the Palace of Good View is a garden called Painting Joy, one thousand yojanas long and wide. The garden walls are seven layers, with seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding them, adorned with the seven treasures. There are also countless birds singing harmoniously together, also like this. In the garden are two stone mounds made of the seven treasures, one called Day and the other called Very Day, each fifty yojanas long and wide. The mounds are soft, as soft as heavenly garments. To the west of the Hall of Good Dharma is a garden called Mixed, one thousand yojanas long and wide. The garden walls are seven layers, with seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding them, adorned with the seven treasures. There are also countless birds singing harmoniously together, also like this. In the garden are two stone mounds, one called Good View and the other called Following Good View, decorated with heavenly gold and made of the seven treasures, each fifty yojanas long and wide. The mounds are soft, as soft as heavenly garments. To the north of the Hall of Good Dharma is a garden called Great Joy, one thousand yojanas long and wide. The garden walls are seven layers, with seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding them, adorned with the seven treasures. There are also countless birds singing harmoniously together, also like this. In the garden are two stone mounds, one called Joy and the other called Great Joy, decorated with agate, each fifty yojanas long and wide. The mounds are soft, as soft as heavenly garments.

「善见宫南有园林，名曰画乐，纵广千由旬，园墙七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。其园内有二石垛，七宝所成，一名昼，二名善昼，各纵广五十由旬，其垛柔软，软若天衣。善见堂西有园林，名杂，纵广千由旬，园墙七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，七宝所成，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。其园中有二石垛，一名善见，二名顺善见，天金校饰，七宝所成，各纵广五十由旬，其垛柔软，软若天衣。善见堂北有园林，名曰大喜，纵广千由旬，园墙七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。其园中有二石垛，一名喜，二名大喜，车璩校饰，纵广五十由旬，其垛柔软，软若天衣。

Between the Rough Garden and the Painting Joy Garden is a pond called Nandana, one hundred yojanas long and wide. The water is clear and pure, without any impurities. There are seven layers of precious moats surrounding it, with seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding them, adorned with the seven treasures. There are four staircases on the four sides of the pond, with railings in between made of the seven treasures. There are also countless birds singing harmoniously together, also like this. There are four kinds of flowers in the pond, blue, yellow, red, white, and purple, mixed and arranged. Each flower leaf shades one yojana, and the fragrance spreads for one yojana. The roots are like chariot hubs, and the sap flows out, white in color like milk, and sweet in taste like honey. On the four sides of the pond there are also gardens. Between the Mixed Garden and the Great Joy Garden is a tree called Cūta, seven yojanas in circumference, one hundred yojanas high, with branches and leaves spreading fifty yojanas. Outside the tree is an empty pavilion five hundred yojanas long and wide, with palace walls seven layers, seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding it, adorned with the seven treasures. There are also countless birds singing harmoniously together, also like this.

「其麤澁园、画乐园中间有难陀池，纵广百由旬，其水清澄，无有垢秽，七重宝堑周匝砌厕，栏楯七重、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成。其池四面有四梯陛，周匝栏楯间以七宝，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。又其池中生四种花，青、黄、赤、白、红缥杂色间厕，其一花叶荫一由旬，香气芬熏闻一由旬，根如车毂，其汁流出，色白如乳，味甘如蜜。其池四面复有园林。其杂园林、大喜园林二园中间有树名昼度，围七由旬，高百由旬，枝叶四布五十由旬。树外空亭纵广五百由旬，宫墙七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。

The other palaces of the Trāyastriṃśa Heaven are one thousand yojanas long and wide. The palace walls are seven layers, with seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding them, adorned with the seven treasures. There are also countless birds singing harmoniously together, also like this. The palaces are nine hundred, eight hundred, and at least one hundred yojanas long and wide. The palace walls are seven layers, with seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding them, adorned with the seven treasures. There are also countless birds singing harmoniously together, also like this. The smaller palaces of the gods are one hundred yojanas long and wide, with ninety, eighty, and at least twelve yojanas. The palace walls are seven layers, with seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, and seven layers of trees surrounding them, adorned with the seven treasures. There are also countless birds singing harmoniously together, also like this.

「其余忉利天宫殿纵广千由旬，宫墙七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，以七宝成，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。其诸宫殿有纵广九百、八百，极小百由旬，宫墙七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝校饰，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。诸小天宫纵广百由旬，有九十、八十，极小至十二由旬，宫墙七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重行树，周匝围遶，以七宝成，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣，亦复如是。

To the north of the Sudharma Hall are two staircases leading to the palace of Śakra, the Lord of the Devas. To the east of the Sudharma Hall are two staircases leading to the Raurava Garden, and another staircase leading to the Citraratha Garden. There is another staircase leading to the Nandana Garden, another staircase leading to the Mahāvana Garden, another staircase leading to the Nandana Pond, another staircase leading to the Cūta Tree, another staircase leading to the palace of the Thirty-three Heavens, and another staircase leading to the palaces of the various heavens, and another staircase leading to the palace of the nāga king Elapatra. When Śakra, the Lord of the Devas, wishes to go to the Raurava Garden to play, he thinks of the ministers of the Thirty-three Heavens. The ministers of the Thirty-three Heavens then think to themselves, 'Now Śakra is thinking of me.' They then adorn themselves, ride in jeweled carriages, and surrounded by countless attendants, they go to Śakra and stand to one side. Śakra then thinks of the other devas, and the devas think, 'Now Śakra is thinking of me.' They then adorn themselves, follow the devas, and go to Śakra, standing to one side. Śakra then thinks of the nāga king Elapatra, and the nāga king Elapatra then thinks to himself, 'Now Śakra is thinking of me.' The nāga king then transforms himself into thirty-three heads, each head with six tusks, each tusk with seven bathing ponds, each bathing pond with seven large lotus flowers, each lotus flower with one hundred petals, and each petal with seven jade maidens playing music, dancing and singing on them. When the nāga king has made this transformation, he goes to Śakra and stands to one side.

「善见堂北有二阶道至帝释宫殿，善见堂东有二阶道至麤澁园，复有阶道至画乐园观，复有阶道至杂园中，复有阶道至大喜园，复有阶道至大喜池，复有阶道至昼度树，复有阶道至三十三天宫，复有阶道至诸天宫，复有阶道至伊罗钵龙王宫。若天帝释欲麤澁园中游观时，即念三十三天臣，三十三天臣即自念言：『今帝释念我。』即自庄严驾乘宝车，与无数众前后围遶至帝释前，于一面立。帝释复念其余诸天，诸天念言：『今帝释念我。』即自庄严，与诸天众相随至帝释前，于一面立。帝释复念伊罗钵龙王，伊罗钵龙王复自念言：『今帝释念我。』龙王即自变身出三十三头，一一头有六牙，一一牙有七浴池，一、一浴池有七大莲华，一一莲花有一百叶，一一花叶有七玉女，鼓乐弦歌，抃舞其上。时，彼龙王作此化已，诣帝释前，于一面立。

At that time, Śakra, Lord of the Devas, adorned himself with various treasures and jeweled ornaments, and sat on the first head of the Elapatra nāga king. On either side were the sixteen heavenly kings, sitting in order on the nāga's heads. Then Śakra, Lord of the Devas, together with countless heavenly attendants, went to the Raurava Garden. There was a natural wind that blew the gate open by itself. There was a natural wind that blew the ground clean. There was a natural wind that blew flowers onto the ground, and the flowers piled up, reaching to the knees. At that time, Śakra, Lord of the Devas, sat on the two stone mounds of Xian and Shanxian as he wished. The thirty-three kings each sat in order. There were also devas who could not attend and see the garden, and could not enter the garden to enjoy the five desires. Why was this? It was because their past meritorious deeds were not the same. There were also devas who could see the garden but could not enter, and could not enjoy the five desires together. Why was this? It was because their past meritorious deeds were not the same. There were also devas who could see and enter, but could not enjoy the five desires together. Why was this? It was because their past meritorious deeds were not the same. There were also devas who could enter and see, and enjoy the five desires. Why was this? It was because their past meritorious deeds were the same.

「时，释提桓因著众宝饰，璎珞其身，坐伊罗钵龙王第一顶上，其次两边各有十六天王，在龙顶上次第而坐。时，天帝释与无数诸天眷属围遶诣麤澁园。有自然风，吹门自开；有自然风，吹地令净；有自然风，吹花散地，众花积聚，花至于膝。时，天帝释于贤、善贤二石垛上随意而坐，三十三王各次第坐，复有诸天不得侍从见彼园观，不得入园五欲娱乐。所以者何？斯由本行功德不同。复有诸天得见园林而不得入，不得五欲共相娱乐。所以者何？斯由本行功德不同。复有诸天得见、得入，不得五欲共相娱乐。所以者何？斯由本行功德不同。复有诸天得入、得见，五欲娱乐。所以者何？斯由本行功德同故。

They play and enjoy themselves in the garden for one, two, up to seven days. After enjoying themselves, they return to their palaces. When Śakra, Lord of the Devas, visits the Citraratha Garden, Nandana Garden, and Mahāvana Garden, it is also like this. Why is it called the Raurava Garden? When one enters this garden, one's body becomes rough and harsh. Why is it called the Citraratha Garden? When one enters this garden, one's body naturally has various painted colors for entertainment. Why is it called the Nandana Garden? On the eighth, fourteenth, and fifteenth days of each month, except for the asura women, the celestial maidens are released to play and enjoy themselves with the celestial sons. Therefore, it is called the Nandana Garden. Why is it called the Mahāvana Garden? When one enters this garden, one is entertained and delighted, so it is called the Mahāvana Garden. Why is it called the Sudharma Hall? On this hall, one contemplates the wonderful Dharma and experiences pure bliss, so it is called the Sudharma Hall. Why is it called the Cūta Tree? There is a deity named Māndhātṛ on this tree, who always plays music to entertain himself, so it is called the Cūta Tree. Moreover, the branches and leaves of this great tree spread in all directions, luxuriant like a great jeweled cloud, so it is called the Cūta Tree.

「游戏园中，五欲自娱，一日、二日，至于七日，相娱乐已，各自还宫。彼天帝释游观画乐园、杂园、大喜园时，亦复如是。何故名之为麤澁园？入此园时，身体麤澁。何故名为画乐园？入此园时，身体自然有种种画色以为娱乐。何故名为杂园？常以月八日、十四日、十五日，除阿须伦女，放诸婇女与诸天子杂错游戏，是故名为杂园。何故名为大喜园？入此园时，娱乐欢乐，故名大喜。何故名为善法堂？于此堂上思惟妙法，受清净乐，故名善法堂。何故名为昼度树？此树有神，名曰漫陀，常作伎乐以自娱乐，故名昼度。又彼大树枝条四布，花叶繁茂如大宝云，故名昼度。

Śakra, Lord of the Devas, always has ten great heavenly sons as attendants. Who are the ten? The first is named Indra, the second is named Gauri, the third is named Virūḍhaka, the fourth is named Virūpākṣa, the fifth is named Dhṛtarāṣṭra, the sixth is named Virūḍhaka, the seventh is named Āyuṣmān, the eighth is named Vaiśravaṇa, the ninth is named Virūpākṣa, and the tenth is named Nārāyaṇa. Śakra, Lord of the Devas, has great supernatural powers and majestic virtue like this. The water and land flowers valued by the people of Jambudvīpa are: blue lotus flowers, red lotus flowers, white lotus flowers, and pink lotus flowers, soft and fragrant. The land-grown flowers are: jasmine flowers, magnolia flowers, pāṭala flowers, sumana flowers, pāṭala flowers, and maiden's hair flowers. The water and land flowers of the palaces of the nāgas, garuḍas, and the people of Kuru, Godānīya, Uttarakuru, and Pūrvavideha are also like this. The water-grown flowers in the palaces of the asuras are: blue lotus flowers, red lotus flowers, white lotus flowers, and pink lotus flowers, soft and fragrant. The land-grown flowers are: special flowers, pūga flowers, great pūga flowers, kācalī flowers, great kācalī flowers, maṇḍala flowers, and great maṇḍala flowers. The water and land flowers valued by the Four Heavenly Kings, the Thirty-three Heavens, the Yāma Heaven, the Tuṣita Heaven, the Nirmāṇarati Heaven, and the Paranirmitavaśavartin Heaven are also like this.

「释提桓因左右常有十大天子随从侍卫。何等为十？一者名因陀罗，二名瞿夷，三名毘楼，四名毘楼婆提，五名陀罗，六名婆罗，七名耆婆，八名灵醯嵬，九名物罗，十名难头。释提桓因有大神力，威德如是。阎浮提人所贵水花：优钵罗花、钵头摩花、拘物头花、分陀利花、须干头花，柔软香洁。其陆生花：解脱花、薝卜花、婆罗陀花、须曼周那花、婆师花、童女花。拘耶尼、欝单曰、弗于逮、龙宫、金翅鸟宫水陆诸花，亦复如是。阿须伦宫水中生花：优钵罗花、钵头摩花、拘物头花、分陀利花，柔软香洁。陆生花：殊好花、频浮花、大频浮花、伽伽利花、大伽伽利花、曼陀罗花、大曼陀罗花。四天王、三十三天、焰摩天、兜率天、化自在天、他化自在天所贵水陆诸花，亦复如是。

The devas have ten qualities. What are the ten? First, they can fly away countless times. Second, they can fly back countless times. Third, they can go without obstruction. Fourth, they can come without obstruction. Fifth, the bodies of the devas have no skin, bones, muscles, blood, or flesh. Sixth, their bodies have no impurities such as feces and urine. Seventh, their bodies have no fatigue. Eighth, the celestial maidens do not give birth. Ninth, the eyes of the devas do not blink. Tenth, their bodies can change color according to their wishes. If they wish to be blue, they are blue. If they wish to be yellow, they are yellow. Red, white, and various colors appear according to their wishes. These are the ten qualities of the devas. Humans have seven colors. What are the seven? Some people are golden in color, some are fiery in color, some are blue in color, some are yellow in color, some are red in color, some are black in color, and some are demonic in color. The devas and asuras also have seven colors, which are the same.

「天有十法，何等为十？一者飞去无限数。二者飞来无限数。三者去无碍。四者来无碍。五者天身无有皮肤、骨体、筋脉、血肉。六者身无不净大小便利。七者身无疲极。八者天女不产。九者天目不眴。十者身随意色，好青则青，好黄则黄，赤、白众色，随意而现。此是诸天十法。人有七色。云何为七？有人金色，有人火色，有人青色，有人黄色，有人赤色，有人黑色，有人魔色。诸天、阿须伦有七色，亦复如是。

Bhikṣus! The light of fireflies is not as bright as that of lamps, the light of lamps is not as bright as that of torches, the light of torches is not as bright as that of a pile of fires, the light of a pile of fires is not as bright as the palaces, cities, ornaments, clothing, and bodily radiance of the Four Heavenly Kings, the palaces, cities, ornaments, clothing, and bodily radiance of the Four Heavenly Kings is not as bright as the radiance of the Thirty-three Heavens, the radiance of the Thirty-three Heavens is not as bright as the radiance of the Yāma Heaven, the radiance of the Yāma Heaven is not as bright as the radiance of the Tuṣita Heaven, the radiance of the Tuṣita Heaven is not as bright as the radiance of the Nirmāṇarati Heaven, the radiance of the Nirmāṇarati Heaven is not as bright as the radiance of the Paranirmitavaśavartin Heaven, the radiance of the Paranirmitavaśavartin Heaven is not as bright as the palaces, clothing, and bodily radiance of the Brahmakāyika Heaven, the palaces, clothing, and bodily radiance of the Brahmakāyika Heaven is not as bright as the radiance of the Ābhāsvara Heaven, the radiance of the Ābhāsvara Heaven is not as bright as the radiance of the Śubhakṛtsna Heaven, the radiance of the Śubhakṛtsna Heaven is not as bright as the radiance of the Anabhraka Heaven, the radiance of the Anabhraka Heaven is not as bright as the radiance of the Puṇyaprasava Heaven, the radiance of the Puṇyaprasava Heaven is not as bright as the radiance of the Bṛhatphala Heaven, the radiance of the Bṛhatphala Heaven is not as bright from the light of fireflies up to the light of the Buddha, is not as bright as the light of the truth of suffering, the truth of the origin, the truth of cessation, and the truth of the path. Therefore, bhikṣus! Those who seek light should seek the light of the truth of suffering, the truth of the origin, the truth of cessation, and the truth of the path. They should practice in this way.

「诸比丘！萤火之明不如灯烛，灯烛之明不如炬火，炬火之明不如积火，积火之明不如四天王宫殿、城墎、璎珞、衣服、身色光明，四天王宫殿、城墎、璎珞、衣服、身色光明不如三十三天光明，三十三天光明不如焰摩天光明，焰摩天光明不如兜率天光明，兜率天光明不如化自在天光明，化自在天光明不如他化自在天光明，他化自在天光明不如梵迦夷天宫殿、衣服身色光明，梵迦夷天宫殿、衣服、身色光明不如光念天光明，光念天光明不如遍净天光明，遍净天光明不如果实天光明，果实天光明不如无想天光明，无想天光明不如无造天，无造天光明不如无热天，无热天光明不如善见天，善见天光明不如大善天，大善天光明不如色究竟天，色究竟天光明不如地自在天，地自在天光明不如佛光明。从萤火光至佛光明，合集尔所光明，不如苦谛光明，集谛、灭谛、道谛光明。是故，诸比丘！欲求光明者，当求苦谛、集谛、灭谛、道谛光明，当作是修行。

The people of Jambudvīpa are three and a half cubits tall, and their clothes are seven cubits long and three and a half cubits wide; the people of Aparagodānīya and Pūrvavideha are also three and a half cubits tall, and their clothes are seven cubits long and three and a half cubits wide; the people of Uttarakuru are seven cubits tall, and their clothes are fourteen cubits long and seven cubits wide, weighing one ounce; the asuras are one yojana tall, and their clothes are two yojanas long and one yojana wide, weighing six zhu; the Four Heavenly Kings are half a yojana tall, and their clothes are one yojana long and half a yojana wide, weighing half an ounce; the Trāyastriṃśa Heaven is one yojana tall, and their clothes are two yojanas long and one yojana wide, weighing six zhu; the Yāma Heaven is two yojanas tall, and their clothes are four yojanas long and two yojanas wide, weighing three zhu; the Tuṣita Heaven is four yojanas tall, and their clothes are eight yojanas long and four yojanas wide, weighing one and a half zhu; the Nirmāṇarati Heaven is eight yojanas tall, and their clothes are sixteen yojanas long and eight yojanas wide, weighing one zhu; the Paranirmitavaśavartin Heaven is sixteen yojanas tall, and their clothes are thirty-two yojanas long and sixteen yojanas wide, weighing half a zhu. The heavens above each wear clothes according to their bodies.

「阎浮提人身长三肘半，衣长七肘，广三肘半；瞿耶尼、弗于逮人身亦三肘半，衣长七肘，广三肘半；欝单曰人身长七肘，衣长十四肘，广七肘，衣重一两；阿须伦身长一由旬，衣长二由旬，广一由旬，衣重六铢；四天王身长半由旬，衣长一由旬，广半由旬，衣重半两；忉利天身长一由旬，衣长二由旬，广一由旬，衣重六铢；焰摩天身长二由旬，衣长四由旬，广二由旬，衣重三铢；兜率天身长四由旬，衣长八由旬，广四由旬，衣重一铢半；化自在天身长八由旬，衣长十六由旬，广八由旬，衣重一铢；他化自在天身长十六由旬，衣长三十二由旬，广十六由旬，衣重半铢。自上诸天，各随其身而著衣服。

The lifespan of the people of Jambudvīpa is one hundred years, with few living longer and many dying sooner. The lifespan of the people of Aparagodānīya is two hundred years, with few living longer and many dying sooner. The lifespan of the people of Pūrvavideha is three hundred years, with few living longer and many dying sooner. The lifespan of the people of Uttarakuru is one thousand years, with no increase or decrease. The lifespan of hungry ghosts is seventy thousand years, with few living longer and many dying sooner. The lifespan of dragons and garuḍas is one kalpa, or less. The lifespan of the asuras is one thousand heavenly years, with few living longer and many dying sooner. The lifespan of the Four Heavenly Kings is five hundred heavenly years, with few living longer and many dying sooner. The lifespan of the Trāyastriṃśa Heaven is one thousand heavenly years, with few living longer and many dying sooner. The lifespan of the Yāma Heaven is two thousand heavenly years, with few living longer and many dying sooner. The lifespan of the Tuṣita Heaven is four thousand heavenly years, with few living longer and many dying sooner. The lifespan of the Nirmāṇarati Heaven is eight thousand heavenly years, with few living longer and many dying sooner. The lifespan of the Paranirmitavaśavartin Heaven is sixteen thousand heavenly years, with few living longer and many dying sooner. The lifespan of the Brahmakāyika Heaven is one kalpa, or less. The lifespan of the Ābhāsvara Heaven is two kalpas, or less. The lifespan of the Śubhakṛtsna Heaven is three kalpas, or less. The lifespan of the Anabhraka Heaven is four kalpas, or less. The lifespan of the Puṇyaprasava Heaven is five hundred kalpas, or less. The lifespan of the Bṛhatphala Heaven is one thousand kalpas, or less. The lifespan of the Ākāśānantyāyatana Heaven is ten thousand kalpas, or less. The lifespan of the Vijñānānantyāyatana Heaven is twenty-one thousand kalpas, or less. The lifespan of the Ākiñcanyāyatana Heaven is forty-two thousand kalpas, or less. The lifespan of the Naivasaṃjñānāsaṃjñāyatana Heaven is eighty-four thousand kalpas, or less. This is the limit of sentient beings, this is the limit of lifespan, this is the limit of the world, this is called birth, old age, sickness, death, coming and going, the aggregate of realms and sense bases.

「阎浮提人寿命百岁，少出多减。拘耶尼人寿命二百岁，少出多减。弗于逮人寿三百岁，少出多减。欝单曰人尽寿千岁，无有增减。饿鬼寿七万岁，少出多减。龙、金翅鸟寿一劫，或有减者。阿须伦寿天千岁，少出多减。四天王寿天五百岁，少出多减。忉利天寿天千岁，少出多减。焰摩天寿天二千岁，少出多减。兜率天寿天四千岁，少出多减。化自在天寿天八千岁，少出多减。他化自在天寿天万六千岁，少出多减。梵迦夷天寿命一劫，或有减者。光音天寿命二劫，或有减者。遍净天寿命三劫，或有减者。果实天寿命四劫，或有减者。无想天寿命五百劫，或有减者。无造天寿命千劫，或有减者。无热天寿命二千劫，或有减者。善见天寿命三千劫，或有减者。大善见天寿命四千劫，或有减者。色究竟天寿命五千劫，或有减者。空处天寿命万劫，或有减者。识处天寿命二万一千劫，或有减者。不用处天寿命四万二千劫，或有减者。有想无想天寿命八万四千劫，或有减者。齐此为众生，齐此为寿命，齐此为世界，齐此名为生、老、病、死往来所趣，界、入聚也。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "All sentient beings subsist on four kinds of food. What are the four? Solid food, fine and smooth food, contact food, and thought food. The food of those sentient beings is not the same. The people of Jambudvīpa eat various kinds of rice, flour, and fish and meat as solid food, and use clothing and bathing as fine and smooth food. The people of Aparagodānīya and Pūrvavideha also eat various kinds of rice, flour, and fish and meat as solid food, and use clothing and bathing as fine and smooth food. The people of Uttarakuru only eat naturally grown rice, with heavenly flavors as solid food, and use clothing and bathing as fine and smooth food. Dragons and garuḍas eat turtles, fish, and tortoises as solid food, and use bathing and clothing as fine and smooth food. The asuras eat pure solid food as solid food, and use bathing and clothing as fine and smooth food. The Four Heavenly Kings, Trāyastriṃśa Heaven, Yāma Heaven, Tuṣita Heaven, Nirmāṇarati Heaven, and Paranirmitavaśavartin Heaven eat pure solid food as solid food, and use bathing and clothing as fine and smooth food. The heavens above eat the joy and bliss of meditation. What sentient beings eat contact food? Egg-born sentient beings eat contact food. What sentient beings eat thought food? There are sentient beings who subsist on thought food, whose faculties grow and whose lifespan does not end. This is called thought food. What sentient beings eat consciousness food? The sentient beings in hell and the formless heavens are called consciousness food.

佛告比丘：「一切众生以四食存。何谓为四？抟、细滑食为第一，触食为第二，念食为第三，识食为第四。彼彼众生所食不同。阎浮提人种种饭、𪎊面、鱼肉以为抟食，衣服、洗浴为细滑食。拘耶尼、弗于逮人亦食种种饭𪎊面、鱼肉以为抟食，衣服、洗浴为细滑食。欝单曰人唯食自然粳米，天味具足以为抟食，衣服、洗浴为细滑食。龙、金翅鸟食鼋鼍、鱼鳖以为抟食，洗浴、衣服为细滑食。阿须伦食净抟食以为抟食，洗浴、衣服为细滑食。四天王、忉利天、焰摩天、兜率天、化自在天、他化自在天食净抟食以为抟食，洗浴、衣服为细滑食。自上诸天以禅定喜乐为食。何等众生触食？卵生众生触食。何等众生念食？有众生因念食得存，诸根增长，寿命不绝，是为念食。何等识食？地狱众生及无色天，是名识食。

The people of Jambudvīpa use gold, silver, jewels, grain, silk, and slaves to trade and sell for a living. The people of Aparagodānīya use cattle, sheep, and jewels to trade for a living. The people of Pūrvavideha use grain, silk, and pearls to trade for a living. The people of Uttarakuru have no trading or selling for a living. The people of Jambudvīpa have marriages, with men marrying and women being given in marriage. The people of Aparagodānīya and Pūrvavideha also have marriages, with men marrying and women being given in marriage. The people of Uttarakuru have no marriages, with men and women not being given in marriage. Dragons, garuḍas, and asuras also have marriages, with men marrying and women being given in marriage. The Four Heavenly Kings, Trāyastriṃśa Heaven, up to Paranirmitavaśavartin Heaven also have marriages, with men marrying and women being given in marriage. The heavens above have no men and women. The people of Jambudvīpa have sexual intercourse between men and women, with their bodies touching each other to form yin and yang. The people of Aparagodānīya, Pūrvavideha, and Uttarakuru also have their bodies touching each other to form yin and yang. Dragons and garuḍas also have their bodies touching each other to form yin and yang. The asuras have their bodies close to each other, forming yin and yang with their breath. The Four Heavenly Kings and Trāyastriṃśa Heaven are also like this. The Yāma Heaven forms yin and yang by being close to each other. The Tuṣita Heaven forms yin and yang by holding hands. The Nirmāṇarati Heaven forms yin and yang by a mature gaze. The Paranirmitavaśavartin Heaven forms yin and yang by a brief glance. The heavens above have no more sexual desire.

「阎浮提人以金银、珍宝、谷帛、奴仆治生贩卖以自生活。拘耶尼人以牛羊、珠宝市易生活。弗于逮人以谷帛、珠玑市易自活。欝单曰人无有市易治生自活。阎浮提人有婚姻往来、男娶女嫁。拘耶尼人、弗于逮人亦有婚姻、男娶女嫁。欝单曰人无有婚姻、男女嫁娶。龙、金翅鸟、阿须伦亦有婚姻、男女嫁娶。四天王、忉利天，乃至他化自在天亦有婚姻、男娶女嫁。自上诸天无复男女。阎浮提人男女交会，身身相触以成阴阳。拘耶尼、弗于逮、欝单曰人亦身身相触以成阴阳。龙、金翅鸟亦身身相触以成阴阳。阿须伦身身相近，以气成阴阳。四天王、忉利天亦复如是。焰摩天相近以成阴阳。兜率天执手成阴阳。化自在天熟视成阴阳。他化自在天暂视成阴阳。自上诸天无复婬欲。

If there are sentient beings who do evil with the body, speak evil, and think evil, when their bodies perish and their lives end, their later consciousness ceases, and the initial consciousness of hell arises. Based on consciousness, there is name and form. Based on name and form, there are the six sense bases. If there are sentient beings who do evil with the body, speak evil, and think evil, when their bodies perish and their lives end, they fall into the animal realm. Their later consciousness ceases, and the initial consciousness of the animal realm arises. Based on consciousness, there is name and form. Based on name and form, there are the six sense bases. If there are sentient beings who do evil with the body, speak evil, and think evil, when their bodies perish and their lives end, they fall into the realm of hungry ghosts. Their later consciousness ceases, and the initial consciousness of the hungry ghost realm arises. Based on consciousness, there is name and form. Based on name and form, there are the six sense bases. If there are sentient beings who do good with the body, speak good, and think good, when their bodies perish and their lives end, they are reborn among humans. Their later consciousness ceases, and the initial consciousness of the human realm arises. Based on consciousness, there is name and form. Based on name and form, there are the six sense bases.

「若有众生身行恶，口言恶，意念恶，身坏命终，此后识灭，泥梨初识生，因识有名色，因名色有六入。或有众生身行恶，口言恶，意念恶，身坏命终，堕畜生中，此后识灭，畜生初识生，因识有名色，因名色有六入。或有众生身行恶，口言恶，意念恶，身坏命终，堕饿鬼中，此后识灭，饿鬼初识生，因识有名色，因名色有六入。或有众生身行善，口言善，意念善，身坏命终，得生人中，此后识灭，人中初识生，因识有名色，因名色有六入。

If there are sentient beings who do good with the body, speak good, and think good, when their bodies perish and their lives end, they are reborn in the Heaven of the Four Heavenly Kings. Their later consciousness ceases, and the initial consciousness of the Heaven of the Four Heavenly Kings arises. Based on consciousness, there is name and form. Based on name and form, there are the six sense bases. When those gods are first born, they are like one or two year old children in the human realm, naturally manifesting and sitting on the laps of the gods. The gods then say: 'This is my child.' Due to the retribution of their actions, natural wisdom arises. They then think to themselves: 'By what actions was I born here?' They then further think: 'In the past, I did good with the body, spoke good, and thought good in the human realm. Because of these actions, I am now reborn in the heavens. If I were to die here and be reborn in the human realm again, I would purify my body, speech, and mind, and be even more diligent in cultivating good practices.' Soon after the child is born, it feels hungry. In front of the child, there is a naturally appearing jeweled vessel filled with pure food of a hundred flavors. If their merit is great, the color of the rice is white. If their merit is middling, the color of the rice is blue. If their merit is lesser, the color of the rice is red. The child reaches out with their hand, takes the rice, and puts it in their mouth. The food naturally digests, like butter poured into fire. After the child has eaten, they feel thirsty. There is a naturally appearing jeweled vessel filled with nectar. If their merit is great, the color of the nectar is white. If their merit is middling, the color of the nectar is blue. If their merit is lesser, the color of the nectar is red. The child takes the nectar and drinks it. The nectar naturally digests, like butter poured into fire.

「或有众生身行善，口言善，意念善，身坏命终，生四天王，此后识灭，四天王识初生，因识有名色，因名色有六入。彼天初生，如此人间一、二岁儿，自然化现，在天膝上坐，彼天即言：『此是我子。』由行报故，自然智生，即自念言：『我由何行，今生此间？』即复自念：『我昔于人间身行善，口言善，意念善，由此行故，今得生天。我设于此命终，复生人间者，当净身、口、意，倍复精勤，修诸善行。』儿生未久便自觉饥，当其儿前有自然宝器，盛天百味自然净食，若福多者饭色为白，其福中者饭色为青，其福下者饭色为赤。彼儿以手探饭著口中，食自然消化，如酥投火。彼儿食讫，方自觉渴，有自然宝器盛甘露浆，其福多者浆色为白，其福中者浆色为青，其福下者浆色为赤。其儿取彼浆饮，浆自消化，如酥投火。

After the child has eaten and drunk, their body grows to the same size as the other gods. They then enter a bathing pool to bathe and wash, enjoying themselves. After enjoying themselves, they leave the bathing pool and go to a fragrant tree. The fragrant tree bends down, and they take various fragrances to anoint their bodies. They then go to a tree of cloth, and the tree bends down, allowing them to take various garments to wear on their bodies. They then go to a tree of ornaments, and the tree bends down, allowing them to take various ornaments to adorn their bodies. They then go to a tree of garlands, and the tree bends down, allowing them to take garlands to wear on their heads. They then go to a tree of vessels, and the tree bends down, allowing them to take jeweled vessels. They then go to a fruit tree, and the tree bends down, allowing them to take natural fruits to eat or chew, or to strain the juice to drink. They then go to a tree of musical instruments, and the tree bends down, allowing them to take heavenly musical instruments to play with clear and wonderful sounds. They sing and go towards the various gardens and forests. They see countless heavenly maidens playing music, singing, laughing, and talking to each other. As they wander and observe, they become attached and forget what they saw in the east when they look west, and forget what they saw in the west when they look east. When they were first born, they knew and thought to themselves: 'By what actions was I born here?' But while wandering and observing, they completely forgot this thought. Then there were maidservants to attend them.

「彼儿饮食已讫，身体长大，与余天等，即入浴池沐浴澡洗，以自娱乐。自娱乐已，还出浴池，诣香树下，香树曲躬，手取众香，以自涂身。复诣劫贝衣树，树为曲躬，取种种衣，著其身上。复诣庄严树，树为曲躬，取种种庄严，以自严身。复诣鬘树，树为曲躬，取鬘贯首。复诣器树，树为曲躬，即取宝器。复诣果树，树为曲躬，取自然果，或食或含，或漉汁而饮。复诣乐器树，树为曲躬，取天乐器，以清妙声和弦而歌，向诸园林。彼见无数天女鼓乐弦歌，语笑相向，其天游观，遂生染著，视东忘西，视西忘东，其初生时，知自念言：『我由何行，今得生此？』当其游处观时，尽忘此念。于是便有婇女侍从。

"If there are sentient beings who do good with the body, speak good, and think good, when their bodies perish and their lives end, they are reborn in the Heaven of the Thirty-three. Their later consciousness ceases, and the initial consciousness of the Heaven of the Thirty-three arises. Based on consciousness, there is name and form. Based on name and form, there are the six sense bases. When those gods are first born, they are like two or three year old children in the human realm. They naturally manifest and sit on the laps of the gods. The gods then say: 'This is my son. This is my daughter.' It is also like this. If there are sentient beings who do good with the body, speak good, and think good, when their bodies perish and their lives end, they are reborn in the Heaven of Yāma. When those gods are first born, they are like three or four year old children in the human realm. If there are sentient beings who do good with the body, speak good, and think good, when their bodies perish and their lives end, they are reborn in the Heaven of Tuṣita. When those gods are first born, they are like four or five year old children in the human realm. If there are sentient beings who do good with the body, speak good, and think good, when their bodies perish and their lives end, they are reborn in the Heaven of Nirmāṇarati. When those gods are first born, they are like five or six year old children in the human realm. If there are sentient beings who do good with the body, speak good, and think good, when their bodies perish and their lives end, they are reborn in the Heaven of Paranirmitavaśavartin. When those gods are first born, they are like six or seven year old children in the human realm. It is also like this."

「若有众生身行善，口言善，意念善，身坏命终，生忉利天，此后识灭，彼初识生，因识有名色，因名色有六入。彼天初生，如阎浮提二、三岁儿，自然化现，在天膝上，彼天即言：『此是我男，此是我女。』亦复如是。或有众生身、口、意善，身坏命终，生焰摩天，其天初生，如阎浮提三、四岁儿。或有众生身、口、意善，身坏命终，生兜率天，其天初生，如此世间四、五岁儿。或有众生身、口、意善，身坏命终，生化自在天，其天初生，如此世间五、六岁儿。或有众生身、口、意善，身坏命终，生他化自在天，其天初生，如此世间六、七岁儿，亦复如是。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "There are three fast days in a half month. What are the three? The eighth day of the month, the fourteenth day, and the fifteenth day. These are the three fast days. Why do we fast on the eighth day of the month? On the eighth day of the month, the Four Heavenly Kings always tell their messengers: 'You should go around the world to observe all people, to see if there are those who are filial to their parents, respectful to śramaṇas and brāhmaṇas, revere the elders, observe the precepts, give alms, and relieve the poor.' When the messengers hear the king's order, they go around the world to see if there are those who are filial to their parents, revere śramaṇas and brāhmaṇas, respect the elders, observe the precepts, give alms, and relieve the poor. After observing, they see that there are those in the world who are unfilial to their parents, disrespectful to their teachers, do not observe the precepts, and do not relieve the poor. They then return to report to the king: 'Heavenly King! There are very few in the world who are filial to their parents, revere śramaṇas and brāhmaṇas, observe the precepts, and give alms to the poor.' When the Four Heavenly Kings hear this, they are sad and displeased, and say: 'Alas! The people in the world are mostly evil. They are unfilial to their parents, disrespectful to their teachers, do not observe the precepts, and do not give alms to the poor. This will reduce the number of heavenly beings and increase the number of asuras.' If the messengers see in the world those who are filial to their parents, revere their teachers, diligently observe the precepts, and give alms to the poor, they will then return to report to the Heavenly King: 'In the world, there are those who are filial to their parents, revere their teachers, diligently observe the precepts, and give alms to the poor.' When the Four Heavenly Kings hear this, they are greatly delighted and exclaim: 'Excellent! We hear good words. In the world, there are those who are filial to their parents, revere their teachers, diligently observe the precepts, and give alms to the poor. This will increase the number of heavenly beings and reduce the number of asuras.'

佛告比丘：「半月三斋。云何为三？月八日斋、十四日斋、十五日斋，是为三斋。何故于月八日斋？常以月八日，四天王告使者言：『汝等案行世间，观视万民，知有孝顺父母，敬顺沙门、婆罗门，宗事长老，斋戒布施，济诸穷乏者不？』尔时，使者闻王教已，遍案行天下，知有孝顺父母，宗事沙门、婆罗门，恭顺长老，持戒守斋，布施穷乏者，具观察已，见诸世间不孝父母，不敬师长，不修斋戒，不济穷乏者，还白王言：『天王！世间孝顺父母，敬事师长，净修斋戒，施诸穷乏者，甚少！甚少！』尔时，四天王闻已，愁忧不悦，答言：『咄此为哉！世人多恶，不孝父母，不事师长，不修斋戒，不施穷乏，减损诸天众，增益阿须伦众。』若使者见世间有孝顺父母，敬事师长，勤修斋戒，布施贫乏者，则还白天王言：『世间有人孝顺父母，敬事师长，勤修斋戒，施诸穷乏者。』四天王闻已，即大欢喜，唱言：『善哉！我闻善言，世间乃能有孝顺父母，敬事师长，勤修斋戒，布施贫乏，增益诸天众，减损阿须伦众。』

Why do we fast on the fourteenth day of the month? On the fourteenth day of the month, the Four Heavenly Kings tell their crown prince: 'You should go around the world to observe all people, to see if there are those who are filial to their parents, respectful to śramaṇas and brāhmaṇas, revere the elders, observe the precepts, give alms, and relieve the poor.' When the crown prince receives the king's order, he goes around the world to observe all people. He knows that there are those who are filial to their parents, revere śramaṇas and brāhmaṇas, respect the elders, observe the precepts, give alms, and relieve the poor. After observing, he sees that there are those in the world who are unfilial to their parents, disrespectful to their teachers, do not observe the precepts, and do not relieve the poor. He then returns to report to the king: 'Heavenly King! There are very few in the world who are filial to their parents, revere śramaṇas and brāhmaṇas, observe the precepts, and give alms to the poor.' The Four Heavenly Kings hear this and are sad and displeased, saying: 'Alas! The people in the world are mostly evil. They are unfilial to their parents, disrespectful to their teachers, do not observe the precepts, and do not give alms to the poor. This will reduce the number of heavenly beings and increase the number of asuras.' If the crown prince sees in the world those who are filial to their parents, revere their teachers, diligently observe the precepts, and give alms to the poor, he will then return to report to the king: 'Heavenly King! There are those in the world who are filial to their parents, revere their teachers, diligently observe the precepts, and give alms to the poor.' The Four Heavenly Kings hear this and are greatly delighted, exclaiming: 'Excellent! We hear good words. In the world, there are those who are filial to their parents, revere their teachers, diligently observe the precepts, and give alms to the poor. This will increase the number of heavenly beings and reduce the number of asuras.' Therefore, we fast on the fourteenth day of the month.

「何故于十四日斋？十四日斋时，四天王告太子言：『汝当案行天下，观察万民，知有孝顺父母，敬事师长，勤修斋戒，布施贫乏者不？』太子受王教已，即案行天下，观察万民，知有孝顺父母，宗事师长，勤修斋戒，布施贫乏者，具观察已，见诸世间有不孝顺父母，不敬师长，不修斋戒，不施贫乏者，还白王言：『天王！世间孝顺父母，敬顺师长，净修斋戒，济诸贫乏者，甚少！甚少！』四天王闻已，愁忧不悦言：『咄此为哉！世人多恶，不孝父母，不事师长，不修斋戒，不济穷乏，减损诸天众，增益阿须伦众。』太子若见世间有孝顺父母，敬事师长，勤修斋戒，布施贫乏者，即还白王言：『天王！世间有人孝顺父母，敬顺师长，勤修斋戒，施诸贫乏者。』四天王闻已，即大欢喜，唱言：『善哉！我闻善言，世间能有孝事父母，宗敬师长，勤修斋戒，布施贫乏，增益诸天众，减损阿须伦众。』是故十四日斋。

Why do we fast on the fifteenth day of the month? On the fifteenth day of the month, the Four Heavenly Kings personally go down to inspect the world and observe all people. Do they see those who are filial to their parents, respectful to śramaṇas and brāhmaṇas, revere the elders, observe the precepts, give alms, and relieve the poor? They see that many people in the world are unfilial to their parents, disrespectful to their teachers, do not diligently observe the precepts, and do not give alms to the poor. Then the Four Heavenly Kings go to the Hall of Good Dharma and tell Śakra: 'Great King! You should know that sentient beings in the world are mostly unfilial to their parents, disrespectful to their teachers, do not cultivate the precepts, and do not give alms to the poor.' When Śakra and the gods of Trāyastriṃśa hear this, they are sad and displeased, saying: 'Alas! The people in the world are mostly evil. They are unfilial to their parents, disrespectful to their teachers, do not cultivate the precepts, and do not give alms to the poor. This will reduce the number of heavenly beings and increase the number of asuras.' If the Four Heavenly Kings see in the world those who are filial to their parents, respectful to their teachers, diligently observe the precepts, and give alms to the poor, they will return to the Hall of Good Dharma and tell Śakra: 'There are those in the world who are filial to their parents, respectful to their teachers, diligently observe the precepts, and give alms to the poor.' When Śakra and the gods of Trāyastriṃśa hear this, they are all greatly delighted and exclaim: 'Excellent! The world now has those who are filial to their parents, respectful to their teachers, diligently observe the precepts, and give alms to the poor. This will increase the number of heavenly beings and reduce the number of asuras.' Therefore, we fast on the fifteenth day of the month. Therefore, there are three fast days. At that time, Śakra wanted to make the gods even more joyful, so he spoke a verse:

「何故于十五日斋？十五日斋时，四天王躬身自下，案行天下，观察万民，世间宁有孝顺父母，敬事师长，勤修斋戒，布施贫乏者不？见世间人多不孝父母，不事师长，不勤斋戒，不施贫乏。时，四天王诣善法殿，白帝释言：『大王！当知世间众生多不孝父母，不敬师长，不修斋戒，不施贫乏。』帝释及忉利诸天闻已，愁忧不悦言：『咄此为哉！世人多恶，不孝父母，不敬师长，不修斋戒，不施穷乏，减损诸天众，增益阿须伦众。』四天王若见世间有孝顺父母，敬事师长，勤修斋戒，布施贫乏者，还诣善法堂，白帝释言：『世人有孝顺父母，敬事师长，勤修斋戒，布施贫乏者。』帝释及忉利诸天闻是语已，皆大欢喜，唱言：『善哉！世间乃有孝顺父母，敬事师长，勤修斋戒，布施贫乏者，增益诸天众，减损阿须伦众。』是故十五日斋戒。是故有三斋。尔时，帝释欲使诸天倍生欢喜，即说偈言：

Always on the eighth, fourteenth, and fifteenth days of the month, accept the
teachings and observe the precepts. Such a person is the same as me.

「『常以月八日，　　十四十五日，受化修斋戒，　　其人与我同。』」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "What Śakra said in this verse is not well received, not well spoken, and is unacceptable to me. Why is that? Because that Śakra has not yet exhausted desire, anger, and ignorance, and has not yet escaped birth, old age, sickness, death, sorrow, lamentation, suffering, and distress. I say that such a person has not yet escaped the root of suffering. If my bhikṣus have exhausted the taints, are arhats, have accomplished what was to be done, have laid down the heavy burden, have attained their own benefit, have exhausted all bonds, and are liberated equally, then such bhikṣus should speak this verse:

佛告比丘：「帝释说此偈，非为善受，非为善说，我所不可。所以者何？彼天帝释婬、怒、痴未尽，未脱生、老、病、死、忧、悲、苦恼。我说其人未离苦本。若我比丘漏尽阿罗汉，所作已办，舍于重担，自获己利，尽诸有结，平等解脱。如此比丘应说此偈：

Always on the eighth, fourteenth, and fifteenth days of the month, accept the
teachings and observe the precepts. Such a person is the same as me.

「『常以月八日，　　十四十五日，受化修斋戒，　　其人与我同。』」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "What that bhikṣu said in this verse is well received, well spoken, and is approved by me. Why is that? Because that bhikṣu has exhausted desire, anger, and ignorance, and has escaped birth, old age, sickness, death, sorrow, lamentation, suffering, and distress. I say that such a person has escaped the root of suffering."

佛告比丘：「彼比丘说此偈者，乃名善受，乃名善说，我所印可。所以者何？彼比丘婬、怒、痴尽已，脱生、老、病、死、忧、悲、苦恼，我说其人离于苦本。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "All the houses where people live have spirits, none are empty. In all the streets and crossroads, butcher shops, markets, and hilltop tombs, there are spirits, none are empty. All spirits follow what they rely on to be named. Relying on people, they are called people. Relying on villages, they are called villages. Relying on cities, they are called cities. Relying on countries, they are called countries. Relying on land, they are called land. Relying on mountains, they are called mountains. Relying on rivers, they are called rivers."

佛告比丘：「一切人民所居舍宅，皆有鬼神，无有空者。一切街巷四衢道中，屠儿市肆及丘冢间，皆有鬼神，无有空者。凡诸鬼神皆随所依，即以为名，依人名人，依村名村，依城名城，依国名国，依土名土，依山名山，依河名河。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "All trees, even the smallest ones the size of a chariot axle, have spirits dwelling in them, none are empty. When all men and women are first born, there are spirits that follow and protect them. When they die, those guardian spirits take away their vital energy, and the person dies."

佛告比丘：「一切树木极小如车轴者，皆有鬼神依止，无有空者。一切男子、女人初始生时，皆有鬼神随逐拥护；若其死时，彼守护鬼摄其精气，其人则死。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "If non-Buddhist brāhmaṇas ask: 'Virtuous ones! When all men and women are first born, there are spirits that follow and protect them. When they are about to die, those guardian spirits take away their vital energy, and the person dies. Why are some people afflicted by spirits, while others are not afflicted by spirits?' If asked this, you should answer them thus: 'Worldly people engage in unwholesome practices, have distorted views, and commit the ten unwholesome actions. Among such people, whether a hundred or a thousand, there is only one spirit that protects them. It is like a herd of cattle or sheep, whether a hundred or a thousand, that are guarded by one person. They are also like this, engaging in unwholesome practices, having distorted views, and committing the ten unwholesome actions. Among such people, whether a hundred or a thousand, there is only one spirit that protects them. If a person practices wholesome dharmas, has right views and faith, and possesses the ten wholesome actions, then that person is protected by a hundred thousand spirits. It is like a king or a king's minister, who is guarded by a hundred thousand people. They are also like this, practicing wholesome dharmas and possessing the ten wholesome actions. Then that person is protected by a hundred thousand spirits. For this reason, some people in the world are afflicted by spirits, while others are not afflicted by spirits.'"

佛告比丘：「设有外道梵志问言：『诸贤！若一切男女初始生时，皆有鬼神随逐守护；其欲死时，彼守护鬼神摄其精气，其人则死者。今人何故有为鬼神所触娆者？有不为鬼神所触娆者？』设有此问，汝等应答彼言：『世人为非法行，邪见颠倒，作十恶业，如是人辈，若百若千，乃至有一神护耳。譬如群牛、群羊，若百若千，一人守牧，彼亦如是，为非法行，邪见颠倒，作十恶业，如是人辈，若百若千，乃有一神护耳。若有人修行善法，见正信行，具十善业，如是一人有百千神护。譬如国王、国王大臣、有百千人卫护一人。彼亦如是，修行善法，具十善业，如是一人有百千神护。以是缘故，世人有为鬼神所触娆者，有不为鬼神所触娆者。』」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "The people of Jambudvīpa are superior to the people of Pūrvavideha in three ways. What are the three? First, they are vigorous and have strong memories, able to create karmic actions. Second, they are vigorous and have strong memories, diligently practicing the brahmacarya. Third, they are vigorous and have strong memories, with the Buddha appearing in their land. These three things make them superior to the people of Pūrvavideha. The people of Pūrvavideha are superior to the people of Jambudvīpa in three ways. What are the three? First, they have many cattle. Second, they have many sheep. Third, they have many pearls and jade. These three things make them superior to the people of Jambudvīpa. The people of Jambudvīpa are superior to the people of Avaragodānīya in three ways. What are the three? First, they are vigorous and have strong memories, able to create karmic actions. Second, they are vigorous and have strong memories, able to practice the brahmacarya. Third, they are vigorous and have strong memories, with the Buddha appearing in their land. These three things make them superior to the people of Avaragodānīya. The people of Avaragodānīya are superior to the people of Jambudvīpa in three ways. What are the three? First, their land is extremely vast. Second, their land is extremely large. Third, their land is extremely wonderful. These three things make them superior to the people of Jambudvīpa.

佛告比丘：「阎浮提人有三事胜拘耶尼人。何等为三？一者勇猛强记，能造业行。二者勇猛强记，勤修梵行。三者勇猛强记，佛出其土。以此三事胜拘耶尼。拘耶尼人有三事胜阎浮提。何等为三？一者多牛，二者多羊，三者多珠玉。以此三事胜阎浮提。阎浮提有三事胜弗于逮。何等为三？一者勇猛强记，能造业行。二者勇猛强记，能修梵行。三者勇猛强记，佛出其土。以此三事胜弗于逮。弗于逮有三事胜阎浮提，何等为三？一者其土极广，二者其土极大，三者其土极妙。以此三事胜阎浮提。

The people of Jambudvīpa are superior to the people of Uttarakuru in three ways. What are the three? First, they are vigorous and have strong memories, able to create karmic actions. Second, they are vigorous and have strong memories, able to practice the brahmacarya. Third, they are vigorous and have strong memories, with the Buddha appearing in their land. These three things make them superior to the people of Uttarakuru. The people of Uttarakuru are superior to the people of Jambudvīpa in three ways. What are the three? First, they are not subject to anything. Second, they have no self. Third, their lifespan is fixed at one thousand years. These three things make them superior to the people of Jambudvīpa. The people of Jambudvīpa are also superior to the hungry ghosts in three ways. What are the three? First, they have long lifespans. Second, their bodies are large. Third, they enjoy the fruits of others' actions. These three things make them superior to the people of Jambudvīpa. The people of Jambudvīpa are also superior to the dragons and garuḍas in three ways. The dragons and garuḍas are also superior to the people of Jambudvīpa in three ways. What are the three? First, they have long lifespans. Second, their bodies are large. Third, they have palaces. These three things make them superior to the people of Jambudvīpa.

「阎浮提有三事胜欝单曰。何等为三？一者勇猛强记，能造业行。二者勇猛强记，能修梵行。三者勇猛强记，佛出其土。以此三事胜欝单曰。欝单曰复有三事胜阎浮提。何等为三？一者无所系属，二者无有我，三者寿定千岁。以此三事胜阎浮提。阎浮提人亦以上三事胜饿鬼趣。饿鬼趣有三事胜阎浮提。何等为三？一者长寿，二者身大，三者他作自受。以此三事胜阎浮提。阎浮提人亦以上三事胜龙、金翅鸟。龙、金翅鸟复有三事胜阎浮提。何等为三？一者长寿，二者身大，三者宫殿。以此三事胜阎浮提。

"The people of Jambudvīpa are superior to the asuras in three ways. What are the three? First, their palaces are tall and wide. Second, their palaces are adorned. Third, their palaces are pure. These three things make them superior to the people of Jambudvīpa. The people of Jambudvīpa are also superior to the Four Heavenly Kings in three ways. What are the three? First, they have long lifespans. Second, they are handsome. Third, they have much happiness. These three things make them superior to the people of Jambudvīpa. The people of Jambudvīpa are also superior to the Trāyastriṃśa Heaven, the Yāma Heaven, the Tuṣita Heaven, the Nirmāṇarati Heaven, and the Paranirmitavaśavartin Heaven in three ways. What are the three? First, they have long lifespans. Second, they are handsome. Third, they have much happiness."

「阎浮提以上三事胜阿须伦。阿须伦复有三事胜阎浮提。何等为三？一者宫殿高广，二者宫殿庄严，三者宫殿清净。以此三事胜阎浮提。阎浮提人以此三事胜四天王。四天王复有三事胜阎浮提。何等为三？一者长寿，二者端正，三者多乐。以此三事胜阎浮提。阎浮提人亦以上三事胜忉利天、焰摩天、兜率天、化自在天、他化自在天。此诸天复有三事胜阎浮提。何等为三？一者长寿，二者端正，三者多乐。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "The sentient beings in the desire realm are of twelve kinds. What are the twelve? First, hell beings, second, animals, third, hungry ghosts, fourth, humans, fifth, asuras, sixth, the Four Heavenly Kings, seventh, the Trāyastriṃśa Heaven, eighth, the Yāma Heaven, ninth, the Tuṣita Heaven, tenth, the Nirmāṇarati Heaven, eleventh, the Paranirmitavaśavartin Heaven, twelfth, the Māra Heaven. The sentient beings in the form realm are of twenty-two kinds: first, the Brahmakāyika Heaven, second, the Brahmapurohita Heaven, third, the Brahmapārṣadya Heaven, fourth, the Mahābrahmā Heaven, fifth, the Ābhāsvara Heaven, sixth, the Parīttābhā Heaven, seventh, the Apramāṇābhā Heaven, eighth, the Ābhāsvarā Heaven, ninth, the Śubhakṛtsna Heaven, tenth, the Parīttaśubha Heaven, eleventh, the Apramāṇaśubha Heaven, twelfth, the Śubhakṛtsna Heaven, thirteenth, the Bṛhatphala Heaven, fourteenth, the Parīttaśubha Heaven, fifteenth, the Apramāṇaśubha Heaven, sixteenth, the Śubhakṛtsna Heaven, seventeenth, the Asaṃjñisattva Heaven, eighteenth, the Naivasaṃjñānāsaṃjñāyatana Heaven, nineteenth, the Avṛha Heaven, twentieth, the Sudṛśa Heaven, twenty-first, the Sudarśana Heaven, twenty-second, the Akaniṣṭha Heaven. The sentient beings in the formless realm are of four kinds. What are the four? First, the Ākāśānantyāyatana Heaven, second, the Vijñānānantyāyatana Heaven, third, the Ākiñcanyāyatana Heaven, fourth, the Naivasaṃjñānāsaṃjñāyatana Heaven."

佛告比丘：「欲界众生有十二种。何等为十二？一者地狱，二者畜生，三者饿鬼，四者人，五者阿须伦，六者四天王，七者忉利天，八者焰摩天，九者兜率天，十者化自在天，十一者他化自在天，十二者魔天。色界众生有二十二种：一者梵身天，二者梵辅天，三者梵众天，四者大梵天，五者光天，六者少光天，七者无量光天，八者光音天，九者净天，十者少净天，十一者无量净天，十二者遍净天，十三者严饰天，十四者小严饰天，十五者无量严饰天，十六者严饰果实天，十七者无想天，十八者无造天，十九者无热天，二十者善见天，二十一者大善见天，二十二者阿迦尼咤天。无色界众生有四种。何等为四？一者空智天，二者识智天，三者无所有智天，四者有想无想智天。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "There are four great divine beings. What are the four? First, the earth spirit, second, the water spirit, third, the wind spirit, fourth, the fire spirit. Once, the earth spirit gave rise to a wrong view, saying, 'There is no water, fire, or wind in the earth.' At that time, I knew what the earth spirit was thinking, and I went to him and said, 'Are you thinking that there is no water, fire, or wind in the earth?' The earth spirit replied, 'There really is no water, fire, or wind in the earth.' I then said to him, 'Do not give rise to this thought that there is no water, fire, or wind in the earth. Why is that? There is water, fire, and wind in the earth, but because the earth element is predominant, the earth element is given the name.'"

佛告比丘：「有四大天神。何等为四？一者地神，二者水神，三者风神，四者火神。昔者，地神生恶见言：『地中无水、火、风。』时，我知此地神所念，即往语言：『汝当生念言：「地中无水、火、风。」耶？』地神报言：『地中实无水、火、风也。』我时语言：『汝勿生此念，谓地中无水、火、风。所以者何？地中有水、火、风，但地大多故，地大得名。』」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "At that time, I expounded the Dharma for the earth spirit in sequence, removing his wrong views, teaching, benefiting, and delighting him, speaking about giving, precepts, and rebirth in heaven, showing that desire is impure, the upper defilements are afflictions, and liberation is supreme. I expounded and revealed pure and holy life. At that time, I knew that his mind was pure, pliant, joyful, without hindrances, and easy to be transformed. As is the constant practice of all Buddhas, I spoke about the noble truth of suffering, the noble truth of the origin of suffering, the noble truth of the cessation of suffering, and the noble truth of the path to the cessation of suffering, expounding and revealing them. At that time, the earth spirit immediately removed dust and defilements on the seat, and attained the purity of the Dharma eye. It is like a pure white cloth that is easy to accept colors. It was also like this. With pure faith, he attained the Dharma eye, without doubt, seeing the Dharma with certainty, not falling into evil destinies, not going to other paths, attaining fearlessness, and said to me, 'I now take refuge in the Buddha, take refuge in the Dharma, take refuge in the Sangha. For as long as I live, I will not kill, steal, engage in sexual misconduct, deceive, or drink alcohol. Please allow me to be a female lay devotee in the true Dharma.'"

佛告比丘：「我时为彼地神次第说法，除其恶见，示教利喜，施论、戒论、生天之论，欲为不净，上漏为患，出要为上；敷演开示，清净梵行。我时知其心净，柔软欢喜，无有阴盖，易可开化，如诸佛常法，说苦圣谛、苦集谛、苦灭谛、苦出要谛，演布开示。尔时，地神即于座上远尘离垢，得法眼净。譬如净洁白衣，易为受色。彼亦如是，信心清净，遂得法眼，无有狐疑，见法决定，不堕恶趣，不向余道，成就无畏，而白我言：『我今归依佛，归依法，归依僧，尽形寿不杀、不盗、不婬、不欺、不饮酒，听我于正法中为优婆夷。』」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "Once, the water spirit gave rise to a wrong view, saying, 'There is no earth, fire, or wind in water.' At that time, the earth spirit knew that the water spirit had given rise to this view, and went to tell the water spirit, 'Do you really give rise to this view, saying, "There is no earth, fire, or wind in water?"'" The water spirit replied, "Indeed." The earth spirit said, "Do not give rise to this view that there is no earth, fire, or wind in water. Why is that? There is earth, fire, and wind in water, but because the water element is predominant, the water element is given the name.' At that time, the earth spirit expounded the Dharma for him, removing his wrong views, teaching, benefiting, and delighting him, speaking about giving, precepts, and rebirth in heaven, showing that desire is impure, the upper defilements are afflictions, and liberation is supreme. He expounded and revealed pure and holy life. At that time, the earth spirit knew that the water spirit's mind was pliant, joyful, with pure faith, without hindrances, and easy to be transformed. As is the constant practice of all Buddhas, he spoke about the noble truth of suffering, the noble truth of the origin of suffering, the noble truth of the cessation of suffering, and the noble truth of the path to the cessation of suffering, expounding and revealing them. At that time, the water spirit immediately removed dust and defilements, and attained the purity of the Dharma eye. It is like a pure white cloth that is easy to accept colors. It was also like this. With pure faith, he attained the purity of the Dharma eye, without doubt, attaining the fruit with certainty, not falling into evil destinies, not going to other paths, attaining fearlessness, and said to the earth spirit, 'I now take refuge in the Buddha, take refuge in the Dharma, take refuge in the Sangha. For as long as I live, I will not kill, steal, engage in sexual misconduct, deceive, or drink alcohol. Please allow me to be a female lay devotee in the true Dharma.'"

佛告比丘：「昔者，水神生恶见言：『水中无地、火、风。』时，地神知彼水神心生此见，往语水神言：『汝实起此见，言：「水中无地、火、风。」耶？』答曰：『实尔。』地神语言：『汝勿起此见，谓水中无地、火、风。所以者何？水中有地、火、风，但水大多故，水大得名。』时，地神即为说法，除其恶见，示教利喜，施论、戒论、生天之论，欲为不净，上漏为患，出要为上；敷演开示，清净梵行。时，地神知彼水神其心柔软，欢喜信解，净无阴盖，易可开化，如诸佛常法，说苦圣谛、苦集谛、苦灭谛、苦出要谛，演布开示。时，彼水神即远尘离垢，得法眼净。犹如净洁白衣，易为受色。彼亦如是，信心清净，得法眼净，无有狐疑，决定得果，不堕恶趣，不向余道，成就无畏，白地神言：『我今归依佛，归依法，归依僧，尽形寿不杀、不盗、不婬、不欺、不饮酒，听我于正法中为优婆夷。』」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "Once, the fire spirit gave rise to a wrong view, saying, 'There is no earth, water, or wind in fire.' At that time, the earth spirit and water spirit knew that the fire spirit had given rise to this view, and together they said to the fire spirit, 'Do you really give rise to this view?' The fire spirit replied, 'Indeed.' The two spirits said, 'Do not give rise to this view. Why is that? There is earth, water, and wind in fire, but because the fire element is predominant, the fire element is given the name.' At that time, the two spirits expounded the Dharma for him, removing his wrong views, teaching, benefiting, and delighting him, speaking about giving, precepts, and rebirth in heaven, showing that desire is impure, the upper defilements are afflictions, and liberation is supreme. They expounded and revealed pure and holy life. The two spirits knew that the fire spirit's mind was pliant, joyful, with pure faith, without hindrances, and easy to be transformed. As is the constant practice of all Buddhas, they spoke about the noble truth of suffering, the noble truth of the origin of suffering, the noble truth of the cessation of suffering, and the noble truth of the path to the cessation of suffering, expounding and revealing them. At that time, the fire spirit immediately removed dust and defilements, and attained the purity of the Dharma eye. It is like a pure white cloth that is easy to accept colors. It was also like this. With pure faith, he attained the purity of the Dharma eye, without doubt, attaining the fruit with certainty, not falling into evil destinies, not going to other paths, attaining fearlessness, and said to the two spirits, 'I now take refuge in the Buddha, Dharma, and the noble Sangha. For as long as I live, I will not kill, steal, engage in sexual misconduct, deceive, or drink alcohol. Please allow me to be a female lay devotee in the true Dharma.'"

佛告比丘：「昔者，火神生恶见言：『火中无地、水、风。』时，地神、水神知彼火神心生此见，共语火神言：『汝实起此见耶？』答曰：『实尔。』二神语言：『汝勿起此见。所以者何？火中有地、水、风，但火大多故，火大得名耳。』时，二神即为说法，除其恶见，示教利喜，施论、戒论、生天之论，欲为不净，上漏为患，出要为上；敷演开示，清净梵行。二神知彼火神其心柔软，欢喜信解，净无阴盖，易可开化，如诸佛常法，说苦圣谛、苦集谛、苦灭谛、苦出要谛，演布开示。时，彼火神即远尘离垢，得法眼净。犹如净洁白衣，易为受色。彼亦如是，信心清净，遂得法眼，无有狐疑，决定得果，不堕恶趣，不向余道，成就无畏，白二神言：『我今归依佛、法、圣众，尽形寿不杀、不盗、不婬、不欺、不饮酒，听我于正法中为优婆夷。』」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "Once, the wind spirit gave rise to a wrong view, saying, 'There is no earth, water, or fire in wind.' The earth, water, and fire spirits knew that the wind spirit had given rise to this wrong view, and went to tell him, 'Do you really give rise to this view?' The wind spirit replied, 'Indeed.' The three spirits said, 'Do not give rise to this view. Why is that? There is earth, water, and fire in wind, but because the wind element is predominant, the wind element is given the name.' At that time, the three spirits expounded the Dharma for him, removing his wrong views, teaching, benefiting, and delighting him, speaking about giving, precepts, and rebirth in heaven, showing that desire is impure, the upper defilements are afflictions, and liberation is supreme. They expounded and revealed pure and holy life. The three spirits knew that the wind spirit's mind was pliant, joyful, with pure faith, without hindrances, and easy to be transformed. As is the constant practice of all Buddhas, they spoke about the noble truth of suffering, the noble truth of the origin of suffering, the noble truth of the cessation of suffering, and the noble truth of the path to the cessation of suffering, expounding and revealing them. At that time, the wind spirit immediately removed dust and defilements, and attained the purity of the Dharma eye. It is like a pure white cloth that is easy to accept colors. It was also like this. With pure faith, he attained the purity of the Dharma eye, without doubt, attaining the fruit with certainty, not falling into evil destinies, not going to other paths, attaining fearlessness, and said to the three spirits, 'I now take refuge in the Buddha, Dharma, and the noble Sangha. For as long as I live, I will not kill, steal, engage in sexual misconduct, deceive, or drink alcohol. Please allow me to be a female lay devotee in the true Dharma. With a compassionate mind towards all, I will not harm any sentient beings.'"

佛告比丘：「昔者，风神生恶见言：『风中无地、水、火。』地、水、火神知彼风神生此恶见，往语之言：『汝实起此见耶？』答曰：『实尔。』三神语言：『汝勿起此见。所以者何？风中有地、水、火，但风大多故，风大得名耳。』时，三神即为说法，除其恶见，示教利喜，施论、戒论、生天之论，欲为不净，上漏为患，出要为上；敷演开示，清净梵行。三神知彼风神其心柔软，欢喜信解，净无阴盖，易可开化，如诸佛常法，说苦圣谛、苦集、苦灭、苦出要谛，演布开示。时，彼风神即远尘离垢，得法眼净。譬如净洁白衣，易为受色。彼亦如是，信心清净，逮得法眼，无有狐疑，决定得果，不堕恶趣，不向余道，成就无畏，白三神言：『我今归依佛、法、圣众，尽形寿不杀、不盗、不婬、不欺、不饮酒，愿听我于正法中为优婆夷，慈心一切，不娆众生。』」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "There are four kinds of clouds. What are the four? First, white, second, black, third, red, and fourth, pink. The white ones are mostly earth, the black ones are mostly water, the red ones are mostly fire, and the pink ones are mostly wind. The clouds are ten, twenty, thirty, up to forty-four thousand yojanas above the ground, except at the beginning and end of the eon when the clouds reach the Heaven of Light Sound. There are four kinds of lightning. What are the four? The lightning in the east is called Body Light, the lightning in the south is called Difficult to Destroy, the lightning in the west is called Flowing Flame, and the lightning in the north is called Certain Brightness. For what reason is there lightning in the clouds in the sky? Sometimes Body Light touches Difficult to Destroy, sometimes Body Light touches Flowing Flame, sometimes Body Light touches Certain Brightness, sometimes Difficult to Destroy touches Flowing Flame, sometimes Difficult to Destroy touches Certain Brightness, sometimes Flowing Flame touches Certain Brightness. For this reason, there is lightning in the clouds in the sky. For what reason is there thunder in the clouds in the sky? Sometimes in the sky, earth and water touch, sometimes earth and fire touch, sometimes earth and wind touch, sometimes water and fire touch, sometimes water and wind touch. For this reason, there is thunder in the clouds in the sky.

佛告比丘：「云有四种。云何为四？一者白色，二者黑色，三者赤色。四者红色。其白色者地大偏多，其黑色者水大偏多，其赤色者火大偏多，其红色者风大偏多。其云去地或十里、二十里、三十里，至四十四千里，除劫初后时云上至光音天。电有四种。云何为四？东方电名身光，南方电名难毁，西方电名流炎，北方电名定明。以何缘故，虚空云中有此电光？有时身光与难毁相触，有时身光与流炎相触，有时身光与定明相触，有时难毁与流炎相触，有时难毁与定明相触，有时流炎与定明相触。以是缘故，虚空云中有电光起。复有何缘，虚空云有雷声起？虚空中有时地大与水大相触，有时地大与火大相触，有时地大与风大相触，有时水大与火大相触，有时水大与风大相触。以是缘故，虚空云中有雷声起。

There are five causes and conditions for which astrologers cannot determine rain, causing them to be confused. What are the five? First, clouds have thunder and lightning, and astrologers predict rain, but because fire is predominant, it burns the clouds and does not rain. This is the first cause of confusion for astrologers. Second, clouds have thunder and lightning, and astrologers predict rain, but a strong wind blows the clouds away and scatters them into the mountains. For this reason, astrologers are confused. Third, clouds have thunder and lightning, and astrologers predict rain, but the great asuras catch the floating clouds and place them in the great ocean. For this reason, astrologers are confused. Fourth, clouds have thunder and lightning, and astrologers predict rain, but the cloud masters and rain masters are negligent and indulge in sexual misconduct, and it does not rain. For this reason, astrologers are confused. Fifth, clouds have thunder and lightning, and astrologers predict rain, but the people of the world are negligent in the Dharma, engage in impure conduct, are stingy, jealous, and have inverted views, and therefore the heavens do not send rain. For this reason, astrologers are confused. These are the five causes and conditions for which astrologers cannot determine rain.

「相师占雨有五因缘不可定知，使占者迷惑。云何为五？一者云有雷电，占谓当雨，以火大多故，烧云不雨，是为占师初迷惑缘。二者云有雷电，占谓当雨，有大风起，吹云四散，入诸山间，以此缘故，相师迷惑。三者云有雷电，占谓当雨，时，大阿须伦接揽浮云，置大海中，以此因缘，相师迷惑。四者云有雷电，占谓当雨，而云师、雨师放逸婬乱，竟不降雨，以此因缘，相师迷惑。五者云有雷电，占谓当雨，而世间众庶非法放逸，行不净行，悭贪嫉妬，所见颠倒，故使天不降雨，以此因缘，相师迷惑。是为五因缘，相师占雨不可定知。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "There are four things that last for a long time, are immeasurable and limitless, and cannot be measured by the number of days, months, and years. What are the four? First, when the world gradually arises and is destroyed, the time in between is long and far, immeasurable and limitless, and cannot be measured by the number of days, months, and years. Second, after this world is destroyed, the time in between when it is empty and desolate, without a world, is long and far, and cannot be measured by the number of days, months, and years. Third, when the heavens and earth first arise and are about to form, the time in between is long, and cannot be measured by the number of days, months, and years. Fourth, after the heavens and earth are formed, they last for a long time without being destroyed, and cannot be measured by the number of days, months, and years. These are the four things that last for a long time, are immeasurable and limitless, and cannot be measured by the number of days, months, and years.

佛告比丘：「有四事长久，无量无限，不可以日月岁数而称计也。云何为四？一者世间灾渐起，坏此世时，中间长久，无量无限，不可以日月岁数而称计也。二者此世间坏已，中间空旷，无有世间，长久逈远，不可以日月岁数而称计也。三者天地初起，向欲成时，中间长久，不可以日月岁数而称计也。四者天地成已，久住不坏，不可以日月岁数而称计也。是为四事长久，无量无限，不可以日月岁数而计量也。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "There are three disasters in the world. What are the three? First, the fire disaster, second, the water disaster, and third, the wind disaster. There are three upper limits to these three disasters. What are the three? First, the Ābhāsvara Heaven, second, the Śubhakṛtsna Heaven, and third, the Bṛhatphala Heaven. When the fire disaster begins, it reaches the Ābhāsvara Heaven, which is the limit. When the water disaster begins, it reaches the Śubhakṛtsna Heaven, which is the limit. When the wind disaster begins, it reaches the Bṛhatphala Heaven, which is the limit. What is the fire disaster? When the fire disaster is about to begin, the people of this world all practice the right Dharma, have right views that are not inverted, and cultivate the ten wholesome practices. When practicing this Dharma, there are those who attain the second dhyāna and immediately leap up into the sky, abiding in the path of the sages, the path of the gods, and the path of the Brahmas, loudly proclaiming, 'Virtuous ones! You should know that the bliss of the second dhyāna without perception and without contemplation is bliss.' At that time, the people of the world, having heard this voice, look up and say to them, 'Excellent! Excellent! Please teach us the path of the second dhyāna without perception and without contemplation.' At that time, the people in the sky, having heard their words, immediately teach them the path of the second dhyāna without perception and without contemplation. Having heard their teaching, the people of this world then cultivate the path of the second dhyāna without perception and without contemplation. When their bodies perish and their lives end, they are reborn in the Ābhāsvara Heaven.

佛告比丘：「世有三灾。云何为三？一者火灾，二者水灾，三者风灾。有三灾上际。云何为三？一者光音天，二者遍净天，三者果实天。若火灾起时，至光音天，光音天为际。若水灾起时，至遍净天，遍净天为际。若风灾起时，至果实天，果实天为际。云何为火灾？火灾始欲起时，此世间人皆行正法，正见不倒，修十善行，行此法时，有人得第二禅者，即踊身上升于虚空中，住圣人道、天道、梵道，高声唱言：『诸贤！当知无觉、无观第二禅乐，第二禅乐。』时，世间人闻此声已，仰语彼言：『善哉！善哉！唯愿为我说无觉、无观第二禅道。』时，空中人闻其语已，即为说无觉、无观第二禅道。此世间人闻彼说已，即修无觉无观第二禅道，身坏命终，生光音天。

"At that time, the sentient beings in hell, having completed their karmic retribution, their lives ended, and they were reborn in the human realm. They again cultivated the second dhyāna without perception and without contemplation. When their bodies perished and their lives ended, they were reborn in the Ābhāsvara Heaven. The sentient beings in the animal realm, the hungry ghost realm, the asura realm, the four heavenly kings, the Trāyastriṃśa Heaven, the Yama Heaven, the Tuṣita Heaven, the Nirmāṇarati Heaven, the Paranirmitavaśavartin Heaven, and the Brahmā Heaven, their lives ended, were reborn in the human realm. They cultivated the second dhyāna without perception and without contemplation. When their bodies perished and their lives ended, they were reborn in the Ābhāsvara Heaven. Due to this cause and condition, the path of hell was exhausted, and the animal realm, the hungry ghost realm, the asura realm, up to the Brahmā Heaven were all exhausted. At that time, the hell realm was exhausted first, then the animal realm was exhausted; after the animal realm was exhausted, the hungry ghost realm was exhausted; after the hungry ghost realm was exhausted, the asura realm was exhausted; after the asura realm was exhausted, the four heavenly kings were exhausted; after the four heavenly kings were exhausted, the Trāyastriṃśa Heaven was exhausted; after the Trāyastriṃśa Heaven was exhausted, the Yama Heaven was exhausted; after the Yama Heaven was exhausted, the Tuṣita Heaven was exhausted; after the Tuṣita Heaven was exhausted, the Nirmāṇarati Heaven was exhausted; after the Nirmāṇarati Heaven was exhausted, the Paranirmitavaśavartin Heaven was exhausted; after the Paranirmitavaśavartin Heaven was exhausted, the Brahmā Heaven was exhausted; after the Brahmā Heaven was exhausted, then the human realm was exhausted, without any remainder. After the human realm was exhausted without remainder, this world was destroyed and became a disaster. After that, the heavens did not rain, and the hundred grains, grasses, and trees naturally withered and died."

「是时，地狱众生罪毕命终，来生人间，复修无觉、无观第二禅，身坏命终，生光音天；畜生、饿鬼、阿须伦、四天王、忉利天、炎天、兜率天、化自在天、他化自在天、梵天众生命终，来生人间，修无觉、无观第二禅，身坏命终，生光音天。由此因缘地狱道尽，畜生、饿鬼、阿须伦乃至梵天皆尽。当于尔时，先地狱尽，然后畜生尽；畜生尽已，饿鬼尽；饿鬼尽已，阿须伦尽；阿须伦尽已，四天王尽；四天王尽已，忉利天王尽；忉利天王尽已，炎摩天尽；炎摩天尽已，兜率天尽；兜率天尽已，化自在天尽；化自在天尽已，他化自在天尽；他化自在天尽已，梵天尽；梵天尽已，然后人尽，无有遗余。人尽无余已，此世败坏，乃成为灾，其后天不降雨，百谷草木自然枯死。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "You should know that all conditioned phenomena are impermanent, subject to change, decay, and destruction. They cannot be relied upon. The conditioned phenomena of the world are very much to be abhorred. One should seek the path of liberation that transcends the world. After a long time, a great black wind suddenly arose, blowing the great ocean, which was eight thousand four hundred yojanas deep, apart into two parts, and taking the sun's palace and placing it on the side of Mount Sumeru, forty-two thousand yojanas above the ground, in the sun's path. Because of this, there were two suns in the world. When there were two suns in the world, it caused all the small rivers, streams, and canals in the world to dry up."

佛告比丘：「以是当知，一切行无常，变易朽坏，不可恃怙，有为诸法，甚可厌患，当求度世解脱之道。其后久久，有大黑风暴起，吹大海水，海水深八万四千由旬，吹使两披，取日宫殿，置于须弥山半，去地四万二千由旬，安日道中，缘此世间有二日出。二日出已，令此世间所有小河、汱浍、渠流皆悉干竭。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "You should know that all conditioned phenomena are impermanent, subject to change, decay, and destruction. They cannot be relied upon. The conditioned phenomena of the world are very much to be abhorred. One should seek the path of liberation that transcends the world. Because of this, there were three suns in the world. When there were three suns in the world, it caused all the great waters in the world, such as the Ganges River, the Yavana River, the Vārāṇasī River, the Airavati River, the Aśvakarṇī River, the Sindhu River, and the Kṛṣṇā River, to dry up without any remainder.

佛告比丘：「以是当知，一切行无常，变易朽坏，不可恃怙，凡诸有为甚可厌患，当求度世解脱之道。其后久久，有大黑风暴起，海水深八万四千由旬，吹使两披，取日宫殿，置于须弥山半，去地四万二千由旬，安日道中，缘此世间有三日出。三日出已，此诸大水，恒河、耶婆那河、婆罗河、阿夷罗婆提河、阿摩怯河、辛陀河、故舍河皆悉干竭，无有遗余。

You should know that all conditioned phenomena are impermanent, subject to change, decay, and destruction. They cannot be relied upon.
