After a long time, a great black wind suddenly arose, blowing the great ocean, which was eight thousand four hundred yojanas deep, apart into two parts, and taking the sun's palace and placing it on the side of Mount Sumeru, in the sun's path. Because of this, there were four suns in the world. When there were four suns in the world, it caused all the springs, ponds, and lakes in the world, such as the Sudarśana Lake, the Anavatapta Lake, the Catuṣpādikā Lake, the Utpala Lake, the Kumuda Lake, the Puṇḍarīka Lake, and the Avirāma Lake, which were fifty yojanas long and wide, to dry up completely.

「以是当知，一切行无常，变易朽坏，不可恃怙，凡诸有为甚可厌患，当求度世解脱之道。其后久久，有大黑风暴起，海水深八万四千由旬，吹使两披，取日宫殿，置于须弥山半，安日道中，缘此世间有四日出。四日出已，此诸世间所有泉源、渊池，善见大池、阿耨大池、四方陀延池、优钵罗池、拘物头池、分陀利池、离池，纵广五十由旬皆尽干竭。

You should know that all conditioned phenomena are impermanent, subject to change, decay, and destruction. They cannot be relied upon. The conditioned phenomena of the world are very much to be abhorred. One should seek the path of liberation that transcends the world. After a long time, a great black wind suddenly arose, blowing the great ocean, which was eight thousand four hundred yojanas deep, apart into two parts, and taking the sun's palace and placing it on the side of Mount Sumeru, in the sun's path. Because of this, there were five suns in the world. When there were five suns in the world, it caused the great ocean to gradually decrease by one hundred yojanas, down to seven hundred yojanas. Because of this, one should know that all conditioned phenomena are impermanent, subject to change, decay, and destruction. They cannot be relied upon. The conditioned phenomena of the world are very much to be abhorred. One should seek the path of liberation that transcends the world. At that time, the great ocean gradually decreased, leaving seven hundred yojanas, six hundred yojanas, five hundred yojanas, four hundred yojanas, down to one hundred yojanas remaining. Because of this, one should know that all conditioned phenomena are impermanent, subject to change, decay, and destruction. They cannot be relied upon. The conditioned phenomena of the world are very much to be abhorred. One should seek the path of liberation that transcends the world. At that time, the great ocean gradually decreased, down to seven yojanas, six yojanas, five yojanas, down to one yojana remaining.

「以是故知，一切无常，变易朽坏，不可恃怙，凡诸有为甚可厌患，当求度世解脱之道。其后久久，有大黑风暴起，吹大海水，使令两披，取日宫殿，置于须弥山半，安日道中，缘此世间有五日出。五日出已，大海水稍减百由旬，至七百由旬。以是可知，一切行无常，变易朽坏，不可恃怙，凡诸有为甚可厌患，当求度世解脱之道。是时，大海稍尽，余有七百由旬、六百由旬、五百由旬、四百由旬乃至百由旬在。以是可知，一切行无常，变易朽坏，不可恃怙，凡诸有为甚可厌患，当求度世解脱之道。时，大海水稍稍减尽，至七由旬、六由旬、五由旬，乃至一由旬在。」

佛告比丘：「是故当知，一切行无常，变易朽坏，不可恃怙，凡诸有为法甚可厌患，当求度世解脱之道。此四天下，乃至梵天火洞然已，风吹火焰至光音天，其彼初生天子见此火焰，皆生怖畏言：『咄！此何物？』先生诸天语后生天言：『勿怖畏也，彼火曾来，齐此而止。』以念前火光，故名光念天。此四天下，乃至梵天火洞然已，须弥山王渐渐颓落，百由旬、二百由旬，至七百由旬。」

The conditioned phenomena of the world are very much to be abhorred. One should seek the path of liberation that transcends the world. After a long time, the great ocean gradually decreased, leaving seven hundred yojanas, six hundred yojanas, five hundred yojanas, four hundred yojanas, down to one hundred yojanas remaining. Because of this, one should know that all conditioned phenomena are impermanent, subject to change, decay, and destruction. They cannot be relied upon. The conditioned phenomena of the world are very much to be abhorred. One should seek the path of liberation that transcends the world. At that time, the great ocean gradually decreased, down to seven yojanas, six yojanas, five yojanas, down to one yojana remaining. The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "

「以何因缘有须弥山？有乱风起，吹此水沫造须弥山，高六十万八千由旬，纵广八万四千由旬，四宝所成，金、银、水精、琉璃。以何因缘有四阿须伦宫殿？其后乱风吹大海水吹大水沫，于须弥山四面起大宫殿，纵广各八万由旬，自然变成七宝宫殿。复何因缘有四天王宫殿？其后乱风吹大海水沫，于须弥山半四万二千由旬，自然变成七宝宫殿，以是故名为四天王宫殿。以何因缘有忉利天宫殿？其后乱风吹大水沫，于须弥山上自然变成七宝宫殿。

"You should know that all conditioned phenomena are impermanent, subject to change, decay, and destruction. They cannot be relied upon. The conditioned phenomena of the world are very much to be abhorred. One should seek the path of liberation that transcends the world. After a long time, the great ocean gradually decreased, leaving seven hundred yojanas, six hundred yojanas, five hundred yojanas, four hundred yojanas, down to one hundred yojanas remaining. Because of this, one should know that all conditioned phenomena are impermanent, subject to change, decay, and destruction. They cannot be relied upon. The conditioned phenomena of the world are very much to be abhorred. One should seek the path of liberation that transcends the world. At that time, the great ocean gradually decreased, down to seven yojanas, six yojanas, five yojanas, down to one yojana remaining. The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "

「复以何缘有伽陀罗山？其后乱风吹大水沫，去须弥山不远，自然化成宝山，下根入地四万二千由旬，纵广四万二千由旬，其边无际，杂色间厕，七宝所成，以是缘故有伽陀罗山。复以何缘有伊沙山？其后乱风吹大水沫，去伽陀罗山不远，自然变成伊沙山，高二万一千由旬，纵广二万一千由旬，其边无际，杂色参间，七宝所成，以是缘故有伊沙山。其后乱风吹大水沫，去伊沙山不远，自然变成树辰陀罗山，高万二千由旬，纵广万二千由旬，其边无际，杂色参间，七宝所成，以是因缘有树辰陀罗山。其后乱风吹大水沫，去树辰陀罗山不远，自然变成阿般泥楼山，高六千由旬，纵广六千由旬，其边无际，杂色参间，七宝所成，以是缘故有阿般尼楼山。

"You should know that all conditioned phenomena are impermanent, subject to change, decay, and destruction. They cannot be relied upon. The conditioned phenomena of the world are very much to be abhorred. One should seek the path of liberation that transcends the world. After a long time, the great ocean gradually decreased, leaving seven hundred yojanas, six hundred yojanas, five hundred yojanas, four hundred yojanas, down to one hundred yojanas remaining. Because of this, one should know that all conditioned phenomena are impermanent, subject to change, decay, and destruction. They cannot be relied upon. The conditioned phenomena of the world are very much to be abhorred. One should seek the path of liberation that transcends the world. At that time, the great ocean gradually decreased, down to seven yojanas, six yojanas, five yojanas, down to one yojana remaining. The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "

「其后乱风吹大水沫，去阿般尼楼山不远，自然变成弥隣陀罗山，高三千由旬，纵广三千由旬，其边无际，杂色参间，七宝所成，以是因缘有尼隣陀罗山。其后乱风吹大水沫，去尼隣陀罗山不远，自然变成比尼陀山，高千二百由旬，纵广千二百由旬，其边无际，杂色参间，七宝所成，以是缘故有比尼陀山。其后乱风吹大水沫，去比尼陀山不远，自然变成金刚轮山，高三百由旬，纵广三百由旬，其边无际，杂色参间，七宝所成，以是因缘有金刚轮山。

"You should know that all conditioned phenomena are impermanent, subject to change, decay, and destruction. They cannot be relied upon. The conditioned phenomena of the world are very much to be abhorred. One should seek the path of liberation that transcends the world. After a long time, the great ocean gradually decreased, leaving seven hundred yojanas, six hundred yojanas, five hundred yojanas, four hundred yojanas, down to one hundred yojanas remaining. Because of this, one should know that all conditioned phenomena are impermanent, subject to change, decay, and destruction. They cannot be relied upon. The conditioned phenomena of the world are very much to be abhorred. One should seek the path of liberation that transcends the world. At that time, the great ocean gradually decreased, down to seven yojanas, six yojanas, five yojanas, down to one yojana remaining. The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "

「何故有月、有七日宫殿？其后乱风吹大水沫，自然变成一月宫殿、七日宫殿，杂色参间，七宝所成，为黑风所吹还到本处，以是因缘有日、月宫殿。

"You should know that all conditioned phenomena are impermanent, subject to change, decay, and destruction. They cannot be relied upon. The conditioned phenomena of the world are very much to be abhorred. One should seek the path of liberation that transcends the world. After a long time, the great ocean gradually decreased, leaving seven hundred yojanas, six hundred yojanas, five hundred yojanas, four hundred yojanas, down to one hundred yojanas remaining. Because of this, one should know that all conditioned phenomena are impermanent, subject to change, decay, and destruction. They cannot be relied upon. The conditioned phenomena of the world are very much to be abhorred. One should seek the path of liberation that transcends the world. At that time, the great ocean gradually decreased, down to seven yojanas, six yojanas, five yojanas, down to one yojana remaining. The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "

「其后乱风吹大水沫，自然变成四天下及八万天下，以是因缘有四天下及八万天下。其后乱风吹大水沫，在四天下及八万天下，自然变成大金刚轮山，高十六万八千由旬，纵广十六万八千由旬，其边无限，金刚坚固，不可毁坏，以是因缘有大金刚轮山。其后久久，有自然云遍满空中，周遍大雨，渧如车轮，其水弥漫，没四天下，与须弥山等，其后乱风吹地为大坑，涧水尽入中，因此为海，以是因缘有四大海水。海水咸苦有三因缘。何等为三？一者有自然云遍满虚空，至光音天，周遍降雨，洗濯天宫，涤荡天下，从梵迦夷天宫、他化自在天宫，下至炎摩天宫、四天下、八万天下、诸山、大山、须弥山王皆洗濯涤荡，其中诸处有秽恶咸苦诸不净汁，下流入海，合为一味，故海水咸。二者昔有大仙人禁呪海水，长使咸苦，人不得饮，是故咸苦。三者彼大海水杂众生居，其身长大，或百由旬、二百由旬，至七百由旬，呼哈吐纳，大小便中，故海水咸。是为火灾。」

"You should know that all conditioned phenomena are impermanent, subject to change, decay, and destruction. They cannot be relied upon. The conditioned phenomena of the world are very much to be abhorred. One should seek the path of liberation that transcends the world. After a long time, the great ocean gradually decreased, leaving seven hundred yojanas, six hundred yojanas, five hundred yojanas, four hundred yojanas, down to one hundred yojanas remaining. Because of this, one should know that all conditioned phenomena are impermanent, subject to change, decay, and destruction. They cannot be relied upon. The conditioned phenomena of the world are very much to be abhorred. One should seek the path of liberation that transcends the world. At that time, the great ocean gradually decreased, down to seven yojanas, six yojanas, five yojanas, down to one yojana remaining. The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "

佛告比丘：「云何为水灾？水灾起时，此世间人皆奉正法，正见，不邪见，修十善业，修善行已。时，有人得无喜第三禅者，踊身上升于虚空中，住圣人道、天道、梵道，高声唱言：『诸贤！当知无喜第三禅乐，无喜第三禅乐。』时，世间人闻此声已，仰语彼言：『善哉！善哉！愿为我说是无喜第三禅道。』时，空中人闻此语已，即为演说无喜第三禅道，此世间人闻其说已，即修第三禅道，身坏命终，生遍净天。

"You should know that all conditioned phenomena are impermanent, subject to change, decay, and destruction. They cannot be relied upon. The conditioned phenomena of the world are very much to be abhorred. One should seek the path of liberation that transcends the world. After a long time, the great ocean gradually decreased, leaving seven hundred yojanas, six hundred yojanas, five hundred yojanas, four hundred yojanas, down to one hundred yojanas remaining. Because of this, one should know that all conditioned phenomena are impermanent, subject to change, decay, and destruction. They cannot be relied upon. The conditioned phenomena of the world are very much to be abhorred. One should seek the path of liberation that transcends the world. At that time, the great ocean gradually decreased, down to seven yojanas, six yojanas, five yojanas, down to one yojana remaining. The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "

「尔时，地狱众生罪毕命终，来生人间，复修第三禅道，身坏命终，生遍净天；畜生、饿鬼、阿须轮、四天王、忉利天、炎摩天、兜率天、化自在天、他化自在天、梵天、光音天众生命终，来生人间，修第三禅道，身坏命终，生遍净天。由此因缘，地狱道尽，畜生、饿鬼、阿须伦、四天王，乃至光音天趣皆尽。当于尔时，先地狱尽，然后畜生尽；畜生尽已，饿鬼尽；饿鬼尽已，阿须伦尽；阿须伦尽已，四天王尽；四天王尽已，忉利天尽；忉利天尽已，炎摩天尽；炎摩天尽已，兜率天尽；兜率天尽已，化自在天尽；化自在天尽已，他化自在天尽；他化自在天尽已，梵天尽；梵天尽已，光音天尽；光音天尽已，然后人尽无余。人尽无余已，此世间败坏，乃成为灾。

"You should know that all conditioned phenomena are impermanent, subject to change, decay, and destruction. They cannot be relied upon. The conditioned phenomena of the world are very much to be abhorred. One should seek the path of liberation that transcends the world. After a long time, the great ocean gradually decreased, leaving seven hundred yojanas, six hundred yojanas, five hundred yojanas, four hundred yojanas, down to one hundred yojanas remaining. Because of this, one should know that all conditioned phenomena are impermanent, subject to change, decay, and destruction. They cannot be relied upon. The conditioned phenomena of the world are very much to be abhorred. One should seek the path of liberation that transcends the world. At that time, the great ocean gradually decreased, down to seven yojanas, six yojanas, five yojanas, down to one yojana remaining. The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "

「其后久久，有大黑云暴起，上至遍净天，周遍大雨，纯雨热水，其水沸涌，煎熬天上，诸天宫殿皆悉消尽，无有遗余。犹如酥油置于火中，煎熬消尽，无有遗余，光音天宫亦复如是。以此可知，一切行无常，为变易法，不可恃怙，有为诸法，甚可厌患，当求度世解脱之道。

"You should know that all conditioned phenomena are impermanent, subject to change, decay, and destruction. They cannot be relied upon. The conditioned phenomena of the world are very much to be abhorred. One should seek the path of liberation that transcends the world. After a long time, the great ocean gradually decreased, leaving seven hundred yojanas, six hundred yojanas, five hundred yojanas, four hundred yojanas, down to one hundred yojanas remaining. Because of this, one should know that all conditioned phenomena are impermanent, subject to change, decay, and destruction. They cannot be relied upon. The conditioned phenomena of the world are very much to be abhorred. One should seek the path of liberation that transcends the world. At that time, the great ocean gradually decreased, down to seven yojanas, six yojanas, five yojanas, down to one yojana remaining. The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "

「其后此雨复浸梵迦夷天宫，煎熬消尽，无有遗余。犹如酥油置于火中，无有遗余，梵迦夷宫亦复如是。其后此雨复浸他化自在天、化自在天、兜率天、炎摩天宫，煎熬消尽，无有遗余。犹如酥油置于火中，无有遗余，彼诸天宫亦复如是。其后此雨复浸四天下及八万天下诸山、大山、须弥山王，煎熬消尽，无有遗余。犹如酥油置于火中，煎熬消尽，无有遗余，彼亦如是。是故当知，一切行无常，为变易法，不可恃怙，凡诸有为甚可厌患，当求度世解脱之道。其后此水煎熬大地，尽无余已，地下水尽，水下风尽。是故当知，一切行无常，为变易法，不可恃怙，凡诸有为甚可厌患，当求度世解脱之道。」

"The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "The palace of the Heaven of Pure Abode was also boiled and dissolved, leaving nothing behind. Who would believe this? Only those who have seen it can know. The palace of the Heaven of Great Purity was also boiled and dissolved, down to the water below the earth being exhausted and the wind below the water being exhausted. Who would believe this? Only those who have seen it can know. This is called the water calamity.

佛告比丘：「遍净天宫煎熬消尽。谁当信者？独有见者，乃能知耳。梵迦夷宫煎熬消尽，乃至地下水尽，水下风尽。谁当信者？独有见者，乃当知耳。是为水灾。

"The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "How does the water calamity return to normal? After a long time, a great black cloud fills the sky and reaches the Heaven of Pure Abode, pouring rain all over, the drops like chariot wheels. For countless hundreds of thousands of years, the water gradually rises to the Heaven of Pure Abode. There are four great winds that hold this water in place. What are the four? One is called the wind of abiding, two is called the wind of holding, three is called immovable, and four is called firm. After that, the water gradually decreases by countless hundreds of thousands of yojanas. There are great winds blowing from the four directions, called Saṃgha, that blow the water, causing it to move and churn, forming waves and foam that accumulate. The wind blows them away from the water and they naturally transform into the palace of the Heaven of Light Sound in the sky, adorned with the seven treasures. For this reason, there is the palace of the Heaven of Light Sound. The water further decreases by countless hundreds of thousands of yojanas. The Saṃgha wind blows the water, causing it to move and churn, forming waves and foam that accumulate. The wind blows them away from the water and they naturally transform into the palace of the Heaven of Great Purity in the sky, adorned with the seven treasures. In this way, the seawater becomes of one taste, salty and bitter, just as in the fire calamity.

「云何水灾还复？其后久久，有大黑云充满虚空，至遍净天，周遍降雨，渧如车轮，如是无数百千万岁，其水渐长，至遍净天。有四大风，持此水住。何等为四？一名住风，二名持风，三名不动，四名坚固。其后此水稍减无数百千由旬，四面有大风起，名曰僧伽，吹水令动，鼓荡涛波，起沫积聚，风吹离水，在虚空中，自然变成光音天宫，七宝校饰，由此因缘有光音天宫。其水转减无数百千由旬，彼僧伽风吹水令动，鼓荡涛波，起沫积聚，风吹离水，在虚空中，自然变成梵迦夷天宫，七宝校饰；如是乃至海水一味咸苦，亦如火灾复时。是为水灾。」

"The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "What is the wind calamity? When the wind calamity arises, all the people in this world will follow the right Dharma, have right views, not wrong views, and practice the ten wholesome actions. When practicing wholesome conduct, there will be people who attain the fourth dhyāna of pure mindfulness and abide in the sky, practicing the path of the sages, the path of the gods, and the path of Brahmā. They will loudly proclaim, 'Virtuous ones! The fourth dhyāna of pure mindfulness is blissful, the fourth dhyāna of pure mindfulness is blissful.' At that time, the people in this world will hear their voices and say to them, 'Excellent! Excellent! Please teach us the path of the fourth dhyāna of pure mindfulness.' When the people in the sky hear these words, they will immediately teach the path of the fourth dhyāna. When the people in this world hear their teachings, they will practice the path of the fourth dhyāna. When their bodies perish and their lives end, they will be reborn in the Heaven of Realization.

佛告比丘：「云何为风灾？风灾起时，此世间人皆奉正法，正见，不邪见，修十善业，修善行时，时，有人得清净护念第四禅，于虚空中住圣人道、天道、梵道，高声唱言：『诸贤！护念清净第四禅乐，护念清净第四禅乐。』时，此世人闻其声已，仰语彼言：『善哉！善哉！愿为我说护念清净第四禅道。』时，空中人闻此语已，即为说第四禅道，此世间人闻其说已，即修第四禅道，身坏命终，生果实天。

At that time, the sentient beings in the hells, having completed their karmic retribution, will end their lives and be reborn among humans. They will again cultivate the fourth dhyāna, and when their bodies perish and their lives end, they will be reborn in the Heaven of Realization. The same will happen to the sentient beings in the animal realm, the hungry ghost realm, the asura realm, the four heavenly kings, and up to the Heaven of Pure Abode. Due to these causes and conditions, the path of the hells will be exhausted, and the paths of the animal realm, the hungry ghost realm, the asura realm, the four heavenly kings, and up to the Heaven of Pure Abode will all be exhausted. At that time, the hells will be exhausted first, then the animal realm will be exhausted; after the animal realm is exhausted, the hungry ghost realm will be exhausted; after the hungry ghost realm is exhausted, the asura realm will be exhausted; after the asura realm is exhausted, the four heavenly kings will be exhausted; after the four heavenly kings are exhausted, it will continue in this way up to the Heaven of Pure Abode being exhausted; after the Heaven of Pure Abode is exhausted, then the human realm will be exhausted without remainder. When the human realm is exhausted without remainder, this world will be destroyed and become a calamity. After a long time, a great wind will arise, called Mahāsattva, up to the Heaven of Realization. This wind will blow in the four directions, striking the palaces of the Heaven of Pure Abode and the Heaven of Light Sound, causing the palaces to collide and shatter into powder. It will be like a strong man holding two copper pestles, striking them together and shattering them into pieces without remainder. The collision of the two palaces will also be like this. From this, we should know that all conditioned phenomena are impermanent, subject to change, and cannot be relied upon. All conditioned phenomena are very much to be despised and abhorred. We should seek the path of liberation that transcends the world.

「尔时，地狱众生罪毕命终，来生人间，复修第四禅，身坏命终，生果实天；畜生、饿鬼、阿须伦、四天王乃至遍净天众生命终，来生人间，修第四禅，身坏命终，生果实天。由此因缘，地狱道尽，畜生、饿鬼、阿须伦、四天王，乃至遍净天趣皆尽。尔时，地狱先尽，然后畜生尽；畜生尽已，饿鬼尽；饿鬼尽已，阿须伦尽；阿须伦尽已，四天王尽；四天王尽已，如是展转至遍净天尽；遍净天尽已，然后人尽无余。人尽无余已，此世间败坏，乃成为灾。其后久久，有大风起，名曰大僧伽，乃至果实天，其风四布，吹遍净天宫、光音天宫，使宫宫相拍，碎若粉尘。犹如力士执二铜杵，杵杵相拍，碎尽无余，二宫相拍亦复如是。以是当知，一切行无常，为变易法，不可恃怙，凡诸有为甚可厌患，当求度世解脱之道。

After that, this wind will blow on the palaces of the Heaven of Free from Strife and the Heaven of Delighting in Emanations, causing the palaces to collide and shatter into powder, leaving nothing behind. It will be like a strong man holding two copper pestles, striking them together and shattering them into pieces without remainder. The collision of the two palaces will also be like this. From this, we should know that all conditioned phenomena are impermanent, subject to change, and cannot be relied upon. All conditioned phenomena are very much to be despised and abhorred. We should seek the path of liberation that transcends the world.

「其后此风吹梵迦夷天宫、他化自在天宫，宫宫相拍，碎如粉尘，无有遗余。犹如力士执二铜杵，杵杵相拍，碎尽无余，二宫相拍亦复如是。以是当知，一切行无常，为变易法，不可恃怙，凡诸有为甚可厌患，当求度世解脱之道。其后此风吹化自在天宫、兜率天宫、炎摩天宫，宫宫相拍，碎若粉尘，无有遗余。犹如力士执二铜杵，杵杵相拍，碎尽无余，彼宫如是碎尽无余。以是当知，一切行无常，为变易法，不可恃怙，凡诸有为甚可厌患，当求度世解脱之道。

After that, this wind will blow on the four continents and the eighty thousand continents, as well as the mountains, great mountains, and Mount Sumeru, lifting them into the sky to a height of a hundred thousand yojanas. The mountains will collide and shatter into powder. It will be like a strong man holding light chaff in his hand and scattering it into the air. The four continents, Mount Sumeru, and the other mountains will be shattered and dispersed in the same way. From this, we should know that all conditioned phenomena are impermanent, subject to change, and cannot be relied upon. All conditioned phenomena are very much to be despised and abhorred. We should seek the path of liberation that transcends the world.

「其后此风吹四天下及八万天下诸山、大山、须弥山王置于虚空，高百千由旬，山山相拍，碎若粉尘。犹如力士手执轻糠散于空中，彼四天下、须弥诸山碎尽分散，亦复如是。以是可知，一切行无常，为变易法，不可恃怙，凡诸有为甚可厌患，当求度世解脱之道。其后风吹大地尽，地下水尽，水下风尽。是故当知，一切行无常，为变易法，不可恃怙，凡诸有为甚可厌患，当求度世解脱之道。」

The Buddha told the monks, "The palaces of the Heaven of Pure Abode and the Heaven of Sound of Brahmā will collide and shatter into powder. Who can believe this? Only those who have seen it can know. In this way, even the water below the earth will be exhausted, and the wind below the water will be exhausted. Who can believe this? Only those who have seen it can believe it. This is called the wind disaster.

佛告比丘：「遍净天宫、光音天宫，宫宫相拍，碎若粉尘。谁当信者？独有见者，乃能知耳。如是乃至地下水尽，水下风尽。谁能信者？独有见者，乃能信耳。是为风灾。

"How does the wind disaster recover? After a long time, a great black cloud will cover the sky up to the Heaven of Fruitful Effects, and a heavy rain will fall, with drops as big as chariot wheels. The rain will continue for countless hundreds of thousands of years. The water will gradually rise to the Heaven of Fruitful Effects. At that time, there will be four winds holding the water in place. What are the four? The first is called the wind of abiding, the second is called the wind of holding, the third is called immovable, and the fourth is called firm. After that, the water will gradually decrease by countless hundreds of thousands of yojanas. On the four sides of the water, a great wind will arise, called saṃgha, blowing the water to move, churning up waves, and the foam will accumulate. The wind blows the foam away from the water and it naturally transforms into the palaces of the Heaven of Pure Abode in the sky, with various colors and seven treasures. For this reason, there are the palaces of the Heaven of Pure Abode. The water will further decrease by countless hundreds of thousands of yojanas. The saṃgha wind blows the water to move, churning up waves, and the foam will accumulate. The wind blows the foam away from the water and it naturally transforms into the palaces of the Heaven of Sound of Brahmā in the sky, with various colors and seven treasures. Up to the seawater having a single taste of salty bitterness, it is also like the recovery time of the fire disaster. This is called the wind disaster. These are the three disasters, and these are the three recoveries."

「云何风灾还复？其后久久，有大黑云周遍虚空，至果实天，而降大雨，渧如车轮，霖雨无数百千万岁，其水渐长，至果实天。时，有四风持此水住。何等为四？一名住风，二名持风，三名不动，四名坚固。其后此水渐渐稍减无数百千由旬，其水四面有大风起，名曰僧伽，吹水令动，鼓荡涛波，起沫积聚，风吹离水，在于空中自然变成遍净天宫，杂色参间，七宝所成，以此因缘有遍净天宫。其水转减无数百千由旬，彼僧伽风吹水令动，鼓荡涛波，起沫积聚，风吹离水，在于空中自然变成光音天宫，杂色参间，七宝所成；乃至海水一味咸苦，亦如火灾复时。是为风灾。是为三灾，是为三复。」

The Buddha told the monks, "In the past, the gods fought with the asuras. At that time, Śakra, lord of the devas, ordered the devas of the Trāyastriṃśa Heaven, saying, 'You should now go and fight with them. If you win, capture Vimalacitra, the asura, bind him with the five bonds, and bring him to the Sudharma Assembly Hall. I wish to see him.' At that time, the devas of the Trāyastriṃśa Heaven, having received Śakra's order, each adorned themselves. At that time, Vimalacitra, the asura, ordered the asuras, saying, 'You should now go and fight with them. If you win, capture Śakra, lord of the devas, bind him with the five bonds, and bring him to the Saptaparṇa Assembly Hall. I wish to see him.' At that time, the asuras, having received Vimalacitra's order, each adorned themselves.

佛告比丘：「昔者，诸天与阿须伦共鬪。时，释提桓因命忉利诸天而告之曰：『汝等今往与彼共战，若得胜者，捉毘摩质多罗阿须伦，以五系系缚，将诣善法讲堂，吾欲观之。』时，忉利诸天受帝释教已，各自庄严。时，毘摩质多罗阿须伦命诸阿须伦而告之曰：『汝等今往与彼共战，若得胜者，捉释提桓因，以五系系缚，将诣七叶讲堂，吾欲观之。』时，诸阿须伦受毘摩质多阿须伦教已，各自庄严。

Then the armies of the gods and asuras fought, and the gods won, while the asuras retreated. At that time, the devas of the Trāyastriṃśa Heaven captured the asura king, bound him with the five bonds, and brought him to the Sudharma Assembly Hall to show Śakra, lord of the devas. At that time, the asura king, seeing the heavenly pleasures, gave rise to a longing heart and thought to himself, 'This place is extraordinary. It is suitable to dwell in. Why return to the asura palace?' When he had this thought, the five bonds were immediately released, and the five pleasures were before him. If the asura gave rise to the thought of wanting to return to his original palace, the five bonds would bind him again, and the five pleasures would leave by themselves. At that time, the bonds that bound the asura became even tighter. The bonds of Māra are even more so. Those who calculate self, person, and Māra are bound by Māra. Those who do not calculate self, person, and Māra are released from Māra's bonds. Attachment to self is bondage, attachment to attachment is bondage, I will be bondage, I will not be bondage, form is bondage, formlessness is bondage, form and formlessness are bondage, I have perception is bondage, no perception is bondage, perception and no perception are bondage. I am a great affliction, a boil, a thorn. Therefore, the noble disciples know that I am a great affliction, a boil, a thorn, and abandon the thought of self. They cultivate the practice of no-self and observe that self is a heavy burden, a distraction, and an existence. The existence of self is conditioned, the non-existence of self is conditioned, form is conditioned, formlessness is conditioned, form and formlessness are conditioned, perception is conditioned, no perception is conditioned, perception and no perception are conditioned. Conditioned existence is a great affliction, a thorn, a wound. Therefore, the noble disciples know that conditioned existence is a great affliction, a thorn, a wound, and abandon conditioned existence, practicing the unconditioned.

「于是，诸天、阿须伦众遂共战鬪，诸天得胜，阿须伦退。时，忉利诸天捉阿须伦王，以五系系缚，将诣善法堂所，示天帝释。时，阿须伦王见天上快乐，生慕乐心，即自念言：『此处殊胜，即可居止，用复还归阿须伦宫为？』发此念时，五系即得解，五乐在前。若阿须伦生念欲还诣本宫殿，五系还缚，五乐自去。时，阿须伦所被系缚，转更牢固。魔所系缚复过于是，计吾我人为魔所缚，不计吾我人魔缚得解，爱我为缚，爱爱为缚，我当有为缚，我当无为缚，有色为缚，无色为缚，有色无色为缚，我有想为缚，无想为缚，有想无想为缚，我为大患、为痈、为刺。是故，贤圣弟子知我为大患、为痈、为刺，舍吾我想，修无我行，观彼我为重担、为放逸、为有。当有我是有为，当有无我是有为，有色是有为，无色是有为，有色无色是有为，有想是有为，无想是有为，有想无想是有为，有为为大患、为刺、为疮。是故，贤圣弟子知有为为大患、为刺、为疮故，舍有为，为无为行。」

The Buddha told the monks, "In the past, the devas fought with the asuras. At that time, Śakra, lord of the devas, ordered the Trāyastriṃśa devas, saying, 'You should now go and fight with the asuras. If you win, capture Vimalacitra, the asura, bind him with the five bonds, and bring him to the Sudharma Assembly Hall. I wish to see him.' At that time, the Trāyastriṃśa devas, having received Śakra's order, each adorned themselves. At that time, Vimalacitra, the asura, also ordered the asuras, saying, 'You should now go and fight with them. If you win, capture Śakra, lord of the devas, bind him with the five bonds, and bring him to the Saptaparṇa Assembly Hall. I wish to see him.' At that time, the asuras, having received Vimalacitra's order, each adorned themselves. Then the armies of the devas and asuras fought, and the devas won, while the asuras retreated. The Trāyastriṃśa devas captured the asura and bound him with the five bonds. They brought him to the Sudharma Assembly Hall to show Śakra, lord of the devas. Wandering and roaming in the Sudharma Assembly Hall, the asura king saw Śakra from afar and cursed him in foul language while bound by the five bonds. At that time, Śakra's attendant spoke a verse before Śakra:

佛告比丘：「昔者，诸天子与阿须伦共鬪。时，释提桓因命忉利天而告之曰：『汝等今往与阿须伦共鬪，若得胜者，捉毘摩质多罗阿须伦，以五系系缚，将诣善法讲堂，吾欲观之。』时，忉利诸天受帝释教已，各即自庄严。时，毘摩质多阿须伦复命诸阿须伦而告之曰：『汝等今往与彼共战，若得胜者，捉释提桓因，以五系系缚，将诣七叶讲堂，吾欲观之。』时，诸阿须伦受毘摩质多阿须伦教已，各自庄严。于是，诸天、阿须伦众遂共战鬪，诸天得胜，阿须伦退。忉利诸天捉阿须伦，以五系系缚，将诣善法堂所，示天帝释。彷徉游善法堂上，阿须伦王遥见帝释，于五系中恶口骂詈。时，天帝侍者于天帝前，即说偈言：

Why is Śakra, lord of the devas, afraid? He himself shows his weakness
Vimalacitra curses him face to face. He silently listens to his evil words.

「『天帝何恐怖，　　自现己劣弱，须质面毁呰，　　默听其恶言。』

At that time, Śakra, lord of the devas, immediately spoke a verse in reply to his attendant:

「时，天帝释即复以偈答侍者曰：

He also has no great power. I am not
afraid. How can a wise person argue with the unwise?

「『彼亦无大力，　　我亦不恐畏，如何大智士，　　与彼无智诤。』

At that time, the attendant again spoke a verse to Śakra, lord of the devas:

「尔时，侍者复作偈颂白帝释言：

If I do not subdue the foolish now, it will be difficult to endure
later. I should strike them with a staff, to make the foolish correct their faults.

「『今不折愚者，　　恐后转难忍，宜加以杖捶，　　使愚自改过。』

At that time, Śakra, lord of the devas, again spoke a verse in reply to the attendant:

「时，天帝释复作偈颂答侍者曰：

I always say that the wise should not argue with the foolish. When the
foolish scold and the wise remain silent, it is believed to be superior to them.

「『我常言智者，　　不应与愚诤，愚骂而智默，　　即为信胜彼。』

At that time, the attendant again spoke a verse to Śakra, lord of the devas:

「尔时，侍者复作偈颂白帝释言：

The heavenly king remains silent because he fears harming the wise. But
those foolish people think the king is afraid. The foolish do not
consider themselves and think they can compete with the king. They come
to touch and strike, wanting the king to retreat like a bull.

「『天王所以默，　　恐损智者行，而彼愚𫘤人，　　谓王怀怖畏。愚不自忖量，　　谓可与王敌，没死来触突，　　欲王如牛退。』

At that time, Śakra, lord of the devas, again spoke a verse in reply to the attendant:

「时，天帝释复作偈颂答侍者曰：

The foolish and ignorant see me as afraid. I contemplate
the ultimate truth, and silence is supreme. The worst of
evils is to be angry at anger. Being able to
not be angry at anger is supreme in battle. There
are two reasons for a person to be for oneself
and for others. When many people dispute and litigate, not
responding is the best. There are two reasons for a
person to be for oneself and for others. Seeing those
who do not dispute and litigate is considered foolish. If
a person with great strength can endure a weak person
this strength is supreme, the best in endurance. The foolish
consider themselves strong, but this strength is not strength. The
strength of endurance according to the Dharma is unstoppable.

「『彼愚无知见，　　谓我怀恐怖，我观第一义，　　忍默为最上。恶中之恶者，　　于瞋复生瞋，能于瞋不瞋，　　为战中最上。夫人有二缘，　　为己亦为他，众人诤有讼，　　不报者为胜。夫人有二缘，　　为己亦为他，见无诤讼者，　　乃谓为愚𫘤。若人有大力，　　能忍无力者，此力为第一，　　于忍中最上。愚自谓有力，　　此力非为力，如法忍力者，　　此力不可沮。』」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "At that time, was Śakra, lord of the devas, not someone else? Do not think so. Śakra, lord of the devas, was none other than myself. At that time, I cultivated patience and did not act rashly. I always praised those who were patient. If a wise person wishes to propagate my teachings, they should cultivate patience and silence, and not harbor anger and disputes."

佛告比丘：「尔时，天帝释岂异人乎？勿造斯观。时，天帝释即我身是也。我于尔时，修习忍辱，不行卒暴，常亦称赞能忍辱者。若有智之人欲弘吾道者，当修忍默，勿怀忿诤。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "In the past, the devas of Trāyastriṃśa fought with the asuras. At that time, Śakra, lord of the devas, said to the asura king Vemacitrin: 'Why do you adorn yourselves with weapons, harbor anger and the intention to harm, and fight with each other? Now I will discuss the meaning of the Way with you to determine victory and defeat.' The asura king Vemacitrin said to Śakra, lord of the devas: 'Even if we put aside all weapons and stop fighting to discuss the meaning, who will know victory and defeat?' Śakra instructed: 'Just discuss the meaning. Now in your assembly and my heavenly assembly, there are wise ones who will know victory and defeat.' At that time, the asura king Vemacitrin said to Śakra, lord of the devas: 'You should speak the verse first.' Śakra replied: 'You are the elder deva. You should speak first.' At that time, the asura king Vemacitrin spoke a verse for Śakra, lord of the devas:

佛告比丘：「昔者，忉利诸天与阿须伦共鬪。时，释提桓因语质多阿须伦言：『卿等何为严饰兵仗，怀怒害心，共战诤为？今当共汝讲论道义，知有胜负。』彼质多阿须伦语帝释言：『正使舍诸兵仗，止于诤讼论义者，谁知胜负？』帝释教言：『但共论议，今汝众中、我天众中，自有智慧知胜负者。』时，阿须伦语帝释言：『汝先说偈。』帝释报言：『汝是旧天，汝应先说。』尔时，质多阿须伦即为帝释而作颂曰：

If one does not correct the foolish now, it will be difficult to endure later. One
should use a staff to beat them, so that the foolish may correct their faults themselves.

「『今不折愚者，　　恐后转难忍，宜加以杖捶，　　使愚自改过。』

At that time, after the asura king Vemacitrin had spoken this verse, the asura assembly was greatly delighted and exclaimed in praise. Only the heavenly assembly was silent and did not speak. At that time, the asura king Vemacitrin said to Śakra, lord of the devas: 'You should speak the verse next.' At that time, Śakra, lord of the devas, spoke a verse for the asura king Vemacitrin:

「时，阿须伦说此偈已，阿须伦众即大欢喜，高声称善；唯诸天众默然无言。时，阿须伦王语帝释言：『汝次说偈。』尔时，帝释即为阿须伦而说偈言：

I always say that the wise should not argue with the foolish. When
the foolish scold and the wise are silent, they are victorious over the foolish.

「『我常言智者，　　不应与愚诤，愚骂而智默，　　即为胜彼愚。』

At that time, after Śakra, lord of the devas, had spoken this verse, the devas of Trāyastriṃśa were all greatly delighted and exclaimed in praise. At that time, the asura assembly was silent and did not speak. At that time, Śakra, lord of the devas, said to the asuras: 'You should speak the verse next.' At that time, the asuras spoke a verse:

「时，天帝释说此偈已，忉利诸天皆大欢喜，举声称善；时，阿须伦众默然无言。尔时，天帝语阿须伦言：『汝次说偈。』时，阿须伦复说偈言：

The reason the heavenly king is silent is to avoid harming the
wise. But those foolish people think the king is afraid. The foolish
do not consider themselves, thinking they can compete with the king. They
come to touch and strike, wanting the king to retreat like a cow.

「『天王所以默，　　恐损智者行，而彼愚𫘤人，　　谓王怀怖畏。愚不自忖量，　　谓可与王敌，没死来触突，　　欲王如牛退。』

At that time, after the asura king had spoken this verse, the asura assembly was elated and exclaimed in praise. At that time, the Trāyastriṃśa devas were silent and did not speak. At that time, the asura king said to Śakra, lord of the devas: 'You should speak the verse next.' At that time, Śakra, lord of the devas, spoke a verse for the asuras:

「时，阿须伦王说此偈已，阿须伦众踊跃欢喜，举声称善；时，忉利天众默然无言。时，阿须伦王语帝释言：『汝次说偈。』时，天帝释为阿须伦而说偈言：

The foolish and ignorant see me as afraid. I contemplate
the ultimate truth, and silence is supreme. Among evils, the
worst is to be angry at anger. Being able to
not be angry at anger is the best in battle
There are two reasons for a person to be for
oneself and for others. When many people quarrel, not retaliating
is the best. There are two reasons for a person
to be for oneself and for others. Seeing those who
do not quarrel is not considered foolish. If a person
with great strength can endure a weak person, this strength
is the best, supreme among endurance. The foolish consider themselves
strong, but this strength is not strength. The strength of
enduring according to the Dharma is unstoppable.

「『彼愚无知见，　　谓我怀恐畏，我观第一义，　　忍默为最上。恶中之恶者，　　于瞋复生瞋，能于瞋不瞋，　　为战中最胜。夫人有二缘，　　为己亦为他，众人为诤讼，　　不报者为胜。夫人有二缘，　　为己亦为他，见无诤讼者，　　不谓为愚𫘤。若人有大力，　　能忍无力者，此力为第一，　　于忍中最上。愚自谓有力，　　此力非为力，如法忍力者，　　此力不可沮。』

"After Śakra, lord of the devas, had spoken this verse, the Trāyastriṃśa devas were elated and exclaimed in praise. The asura assembly was silent and did not speak. At that time, the devas and asuras each retreated a little and said to each other: 'The verses spoken by the asura king are offensive, giving rise to the enmity of swords and weapons, the root of quarrels, increasing all resentments, and establishing the basis of the three realms of existence. The verses spoken by Śakra, lord of the devas, are not offensive, not giving rise to the enmity of swords and weapons, not giving rise to quarrels, not increasing resentments, and severing the basis of the three realms of existence. The words of Śakra are good, the words of the asura king are not good. The devas are victorious, the asuras are defeated.'"

「释提桓因说此偈已，忉利天众踊跃欢喜，举声称善；阿须伦众默然无言。时，天众、阿须伦众各小退却，自相谓言：『阿须伦王所说偈颂，有所触犯，起刀剑讐，生鬪讼根，长诸怨结，树三有本。天帝释所说偈者，无所触娆，不起刀剑，不生鬪讼，不长怨结，绝三有本。天帝所说为善，阿须伦所说不善。诸天为胜，阿须伦负。』」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "At that time, was Śakra, lord of the devas, not someone else? Do not think so. Why? It was I myself. At that time, I used gentle words to defeat the asura assembly."

佛告比丘：「尔时，释提桓因岂异人乎？勿造斯观。所以者何？即我身是。我于尔时，以柔濡言，胜阿须伦众。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "In the past, the devas again fought with the asuras. At that time, the asuras were victorious and the devas were defeated. Then Śakra, lord of the devas, rode in a jeweled chariot with a thousand spokes and fled in fear. On the way, he saw two young ones in a nest in a tree. He then addressed the charioteer in verse, saying:

佛告比丘：「昔者，诸天复与阿须伦共鬪。时，阿须伦胜，诸天不如。时，释提桓因乘千辐宝车怖惧而走，中路见晱婆罗树上有一巢，巢有两子，即以偈颂告御者言，颂曰：

There are two birds in this tree. You should turn the chariot to avoid them
Even if the enemy harms me, do not injure the lives of the two birds.

「『此树有二鸟，　　汝当回车避，正使贼害我，　　勿伤二鸟命。』

At that time, the charioteer, having heard Śakra's verse, immediately stopped the chariot and avoided the birds. At that time, the front of the chariot faced the asuras. The asura army, seeing the jeweled chariot with a thousand spokes turning towards them, immediately said to each other, 'The heavenly emperor Śakra is riding in a jeweled chariot with a thousand spokes and turning towards our army. He must want to fight again. It is unbearable!' The asura army then retreated and scattered. The devas were victorious and the asuras retreated.

「尔时，御者闻帝释偈已，寻便住车回避鸟。尔时，车头向阿须伦，阿须伦众遥见宝车回向，其军即相谓言：『今天帝释乘千辐宝车回向我众，必欲还鬪，不可当也。』阿须伦众即便退散，诸天得胜，阿须伦退。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "At that time, was Śakra someone else? Do not think so. Why? It was I myself. At that time, I gave rise to a compassionate mind towards all beings. Bhikṣus! You have left home and practiced the path in my Dharma. You should give rise to a compassionate mind and have pity on all sentient beings."

佛告比丘：「尔时，帝释者岂异人乎？勿造斯观。所以者何？即我身是也。我于尔时，于诸众生起慈愍心。诸比丘！汝等于我法中出家修道，宜起慈心，哀愍黎庶。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "In the past, the devas fought with the asuras." At that time, the devas were victorious and the asuras retreated. Then, Śakra, the lord of the devas, returned to his palace after winning the battle. He built a hall called "Most Victorious," which was one hundred yojanas long from east to west and sixty yojanas wide from south to north. The hall had a hundred chambers, and each chamber had seven intersecting pavilions. On each pavilion were seven jade maidens, and each jade maiden had seven attendants. Śakra did not worry about providing clothing, food, and adornments for the jade maidens. According to their past deeds, they received their own blessings. Because he had defeated the asuras in battle, he joyfully built this hall out of joy, thus it was called the "Most Victorious Hall." Moreover, among the halls and pavilions in the thousand worlds, none could compare to this hall, thus it was called "Most Victorious."

佛告比丘：「昔者，诸天与阿须伦共鬪。」尔时，诸天得胜，阿须伦退。时，天帝释战胜还宫，更造一堂，名曰最胜，东西长百由旬，南北广六十由旬。其堂百间，间间有七交露台，一一台上有七玉女，一一玉女有七使人。释提桓因亦不忧供给诸玉女衣被、饮食、庄严之具，随本所造，自受其福，以战胜阿须伦，因欢喜心而造此堂，故名最胜堂。又千世界中所有堂观无及此堂，故名最胜。

The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "In the past, the asuras had this thought: 'We have great power and supernatural abilities, yet the devas of Trāyastriṃśa, the sun, and the moon always roam freely above our heads in the sky. Now, should we take the sun and moon as earrings and roam freely?' At that time, the king of the asuras was filled with anger and immediately thought of beating the asuras. The asuras then thought, 'Now the king of the asuras is thinking of us. We should quickly prepare.' They then ordered their attendants to arm themselves, drive their jeweled chariots, and, accompanied by countless asura troops, went before the king of the asuras and stood to one side. At that time, the king again thought of Śaṃbara, the asura. Śaṃbara then thought to himself, 'Now the king is thinking of me. We should quickly prepare.' He then ordered his attendants to arm themselves, drive their jeweled chariots, and, accompanied by countless asura troops, went before the king of the asuras and stood to one side.

佛告比丘：「昔者，阿须伦自生念言：『我有大威德，神力不少，而忉利天、日月诸天常在虚空，于我顶上游行自在，今我宁可取彼日月以为耳珰，自在游行耶？』时，阿须伦王瞋恚炽盛，即念捶打阿须伦，捶打阿须伦即复念言：『今阿须伦王念我，我等当速庄严。』即勅左右备具兵仗，驾乘宝车，与无数阿须伦众前后导从，诣阿须伦王前，于一面立。时，王复念舍摩梨阿须伦，舍摩梨阿须伦复自念言：『今王念我，我等宜速庄严。』即勅左右备具兵仗，驾乘宝车，与无数阿须伦众前后导从，诣阿须伦王前，在一面立。

At that time, the king again thought of Vimalacitra, the asura. Vimalacitra then thought to himself, 'Now the king is thinking of me. We should quickly prepare.' He then ordered his attendants to arm themselves, drive their jeweled chariots, and, accompanied by countless asura troops, went before the king and stood to one side. At that time, the king again thought of his ministers, the asuras. The ministers then thought to themselves, 'Now the king is thinking of us. We should quickly prepare.' They then ordered their attendants to arm themselves, drive their jeweled chariots, and, accompanied by countless asura troops, went before the king and stood to one side. At that time, the king again thought of the lesser asuras. The lesser asuras then thought to themselves, 'Now the king is thinking of us. We should quickly prepare.' They then armed themselves, drove their jeweled chariots, and, accompanied by countless troops, went before the king and stood to one side. At that time, King Rāhu himself armed himself, donned his jeweled armor, drove his jeweled chariot, and, surrounded by countless hundreds of thousands of asura troops, left his realm to go and fight with the devas.

「时，王复念毘摩质多阿须伦，毘摩质多阿须伦复自念言：『今王念我，我等宜速庄严。』即勅左右备具兵仗，驾乘宝车，与无数阿须伦众前后导从，往诣王前，在一面立。时，王复念大臣阿须伦，大臣阿须伦即自念言：『今王念我，我等宜速庄严。』即勅左右备具兵仗，驾乘宝车，与无数阿须伦众前后导从，往诣王前，于一面立。时，王复念诸小阿须伦，诸小阿须伦复自念言：『今王念我，我等宜速庄严。』即自庄严，备具兵仗，与无数众相随，往诣王前，于一面立。时，罗呵阿须伦王即自庄严，身著宝铠，驾乘宝车，与无数百千阿须伦众兵仗严事，前后围遶出其境界，欲往与诸天共鬪。」

At that time, the nāga kings Nanda and Upananda wrapped their bodies around Mount Sumeru seven times, shaking the valleys, and thinly spread light rain, with their tails striking the great ocean, causing the sea water to surge and reach the summit of Mount Sumeru. At that time, the devas of Trāyastriṃśa immediately thought, 'Now the thin clouds are spreading, the light rain is falling, and the sea water is surging, reaching here. This must be an omen that the asuras are coming to fight.'

「尔时，难陀龙王、跋难陀龙王以身缠遶须弥山七匝，震动山谷，薄布微云，渧渧稍雨，以尾打大海水，海水波涌，至须弥山顶。时，忉利天即生念言：『今薄云微布，渧渧稍雨，海水波涌，乃来至此。将是阿须伦欲来战鬪，故有此异瑞耳。』

At that time, the countless millions of dragon troops in the ocean all held spears, bows, arrows, swords, and heavily armored themselves. Their weapons were well-equipped. They fought against the asuras. If the dragon troops were victorious, they would chase the asuras into their palaces. If the dragon troops retreated, the dragons would not return to their palaces. They would then flee to the realm of the garuḍa spirits and say, 'The asura troops want to fight with the devas. I fought against them, but they are now victorious. You should prepare your weapons and join forces to fight them.' When the spirits heard the words of the dragons, they immediately armed themselves, heavily armored themselves, and fought together with the dragon troops against the asuras. If they were victorious, they would chase the asuras into their palaces. If they were not victorious, they would not return to their original palaces. They would then retreat to the realm of the flower-holding spirits and say, 'The asura troops want to fight with the devas. We fought against them, but they are now victorious. You should prepare your weapons and join forces to fight them.'

「尔时，海中诸龙兵众无数巨亿，皆持戈𫓴、弓矢、刀剑，重被宝铠，器仗严整，逆与阿须伦共战，若龙众胜时，即逐阿须伦入其宫殿。若龙众退，龙不还宫，即［马＊奔］趣伽楼罗鬼神所，而告之曰：『阿须伦众欲与诸天共战，我往逆鬪，彼今得胜；汝等当备诸兵仗，众共并力，与彼共战。』时，诸鬼神闻龙语已，即自庄严，备诸兵仗，重被宝铠，与诸龙众共阿须伦鬪，得胜时，即逐阿须伦入其宫殿。若不如时，不还本宫，即退走［马＊奔］持华鬼神界，而告之言：『阿须伦众欲与诸天共鬪，我等逆战，彼今得胜；汝等当备诸兵仗，众共并力，与彼共战。』

The flower-holding spirits heard the words of the dragons and immediately armed themselves, heavily armored themselves, and joined forces to fight against the asuras. If they were victorious, they would chase the asuras into their palaces. If they were not victorious, they would not return to their original palaces. They would then retreat to the realm of the always joyful spirits and say, 'The asura troops want to fight with the devas. We fought against them, but they are now victorious. You should prepare your weapons and join forces to fight them.' At that time, the always joyful spirits heard these words and immediately armed themselves, heavily armored themselves, and joined forces to fight against the asuras. If they were victorious, they would chase the asuras into their palaces. If they were not victorious, they would not return to their original palaces. They would then retreat to the realm of the Four Heavenly Kings and say, 'The asura troops want to fight with the devas. We fought against them, but they are now victorious. You should prepare your weapons and join forces to fight them.'

「诸持华鬼神闻龙语已，即自庄严，备诸兵仗，重被宝铠，众共并力，与阿须伦鬪，若得胜时，即逐阿须伦入其宫殿。若不如时，不还本宫，即退走［马＊奔］常乐鬼神界，而告之言：『阿须伦众欲与诸天共鬪，我等逆战，彼今得胜；汝等当备诸兵仗，与我并力，共彼战鬪。』时，诸常乐鬼神闻是语已，即自庄严，备诸兵仗，重被宝铠，众共并力，与阿须伦鬪，若得胜时，即逐阿须伦入其宫殿。若不如时，不还本宫，即退走［马＊奔］四天王，而告之曰：『阿须伦众欲与诸天共鬪，我等逆战，彼今得胜；汝等当备诸兵仗，众共并力，与彼共战。』

"At that time, the Four Heavenly Kings heard these words and immediately armed themselves, heavily armored themselves, and joined forces to fight against the asuras. If they were victorious, they would chase the asuras into their palaces. If they were not victorious, the Four Heavenly Kings would then go to the hall of good Dharma and tell the Heavenly King Śakra and the devas of Trāyastriṃśa, 'The asuras want to fight with the devas. Now the devas of Trāyastriṃśa should arm themselves, prepare their weapons, and join forces to fight against them.' At that time, the Heavenly King Śakra ordered an attendant deva and said to him, 'You go and tell the devas of Yāma Heaven, Tuṣita Heaven, Nirmāṇarati Heaven, and Paranirmitavaśavartin Heaven, "The asuras with countless troops want to come and fight. Now the devas should arm themselves, prepare their weapons, and help me fight."'" At that time, the attendant deva received the order of the Heavenly King and went to Yāma Heaven, up to Paranirmitavaśavartin Heaven, and told them with the voice of the Heavenly King Śakra, "The asuras with countless troops are coming to fight. Now the devas should arm themselves, prepare their weapons, and help me fight."

「时，四天王闻此语已，即自庄严，备诸兵仗，重被宝铠，众共并力，与阿须伦共鬪，若得胜时，即逐阿须伦入其宫殿。若不如者，四天王即诣善法讲堂，白天帝释及忉利诸天言：『阿须伦欲与诸天共鬪，今忉利诸天当自庄严，备诸兵仗，众共并力，往共彼战。』时，天帝释命一侍天而告之曰：『汝持我声往告焰摩天、兜率天、化自在天、他化自在天子言：「阿须伦与无数众欲来战鬪，今者诸天当自庄严，备诸兵仗，助我鬪战。」』时，彼侍天受帝教已，即诣焰摩天，乃至他化自在天，持天帝释声而告之曰：『彼阿须伦无数众来战鬪，今者诸天当自庄严，备诸兵仗，助我战鬪。』

At that time, the devas of Yāma Heaven heard these words and immediately armed themselves, prepared their weapons, heavily armored themselves, drove their jeweled chariots, and surrounded themselves with countless hundreds of thousands of devas. They stayed on the eastern side of Mount Sumeru. At that time, the devas of Tuṣita Heaven heard these words and immediately armed themselves, prepared their weapons, heavily armored themselves, drove their jeweled chariots, and surrounded themselves with countless hundreds of thousands of devas. They stayed on the southern side of Mount Sumeru. At that time, the devas of Nirmāṇarati Heaven heard these words and also armed their troops, staying on the western side of Mount Sumeru. At that time, the devas of Paranirmitavaśavartin Heaven heard these words and also armed their troops, staying on the northern side of Mount Sumeru.

「时，焰摩天子闻此语已，即自庄严，备诸兵仗，重被宝铠，驾乘宝车，与无数巨亿百千天众前后围遶，在须弥山东面住。时，兜率天子闻此语已，即自庄严，备诸兵仗，重被宝铠，驾乘宝车，与无数巨亿百千天众围遶，在须弥山南面住。时，化自在天子闻此语已，亦严兵众，在须弥山西面住。时，他化自在天子闻此语已，亦严兵众，在须弥山北住。

At that time, the Heavenly King Śakra immediately thought of the Trāyastriṃśa devas, and the Trāyastriṃśa devas immediately thought to themselves, 'Now the Heavenly King Śakra is thinking of us. We should quickly arm ourselves.' They then ordered their attendants to prepare their weapons, drive their jeweled chariots, and surround themselves with countless hundreds of thousands of devas. They went to the Heavenly King Śakra and stood to one side. At that time, the Heavenly King Śakra again thought of the other Trāyastriṃśa devas, and the other Trāyastriṃśa devas immediately thought to themselves, 'Now the Heavenly King Śakra is thinking of us. We should quickly arm ourselves.' They then ordered their attendants to prepare their weapons, drive their jeweled chariots, and surround themselves with countless hundreds of thousands of devas. They went to the Heavenly King Śakra and stood to one side. At that time, the Heavenly King Śakra again thought of the skillful divine craftsmen, and the skillful divine craftsmen immediately thought to themselves, 'Now the Heavenly King Śakra is thinking of us. We should quickly arm ourselves.' They then ordered their attendants to prepare their weapons, drive their jeweled chariots, and be surrounded by countless thousands of devas. They went to the Heavenly King Śakra and stood before him. At that time, the Heavenly King Śakra again thought of the dragon king Suparṇa, and the dragon king Suparṇa immediately thought to himself, 'Now the Heavenly King Śakra is thinking of me. I should go now.' He then went to stand before the Heavenly King Śakra.

「时，天帝释即念三十三天忉利天，三十三天忉利天即自念言：『今帝释念我，我等宜速庄严。』即勅左右备诸兵仗，驾乘宝车，与无数巨亿诸天众前后围遶，诣天帝释前，于一面立。时，天帝释复念余忉利诸天，余忉利诸天即自念言：『今帝释念我，我等宜速庄严。』即勅左右备诸兵仗，驾乘宝车，与无数巨亿诸天众前后围遶，诣帝释前，于一面立。时，帝释复念妙匠鬼神，妙匠鬼神即自念言：『今帝释念我，我宜速庄严。』即勅左右备诸兵仗，驾乘宝车，无数千众前后围遶，诣帝释前立。时，帝释复念善住龙王，善住龙王即自念言：『今天帝释念我，我今宜往。』即诣帝释前立。

At that time, the Heavenly King Śakra immediately armed himself, prepared his weapons, heavily armored himself, rode on the head of the dragon king Suparṇa, and was surrounded by countless devas and spirits. He left his heavenly palace and went to fight with the asuras. Namely, he armed himself with weapons such as swords, spears, bows and arrows, axes, battle-axes, whirling wheels, and nooses. The weapons and armor were made of the seven treasures, and when they touched the bodies of the asuras, they did not injure them, but only touched them. The asura army held swords, spears, bows and arrows, axes, battle-axes, whirling wheels, and nooses made of the seven treasures. When they touched the bodies of the devas, they only touched them and could not injure them. Thus, the devas of the desire realm fought with the asuras because of desire and for the sake of desire.

「时，帝释即自庄严，备诸兵仗，身被宝铠，乘善住龙王顶上，与无数诸天鬼神前后围遶，自出天宫与阿须伦往鬪。所谓严兵仗、刀剑、𫓴矟、弓矢、斲𬬱、钺] cf.【丽】斧、旋轮、羂索，兵仗铠器，以七宝成，复以锋刃加阿须伦身，其身不伤，但刃触而已。阿须伦众执持七宝刀剑、𫓴矟、弓矢、斲𬬱、钺斧、旋轮、羂索，以锋刃加诸天身，但触而已，不能伤损。如是欲行诸天共阿须伦鬪，欲因欲是。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus, "There are three intermediate eons. What are the three? They are called the eon of weapons, the eon of famine, and the eon of pestilence. What is the eon of weapons? In this world, people originally lived for forty thousand years. After that, their lifespan gradually decreased to twenty thousand years, then ten thousand years, then one thousand years, then five hundred years, then three hundred years, then two hundred years, now people live for a hundred years, with a few more or less. After that, people's lifespan will gradually decrease to ten years. At that time, women will be married at the age of five. At that time, all the delicious foods such as butter, oil, honey, rock candy, and molasses will naturally disappear, and the five grains will not grow, only weeds will grow. At that time, all the fine clothes such as brocade, silk, cotton, and wool will no longer exist, only coarse woven grass clothes will remain. At that time, this land will be full of thorns, mosquitoes, bees, scorpions, snakes, and poisonous insects. Gold, silver, lapis lazuli, the seven treasures, and pearls will naturally sink into the ground, leaving only stones, sand, and filth. At that time, beings will only increase the ten unwholesome deeds, and will no longer hear the name of the ten wholesome deeds. At that time, there will be no name of goodness, let alone those who practice goodness. At that time, people who are unfilial to their parents and disrespectful to their teachers and elders will be able to receive offerings and be respected by others, just as people today who are filial to their parents and respectful to their teachers and elders can receive offerings and be respected by others. At that time, those who do evil will also receive offerings in the same way. When those people die, they will fall into the animal realm, just as people today can be reborn in the heavens. At that time, when people see each other, they will harbor malicious thoughts and only want to kill each other, just as a hunter sees a herd of deer and only wants to kill them, without a single good thought. Those people will be like this, only wanting to kill each other, without a single good thought. At that time, this land will have ditches, ravines, valleys, hills, and mounds, without a single flat area. When people walk, they will be terrified and fearful, with their hair standing on end.

佛告比丘：「有三中劫。何等为三？一名刀兵劫，二名谷贵劫，三名疾疫劫。云何为刀兵劫？此世间人本寿四万岁，其后稍减寿二万岁，其后复减寿万岁，转寿千岁，转寿五百岁，转寿三百岁、二百岁，如今人寿于百岁少出多减；其后人寿稍减，当寿十岁，是时女人生五月行嫁。时，世间所有美味，酥油、蜜、石蜜、黑石蜜，诸有美味皆悉自然消灭，五谷不生，唯有稊稗。是时，有上服锦绫、缯绢、劫贝、刍摩皆无复有，唯有麤织草衣。尔时，此地纯生荆棘、蚊虻、蜂蝎、蚖蛇、毒虫，金银、琉璃、七宝珠玉自然没地，唯有石沙秽恶充满。是时，众生但增十恶，不复闻有十善之名，乃无善名，况有行善者？尔时，人有不孝父母，不敬师长，能为恶者，则得供养，人所敬待，如今人孝顺父母，敬事师长，能为善者，则得供养，人所敬待。彼人为恶，便得供养，亦复如是。时人命终堕畜生中，犹如今人得生天上。时，人相见怀毒害心，但欲相杀。犹如猎师见彼群鹿，但欲杀之，无一善念。其人如是，但欲相杀，无一善念。尔时，此地沟涧、溪谷、山陵、塠阜，无一平地，时，人行] cf.【丽】来恐怖惶惧，衣毛为竖。

At that time, during the seven days, the eon of weapons arose. People held grass, wood, tiles, and stones in their hands, which all turned into swords and spears. The swords and spears were sharp, and whatever they struck was cut. They killed each other. Among them, there were wise ones who saw the killing with weapons and fled in terror, entering the mountains, forests, ravines, and uninhabited places to hide for seven days. They said to themselves, 'I will not harm others, and others should not harm me.' Those people ate the roots of grass and trees to sustain themselves for seven days. After seven days, they came out of the mountains and forests. At that time, one person met another and said with joy, 'Now I see a living person, now I see a living person.' It was like parents being reunited with their only child after a long separation, rejoicing and leaping with joy. They were also like this, rejoicing and leaping with joy. At that time, the people wept and faced each other for seven days, and for another seven days, they enjoyed themselves together, rejoicing and celebrating. At that time, when their bodies perished and their lives ended, they all fell into hell. Why was that? It was because those people always harbored anger and malice towards each other, without compassion and kindness. This is called the eon of weapons.

「时，七日中有刀剑劫起，时，人手执草木、瓦石，皆变成刀剑，刀剑锋利，所拟皆断，展转相害。其中有黠慧者见刀兵相害，恐怖逃避，入山林、坑涧无人之处，七日藏避，心口自言：『我不害人，人勿害我。』其人于七日中，食草木根，以自存活，过七日已，还出山林。时，有一人得共相见，欢喜而言：『今见生人，今见生人。』犹如父母与一子别，久乃相见，欢喜踊跃，不能自胜。彼亦如是，欢喜踊跃，不能自胜。是时，人民于七日中，哭泣相向，复于七日中，共相娱乐，欢喜庆贺。时人身坏命终，皆堕地狱中。所以者何？斯由其人常怀瞋怒，害心相向，无慈仁故，是为刀兵劫。」

What is the eon of famine? At that time, the people practiced many unwholesome dharmas, had wrong views, and engaged in the ten unwholesome deeds. Because of engaging in evil deeds, the heavens did not send rain, the herbs withered and died, and the five grains did not ripen, only the stalks remained. What is meant by famine? At that time, the people collected and swept the fields, streets, and roads, and the leftover grains in the dung to sustain themselves. This is called famine. Furthermore, during the famine, people picked up the bones in the streets, alleys, slaughterhouses, and hillsides, boiled them for juice, and drank them to sustain themselves. This is called the famine of white bones. Furthermore, during the famine eon, the five grains sown all turned into grass and trees. At that time, people picked the flowers and boiled them for juice to drink. Furthermore, during the famine, the flowers and leaves of the grass and trees fell and covered the ground. At that time, people dug the ground to pick the flowers and cooked them to eat, sustaining themselves with this. This is called the famine of grass and trees. At that time, when sentient beings' bodies perished and their lives ended, they fell into the realm of hungry ghosts. Why was that? It was because those people during the famine eon always harbored greed and stinginess, had no mind of giving and generosity, were unwilling to share, and did not think of those in distress. This is called the famine eon.

佛告比丘：「云何为饥饿劫？尔时，人民多行非法，邪见颠倒，为十恶业，以行恶故，天不降雨，百草枯死，五谷不成，但有茎秆。云何为饥饿？尔时，人民收扫田里、街巷、道陌、粪土遗谷，以自存活，是为饥饿。复次，饥饿时，其人于街巷、市里、屠杀之处及丘冢间，拾诸骸骨，煮汁饮之，以此自存，是为白骨饥饿。复次，饥饿劫时，所种五谷尽变成草木，时，人取华煮汁而饮。复次，饥饿时，草木华落，覆在土下，时，人掘地取华煮食，以是自存，是为草木饥饿。尔时，众生身坏命终，堕饿鬼中。所以者何？斯由其人于饥饿劫中，常怀悭贪，无施惠心，不肯分割，不念厄人故也，是为饥饿劫。」

What is the eon of pestilence? At that time, the people of the world practiced the right Dharma, had right views, and were not deluded. They were endowed with the ten wholesome deeds. The ghosts and spirits from other worlds came. The ghosts and spirits of this world were indulgent and licentious, unable to protect the people. The ghosts and spirits from other worlds harassed the people of this world, beating and striking them, taking their vital energy, causing their minds to be disturbed, and driving them away. It was like a king ordering his generals to guard something, but thieves from other places came to invade and harass the villages and countries. It was also like this. The ghosts and spirits from other worlds came and took the people of this world, beating and striking them, taking their vital energy, and driving them away.

佛告比丘：「云何为疾疫劫？尔时，世人修行正法，正见，不颠倒见，具十善行。他方世界有鬼神来，此间鬼神放逸婬乱，不能护人，他方鬼神侵娆此世间人，挝打捶杖，接其精气，使人心乱，驱逼将去。犹如国王勅诸将帅有所守护，余方有贼寇来侵娆，此放逸之人劫于村国。此亦如是，他方世界有鬼神来，取此间人，挝打捶杖，接其精气，驱逼将去。」

Even if the ghosts and spirits of this world were not indulgent and licentious, the ghosts and spirits of great power from other worlds would come. The ghosts and spirits of this world would be afraid and flee. Those great ghosts and spirits would harass these people, beating and striking them, taking their vital energy, and killing them. It was like a king or a king's minister sending generals to guard the people. The generals were pure and careful, without indulgence. But from other places came strong and brave generals with many soldiers and troops to break through the villages and cities, plundering the people. It was also like this. Even if the ghosts and spirits of this world did not dare to be indulgent, the ghosts and spirits of great power from other worlds would come. The ghosts and spirits of this world would be terrified and flee. Those great ghosts and spirits would harass these people, beating and striking them, taking their vital energy, and killing them. At that time, during the eon of pestilence, when the people's bodies perished and their lives ended, they were all reborn in the heavens. Why was that? It was because at that time people had compassionate minds towards each other, and they asked each other in turn, 'Are you well? Are you at ease?' Because of this cause and condition, they were reborn in the heavens. Therefore it was called the eon of pestilence. This is the third intermediate eon.

佛告比丘：「正使此间鬼神不放逸婬乱，他方世界有大力鬼神来，此间鬼神畏怖避去，彼大鬼神侵娆此人，挝打捶杖，接其精气，杀之而去。譬如国王、若王大臣，遣诸将帅守卫人民，将帅清慎，无有放逸；他方有强猛将帅，人兵众多来破村城，掠夺人物。彼亦如是，正使此间鬼神不敢放逸，他方世界有大力鬼神来，此间鬼神恐怖避去，彼大鬼神侵娆此人，挝打捶杖，接其精气，杀之而去。时，疾疫劫中人民身坏命终，皆生天上。所以者何？斯由时人慈心相向，展转相问：『汝病差不？身安隐不？』以此因缘得生天上。是故名为疾疫劫。是为三中劫也。」

After the fire calamity, when this world was about to form again, there were other beings whose blessings, practices, and lives were exhausted. They died in the Ābhāsvara Heaven and were reborn in the empty Brahma realm. They became attached to that place, loved it, and wished that other beings would be reborn there with them. After making this wish, other beings whose blessings, practices, and lives were exhausted died in the Ābhāsvara Heaven and were reborn in the empty Brahma realm. The Brahma Heaven who was born first thought to himself, 'I am the Brahma King, the Great Brahma Heaven. I was not created by anyone. I naturally exist. I am not subject to anyone. I am the most free in the thousand worlds. I am good at all meanings. I am rich and abundant. I can create all things. I am the parent of all beings.' The later Brahma Heavens also thought to themselves, 'The Brahma Heaven who was born first is the Brahma King, the Great Brahma Heaven. He naturally exists. He was not created by anyone. He is the most honored in the thousand worlds. He is not subject to anyone. He is good at all meanings. He is rich and abundant. He can create all things. He is the parent of all beings. I exist because of him.' The Brahma King's appearance and features are always like a child. Therefore the Brahma King is called 'Child'.

佛告比丘：「火灾过已，此世天地还欲成时，有余众生福尽、行尽、命尽，于光音天命终，生空梵处，于彼生染著心，爱乐彼处，愿余众生共生彼处。发此念已，有余众生福、行、命尽，于光音天身坏命终，生空梵处。时，先生梵天即自念言：『我是梵王大梵天王，无造我者，我自然有，无所承受，于千世界最得自在，善诸义趣，富有丰饶，能造化万物，我即是一切众生父母。』其后来诸梵复自念言：『彼先梵天即是梵王大梵天王，彼自然有，无造彼者，于千世界最尊第一，无所承受，善诸义趣，富有丰饶，能造万物，是众生父母，我从彼有。』彼梵天王颜貌容状常如童子，是故梵王名曰童子。

Sometimes, when this world was about to form again, many beings were born in the Ābhāsvara Heaven. They were born by transformation, with joy as their food. Their bodies were self-illuminating, they flew through the sky with supernatural powers, were at ease and unimpeded, and lived for a long time. Later, this world became a vast body of water, covering everywhere. At that time, the world was completely dark, with no sun, moon, stars, day or night, no years, months, or seasons. Later, when this world was about to change again, there were other beings whose blessings, practices, and lives were exhausted. They died in the Ābhāsvara Heaven and were reborn here. They were all born by transformation, with joy as their food. Their bodies were self-illuminating, they flew through the sky with supernatural powers, were at ease and unimpeded, and lived here for a long time. At that time, there were no men or women, no distinctions of high or low, no different names. They were all born together in the world, so they were called beings.

「或有是时，此世还成世间，众生多有生光音天者，自然化生，欢喜为食，身光自照，神足飞空，安乐无碍，寿命长久。其后此世变成大水，周遍弥满。当于尔时，天下大暗，无有日月、星辰、昼夜，亦无岁月、四时之数。其后此世还欲变时，有余众生福尽、行尽、命尽，从光音天命终，来生此间，皆悉化生，欢喜为食，身光自照，神足飞空，安乐无碍，久住此间。尔时，无有男女、尊卑、上下，亦无异名，众共生世，故名众生。

At that time, natural earth essence emerged from the ground, coagulating on the ground like ghee. When the earth essence emerged, it was also like fresh butter, sweet like honey. Later, the beings tried it with their hands to know what it tasted like. When they first tasted it, they found it delicious and became attached to it. As they kept tasting it, they became greedy and started scooping it up. Gradually, it became a solid food. As they kept eating it, other beings saw it and imitated them. As they kept eating it, the beings' bodies became rough and their light gradually dimmed. They lost their supernatural powers and could no longer fly. At that time, there were no sun and moon. When the beings' light dimmed, the world became completely dark, just like before. Later, after a long time, a great violent wind blew the deep ocean water, which was eighty-four thousand yojanas deep, apart. It took the sun palace and placed it halfway up Mount Sumeru, in the path of the sun. It rose in the east and set in the west, circling the world.

「是时，此地有自然地味出，凝停于地，犹如醍醐，地味出时，亦复如是，犹如生酥，味甜如蜜。其后众生以手试甞知为何味，初甞觉好，遂生味著。如是展转甞之不已，遂生贪著，便以手掬，渐成抟食，抟食不已，余众生见，复效食之，食之不已。时，此众生身体麤澁，光明转灭，无复神足，不能飞行。尔时，未有日月，众生光灭，是时，天地大暗，如前无异。其后久久，有大暴风吹大海水，深八万四千由旬，使令两披飘，取日宫殿，著须弥山半，安日道中，东出西没，周旋天下。

The second sun palace rose in the east and set in the west. At that time, the beings said, 'This is yesterday.' Some said, 'It is not yesterday.' The third sun palace circled Mount Sumeru, rising in the east and setting in the west. At that time, the beings said, 'It is definitely the same sun.' The meaning of 'sun' is 'previous illumination cause', so it is called 'sun'. The sun has two meanings: one is to always stay at a fixed distance, and the other is the palace.

「第二日宫从东出西没，时，众生有言：『是即昨日也。』或言：『非昨也。』第三日宫绕须弥山，东出西没，彼时众生言：『定是一日。』日者，义言是前明因，是故名为日。日有二义：一曰住常度，二曰宫殿。

The palace is seen as round from all four sides. It is cool and warm, made of heavenly gold interspersed with crystal. Two parts are pure heavenly gold, unadulterated, clear inside and out, with distant illumination. One part is pure crystal, unadulterated, clear inside and out, with distant illumination. The sun palace is fifty-one yojanas long and wide. The palace walls and ground are as thin as a zizhu or cypress tree.

「宫殿四方远见故圆，寒温和适，天金所成，颇梨间厕，二分天金，纯真无杂，外内清彻，光明远照，一分颇梨，纯真无杂，外内清彻，光明远照。日宫纵广五十一由旬，宫墙及地薄如梓柏。」

The palace has seven layers of walls, seven layers of railings, seven layers of nets, seven layers of jeweled bells, and seven layers of rows of trees, all adorned with the seven treasures. The golden walls have silver gates, the silver walls have golden gates, the lapis lazuli walls have crystal gates, the crystal walls have lapis lazuli gates, the red pearl walls have agate gates, the agate walls have red pearl gates, the carnelian walls have all-gemstone gates, and the all-gemstone walls have carnelian gates. The railings are also adorned with the seven treasures. The golden railings have silver crossbars, the silver railings have golden crossbars, the lapis lazuli railings have crystal crossbars, the crystal railings have lapis lazuli crossbars, the red pearl railings have agate crossbars, the agate railings have red pearl crossbars, the carnelian railings have all-gemstone crossbars, and the all-gemstone railings have carnelian crossbars. The golden nets have silver bells, the silver nets have golden bells, the crystal nets have lapis lazuli bells, the lapis lazuli nets have crystal bells, the red pearl nets have agate bells, the agate nets have red pearl bells, the carnelian nets have all-gemstone bells, and the all-gemstone nets have carnelian bells. The golden trees have silver leaves and fruits, the silver trees have golden leaves and fruits, the lapis lazuli trees have crystal flowers and fruits, the crystal trees have lapis lazuli flowers and fruits, the red pearl trees have agate flowers and fruits, the agate trees have red pearl flowers and fruits, the carnelian trees have all-gemstone flowers and fruits, and the all-gemstone trees have carnelian flowers and fruits. The palace has four gates, each with seven steps. Around it are railings, towers, pavilions, gardens, ponds, and various precious flowers growing in rows. There are various fruit trees with flowers and leaves of mixed colors, and the fragrance of the trees spreads far and wide. Various birds sing harmoniously.

「宫墙七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重宝铃、七重行树，周匝校饰以七宝成，金墙银门，银墙金门，琉璃墙水精门，水精墙琉璃门，赤珠墙马碯门，马碯墙赤珠门，车璩墙众宝门，众宝墙车璩门。又其栏楯，金栏银桄，银栏金桄，琉璃栏水精桄，水精栏琉璃桄，赤珠栏马碯桄，马碯栏赤珠桄，众宝栏车璩桄，车璩栏众宝桄。金网银铃，银网金铃，水精网琉璃铃，琉璃网水精铃，赤珠网马碯铃，马碯网赤珠铃，车璩网众宝铃，众宝网车璩铃。其金树者银叶华实，银树者金叶华实，琉璃树者水精华实，水精树者琉璃华实，赤珠树者马碯华实，马碯树者赤珠华实，车璩树者众宝华实，众宝树者车璩华实。宫墙四门，门有七阶，周匝栏楯，楼阁台观、园林浴池，次第相比，生众宝华，行行相当，种种果树，华叶杂色，树香芬馥，周流四远，杂类众鸟相和而鸣。

The sun palace is supported by five winds: the holding wind, the nourishing wind, the receiving wind, the turning wind, and the regulating wind. The main hall where the sun god resides is made entirely of gold, sixteen yojanas high, with four gates and railings all around. The throne of the sun god is half a yojana long and wide, made of the seven treasures, pure and soft, like heavenly garments. The sun god himself emits light that illuminates the golden hall, the light of the golden hall illuminates the sun palace, and the light of the sun palace shines on the four continents. The sun god lives for five hundred years in heaven, and his descendants succeed one another without interruption. The palace will not be destroyed until the end of the eon. When the sun palace moves, the sun god has no intention of moving, saying, 'I am moving and staying,' always entertaining himself with the five desires. When the sun palace moves, countless hundreds of thousands of great gods lead and follow in front, joyfully and tirelessly, delighting in speed. For this reason, the sun god is called 'swift'.

「其日宫殿为五风所持：一曰持风，二曰养风，三曰受风，四曰转风，五曰调风。日天子所止正殿，纯金所造，高十六由旬，殿有四门，周匝栏楯。日天子座纵广半由旬，七宝所成，清净柔软，犹如天衣。日天子自身放光照于金殿，金殿光照于日宫，日宫光出照四天下。日天子寿天五百岁，子孙相承，无有间异。其宫不坏，终于一劫。日宫行时，其日天子无有行意，言我行住，常以五欲自相娱乐。日宫行时，无数百千诸大天神在前导从，欢乐无倦，好乐捷疾，因是日天子名为捷疾。

The sun god emits a thousand rays of light, five hundred shining downward and five hundred shining sideways. This is due to the merit of past karma. Therefore, the sun god is called 'one with a thousand rays'. What is the merit of past karma? There was once a person who made offerings to śramaṇas and brāhmaṇas, relieved the poor and destitute, gave them food, clothing, medicine, elephants, horses, carriages, dwellings, and lamps, distributed them in a timely manner according to their needs, did not go against people's wishes, and made offerings to virtuous and holy people who upheld the precepts. Due to the causes and conditions of various kinds of Dharma joy and light, he was joyful in his good mind. It was like when a kṣatriya king of the water-sprinkling clan first ascended the throne, his good mind was joyful, just like that. Due to these causes and conditions, when his body perished and his life ended, he became the sun god, obtained the sun palace, and had a thousand rays of light. Therefore, it is said that good karma results in a thousand rays of light.

「日天子身出千光，五百光下照，五百光傍照，斯由宿业功德，故有此千光，是故日天子名为千光。宿业功德云何？或有一人供养沙门、婆罗门，济诸穷乏，施以饮食、衣服、汤药、象马、车乘、房舍、灯烛，分布时与，随其所须，不逆人意，供养持戒诸贤圣人。由彼种种无数法喜光明因缘，善心欢喜。如刹利王水浇头种初登王位，善心欢喜，亦复如是。以此因缘，身坏命终，为日天子，得日宫殿，有千光明，故言善业得千光明。

Furthermore, why is it called 'light of past karma'? There was once a person who did not kill, steal, engage in sexual misconduct, speak divisively, harshly, falsely, or frivolously, was not greedy, did not harbor ill-will or wrong views. Due to these causes and conditions, his good mind was joyful. It was like a large bathing pond at a four-way intersection, pure and free from impurities. A person traveling far would come to this pond, exhausted and thirsty, bathe and cool off, joyfully and lovingly. The ten wholesome deeds bring joy to the good mind in the same way. When that person's body perished and life ended, he became the sun god, dwelling in the sun palace with a thousand rays of light. For this reason, it is called 'light of good karma'.

「复以何等故，名为宿业光明？或有人不杀生，不盗，不邪婬，不两舌、恶口、妄言、绮语，不贪取，不瞋恚、邪见，以此因缘，善心欢喜。犹如四衢道头有大浴池，清净无秽，有人远行，疲极热渴，来入此池，澡浴清凉，欢喜爱乐。彼十善者，善心欢喜，亦复如是。其人身坏命终，为日天子，居日宫殿，有千光明，以是因缘故，名善业光明。

Furthermore, why is it called 'a thousand lights'? There was once a person who did not kill, steal, engage in sexual misconduct, deceive, or drink alcohol. Due to these causes and conditions, his good mind was joyful. When his body perished and life ended, he became the sun god, dwelling in the sun palace with a thousand rays of light. For this reason, it is called 'a thousand lights of good karma'.

「复以何缘名千光明？或有人不杀、不盗、不婬、不欺、不饮酒，以此因缘，善心欢喜，身坏命终，为日天子，居日宫殿，有千光明，以是因缘故，名善业千光明。

"Sixty moments of thought are called one laya. Thirty layas are called mahouda. One hundred mahoudas are called upama. The sun palace moves south for six months, traveling thirty li a day. It never goes beyond Jambudvipa to the south. The sun moves north in the same way."

「六十念顷名一罗耶，三十罗耶名摩睺多，百摩睺多名优波摩。日宫殿六月南行，日行三十里，极南不过阎浮提，日北行亦复如是。」

Why is the sunlight so hot? There are ten reasons. What are the ten? First, outside Mount Sumeru is Mount Khadara, 42,000 yojanas high, with a peak 42,000 yojanas wide, immeasurable in circumference, made of the seven treasures. The sunlight shines on the mountain, touching it and causing heat. This is the first reason for the hot sunlight. Second, outside Mount Khadara is Mount Ishadhara, 21,000 yojanas high, 21,000 yojanas long and wide, immeasurable in circumference, made of the seven treasures. The sunlight shines on the mountain, touching it and causing heat. This is the second reason for the hot sunlight. Third, outside Mount Ishadhara is Mount Tita, 12,000 yojanas high, 12,000 yojanas long and wide, immeasurable in circumference, made of the seven treasures. The sunlight shines on the mountain, touching it and causing heat. This is the third reason for the hot sunlight. Fourth, outside Mount Tita is Mount Sudarsana, 6,000 yojanas high, 6,000 yojanas long and wide, immeasurable in circumference, made of the seven treasures. The sunlight shines on the mountain, touching it and causing heat. This is the fourth reason for the hot sunlight. Fifth, outside Mount Sudarsana is Mount Asvakarna, 3,000 yojanas high, 3,000 yojanas long and wide, immeasurable in circumference, made of the seven treasures. The sunlight shines on the mountain, touching it and causing heat. This is the fifth reason for the hot sunlight. Sixth, outside Mount Asvakarna is Mount Nimindhara, 1,200 yojanas high, 1,200 yojanas long and wide, immeasurable in circumference, made of the seven treasures. The sunlight shines on the mountain, touching it and causing heat. This is the sixth reason for the hot sunlight. Seventh, outside Mount Nimindhara is Mount Vinataka, 600 yojanas high, 600 yojanas long and wide, immeasurable in circumference, made of the seven treasures. The sunlight shines on the mountain, touching it and causing heat. This is the seventh reason for the hot sunlight. Eighth, outside Mount Vinataka is Mount Vajra, 300 yojanas high, 300 yojanas long and wide, immeasurable in circumference, made of the seven treasures. The sunlight shines on the mountain, touching it and causing heat. This is the eighth reason for the hot sunlight. Furthermore, above 10,000 yojanas is a celestial palace called the stars, made of crystal. The sunlight shines on

「以何缘故日光炎热？有十因缘。何等为十？一者须弥山外有佉陀罗山，高四万二千由旬，顶广四万二千由旬，其边无量，七宝所成，日光照山，触而生热，是为一缘日光炎热。二者佉陀罗山表有伊沙陀山，高二万一千由旬，纵广二万一千由旬，周匝无量，七宝所成，日光照山，触而生热，是为二缘日光炎热。三者伊沙陀山表有树提陀罗山，上高万二千由旬，纵广万二千由旬，周匝无量，七宝所成，日光照山，触而生热，是为三缘日光炎热。四者去树提陀罗山表有山名善见，高六千由旬，纵广六千由旬，周匝无量，七宝所成，日光照山，触而生热，是为四缘日光炎热。五者善见山表有马祀山，高三千由旬，纵广三千由旬，周匝无量，七宝所成，日光照山，触而生热，是为五缘日光炎热。六者去马祀山表有尼弥陀罗山，高千二百由旬，纵广千二百由旬，周匝无量，七宝所成，日光照山，触而生热，是为六缘日光炎热。七者去尼弥陀罗山表有调伏山，高六百由旬，纵广六百由旬，周匝无量，七宝所成，日光照山，触而生热，是为七缘日光炎热。八者调伏山表有金刚轮山，高三百由旬，纵广三百由旬，周匝无量，七宝所成，日光照山，触而生热，是为八缘日光炎热。复次，上万由旬有天宫殿，名为星宿，琉] cf.【丽】璃所成，日光照彼，触而生热，是为九缘日光炎热。复次，日宫殿光照于大地，触而生热，是为十缘日光炎热。」尔时，世尊以偈颂曰：

For these ten reasons, the sun is called the thousand-rayed one
The light is blazing hot. This is what the Buddha has said.

「以此十因缘，　　日名为千光，光明炎炽热，　　佛日之所说。」

Why is the winter sun's palace cold and unapproachable, with light but cold? There are thirteen reasons why the sunlight is cold. What are the thirteen? First, between Mount Sumeru and Mount Khadara is water, 84,000 yojanas wide, immeasurable in circumference. Various flowers grow in the water: blue lotus flowers, red lotus flowers, white lotus flowers, and water lilies. The sunlight shines on them, touching them and causing coolness. This is the first reason why the sunlight is cool. Second, between Mount Khadara and Mount Ishadhara is water, 42,000 yojanas wide, 42,000 yojanas long and wide, immeasurable in circumference. Various flowers grow in the water. The sunlight shines on them, touching them and causing coolness. This is the second reason why the sunlight is cool. Third, between Mount Ishadhara and Mount Tita is water, 21,000 yojanas wide, immeasurable in circumference. Various flowers grow in the water. The sunlight shines on them, touching them and causing coolness. This is the third reason why the sunlight is cool. Fourth, between Mount Tita and Mount Sudarsana is water, 12,000 yojanas wide, immeasurable in circumference. Various flowers grow in the water. The sunlight shines on them, touching them and causing coolness. This is the fourth reason why the sunlight is cool. Fifth, between Mount Sudarsana and Mount Asvakarna is water, 6,000 yojanas wide. Various flowers grow in the water. The sunlight shines on them, touching them and causing coolness. This is the fifth reason why the sunlight is cool. Sixth, between Mount Asvakarna and Mount Nimindhara is water, 1,200 yojanas wide, immeasurable in circumference. Various flowers grow in the water. The sunlight shines on them, touching them and causing coolness. This is the sixth reason why the sunlight is cool. Between Mount Nimindhara and Mount Vinataka is water, 600 yojanas wide, immeasurable in circumference. Various flowers grow in the water. The sunlight shines on them, touching them and causing coolness. This is the seventh reason why the sunlight is cool. Between Mount Vinataka and Mount Vajra is water, 300 yojanas wide, immeasurable in circumference. Various flowers grow in the water. The sunlight shines on them, touching them and causing coolness. This is the eighth reason why the sunlight is cool. Furthermore, the sunlight shines on the great ocean waters of this Jambudvipa, touching them and causing coolness. This is the ninth reason why the sunlight is cool. In Jambudvipa, there are few rivers. In Kuru, there is much water. The sunlight shines on it, touching it and causing coolness. This is the tenth

佛告比丘：「何故冬日宫殿寒而不可近，有光而冷？有十三缘，虽光而冷。云何为十三？一者须弥山、佉陀罗山中间有水，广八万四千由旬，周匝无量，其水生杂华：优钵罗华、拘勿头、钵头摩、分陀利、须干提华，日光所照，触而生冷，是为一缘日光为冷。二者佉陀罗山、伊沙陀罗山中间有水，广四万二千由旬，纵广四万二千由旬，周匝无量，有水生诸杂华，日光所照，触而生冷，是为二缘日光为冷。三者伊沙陀罗山去树提陀罗山中间有水，广二万一千由旬，周匝无量，生诸杂华，日光所照，触而生冷，是为三缘日光为冷。四者善见山、树提山中间有水，广万二千由旬，周匝无量，生诸杂华，日光所照，触而生冷，是为四缘日光为冷。五者善见山、马祀山中间有水，广六千由旬，生诸杂华，日光所照，触而生冷，是为五缘日光为冷。六者马祀山、尼弥陀罗山中间有水，广千二百由旬，周匝无量，生诸杂华，日光所照，触而生冷，是为六缘日光为冷。尼弥陀罗山、调伏山中间有水，广六百由旬，周匝无量，生诸杂华，日光所照，触而生冷，是为七缘日光为冷。调伏山、金刚轮山中间有水，广三百由旬，周匝无量，生诸杂华，日光所照，触而生冷，是为八缘日光为冷。复次，此阎浮利地大海江河，日光所照，触而生冷，是为九缘日光为冷。阎浮提地河少，拘耶尼地水多，日光所照，触而生冷，是为十缘日光为冷。拘耶尼河少，弗于逮水多，日光所照，触而生冷，是为十一缘日光为冷。弗于逮河少，欝单曰河多，日光所照，触而生冷，是为十二缘日光为冷。复次，日宫殿光照大海水，日光所照，触而生冷，是为十三缘日光为冷。」佛时颂曰：

For these thirteen reasons, the sun is called the thousand-rayed one. Its
light is cool and clear. This is what the Buddha has said.

「以此十三缘，　　日名为千光，其光明清冷，　　佛日之所说。」

The Buddha told the monks, 'The moon palace sometimes loses its substance and waxes and wanes, and its light diminishes. Therefore, the moon palace is called 'loss'. The moon has two meanings: one is to always abide in its orbit, and the other is the palace. Seen from afar in the four directions, it appears round. The temperature is moderate and pleasant. It is made of celestial silver and lapis lazuli. Two parts are pure celestial silver, without any impurities, clear inside and out, with light shining far. One part is pure lapis lazuli, without any impurities, clear inside and out, with light shining far. The moon palace is forty-nine yojanas long and wide. The palace walls and ground are as thin as a zizhu tree. The palace walls are sevenfold, with seven railings, seven nets, seven rows of jeweled bells, and seven rows of trees, all adorned with the seven treasures, up to countless birds singing harmoniously together.

佛告比丘：「月宫殿有时损质盈亏，光明损减，是故月宫名之为损。月有二义：一曰住常度，二曰宫殿。四方远见故圆，寒温和适，天银、琉璃所成，二分天银，纯真无杂，内外清彻，光明远照，一分琉璃，纯真无杂，外内清彻，光明远照。月宫殿纵广四十九由旬，宫墙及地薄如梓柏，宫墙七重，七重栏楯、七重罗网、七重宝铃、七重行树，周匝校饰以七宝成，乃至无数众鸟相和而鸣。

The moon palace is held by five winds: the holding wind, the nourishing wind, the receiving wind, the turning wind, and the regulating wind. The main hall where the moon king resides is made of lapis lazuli, sixteen yojanas high, with four gates and railings all around. The moon king's seat is half a yojana long and wide, made of the seven treasures, pure and soft, like heavenly garments. The moon king's body emits light, illuminating the lapis lazuli hall. The light from the lapis lazuli hall illuminates the moon palace, and the light from the moon palace shines on the four continents. The moon king's lifespan is five hundred years in the heavens, and his descendants succeed one another without interruption. The palace will not be destroyed until the end of the eon. When the moon palace moves, the moon king has no intention of moving, saying, 'I am moving and staying,' always amusing himself with the five desires. When the moon palace moves, countless hundreds of thousands of great gods always lead the way, enjoying themselves without weariness, enjoying themselves swiftly. For this reason, the moon king is called 'swift'.
