「其月宫殿为五风所持：一曰持风，二曰养风，三曰受风，四曰转风，五曰调风。月天子所止正殿，琉璃所造，高十六由旬，殿有四门，周匝栏楯。月天子座纵广半由旬，七宝所成，清净柔软，犹如天衣。月天子身放光明，照琉璃殿，琉璃殿光照于月宫，月宫光出照四天下。月天子寿天五百岁，子孙相承，无有异系。其宫不坏，终于一劫。月宫行时，其月天子无有行意，言我行住，常以五欲自相娱乐。月宫行时，无数百千诸大天神常在前导，好乐无倦，好乐捷疾，因是月天名为捷疾。

The moon king's body emits a thousand lights, five hundred lights shining downward and five hundred lights shining sideways. This is due to the merit of past karma, and thus the moon king is called 'a thousand lights'. What is the merit of past karma? In the world, there are people who make offerings to śramaṇas and brāhmaṇas, give food, clothing, medicine, elephants, horses, carriages, dwellings, and lamps to the poor and destitute, distribute them according to their needs, not going against their wishes, and make offerings to virtuous and holy people who uphold the precepts. This is the joy of various immeasurable dharmas, the light of a good mind. It is like when a kṣatriya king ascends the throne after being consecrated with water, the joy of his good mind is also like this. For this cause and condition, when the body perishes and life ends, he becomes the moon king, and the moon palace has a thousand lights. Therefore, it is said that good karma obtains a thousand lights.

「月天子身出千光明，五百光下照，五百光傍照，斯由宿业功德故有此光明，是故月天子名曰千光。宿业功德云何？世间有人供养沙门、婆罗门，施诸穷乏饮食、衣服、汤药、象马、车乘、房舍、灯烛，分布时与，随意所须，不逆人意，供养持戒诸贤圣人。犹是种种无数法喜，善心光明。如刹利王水浇头种初登王位，善心欢喜，亦复如是。以是因缘，身坏命终，为月天子，月宫殿有千光明，故言善业得千光明。

Furthermore, what karma is obtained for a thousand lights? There are people in the world who do not kill, steal, engage in sexual misconduct, speak divisively, harshly, falsely, or frivolously, are not greedy, angry, or have wrong views. For this cause and condition, they have a good mind and rejoice. It is like a large bathing pond at a four-way intersection, clean and free from impurities. Someone traveling far, tired and thirsty, comes and bathes in the pond, feeling refreshed and joyful. Those who practice the ten wholesome deeds and rejoice with a good mind are also like this. When their bodies perish and lives end, they become moon kings, dwelling in the moon palace with a thousand lights. For this cause and condition, they are called 'a thousand lights through good karma'.

「复以何业得千光明？世间有人不杀，不盗，不邪婬，不两舌、恶口、妄言、绮语，不贪取、瞋恚、邪见，以此因缘，善心欢喜。犹如四衢道头有大浴池清净无秽，有人远行，疲极热渴，来入此池，澡浴清凉，欢喜快乐。彼行十善者，善心欢喜，亦复如是。其人身坏命终，为月天子，居月宫殿，有千光明，以是因缘故，名善业千光。

Furthermore, what causes and conditions are obtained for a thousand lights? There are people in the world who do not kill, steal, engage in sexual misconduct, deceive, or drink alcohol. For this cause and condition, they have a good mind and rejoice. When their bodies perish and lives end, they become moon kings, dwelling in the moon palace with a thousand lights. For this cause and condition, they are called 'a thousand lights through good karma'.

「复以何因缘得千光明？世间有人不杀、不盗、不婬、不欺、不饮酒，以此因缘，善心欢喜。身坏命终，为月天子，居月宫殿，有千光明，以是因缘故，名善业千光。六十念顷名一罗耶，三十罗耶名摩睺多，百摩睺多名优婆摩。若日宫殿六月南行，日行三十里，极南不过阎浮提，是时，月宫殿半岁南行，不过阎浮提；月北行亦复如是。

What are the reasons for the gradual decrease of the moon palace? There are three reasons for the gradual decrease of the moon palace: First, when the moon rises, this is one reason for the moon's gradual decrease. Furthermore, in the moon palace, the ministers wear blue robes, ascending in order, and where they stand becomes blue. Therefore, the moon gradually decreases. This is the second reason for the moon's gradual decrease. Furthermore, the sun palace has sixty lights that shine on the moon palace, obscuring it from view. Therefore, where it is obscured, the moon gradually decreases. This is the third reason for the gradual decrease of the moon's light.

「以何缘故月宫殿小小损减？有三因缘故月宫殿小小损减：一者月出于维，是为一缘故月损减。复次，月宫殿内有诸大臣身著青服，随次而上，住处则青，是故月减，是为二缘月日日减。复次，日宫有六十光，光照于月宫，映使不现，是故所映之处月则损减。是为三缘月光损减。

Furthermore, what are the reasons for the gradual increase of the moon's light? There are also three reasons for the gradual increase of the moon's light. What are the three? First, when the moon faces the cardinal directions, this is why the moon's light gradually increases. Second, all the ministers in the moon palace wear blue robes. When the moon king sits in the middle on the fifteenth day to enjoy himself, his light shines everywhere, outshining the light of the gods. Therefore, the light is completely full, just like when a large torch is lit among many lamps and candles, outshining the light of the lamps. The moon king is also like this. On the fifteenth day, he is among the heavenly beings, outshining the light of the multitude. His light shines alone, also like this. This is the second reason. Third, although the sun king has sixty lights that shine on the moon palace, on the fifteenth day, the moon king is able to shine his light back, preventing it from being obscured. This is the third reason for the moon palace being completely full without any decrease. Furthermore, what are the reasons for the moon having a black shadow? Because the shadow of the Jambū tree is in the middle of the moon, the moon has a shadow.

「复以何缘月光渐满？复有三因缘使月光渐满。何等为三？一者月向正方，是故月光满。二者月宫诸臣尽著青衣，彼月天子以十五日处中而坐，共相娱乐，光明遍照，遏诸天光，故光普满。犹如众灯烛中燃大炬火，遏诸灯明。彼月天子亦复如是，以十五日在天众中，遏绝众明，其光独照，亦复如是，是为二因缘。三者日天子虽有六十光照于月宫，十五日时月天子能以光明逆照，使不掩翳，是为三因缘月宫团满无有损减。复以何缘月有黑影？以阎浮树影在于月中，故月有影。」

The Buddha told the bhikṣus: "The mind should be like the moon, cool and free from heat. When visiting the homes of benefactors, be focused and undistracted. Furthermore, what are the reasons for the existence of rivers? Due to the heat of the sun and moon, there is burning. Due to burning, there is sweating. Due to sweating, rivers are formed. Therefore, there are rivers in the world. What are the reasons for the existence of the five kinds of seeds in the world? There are great turbulent winds that blow seeds from the world of non-decay and bring them to be born in this country. The first is root seeds, the second is stem seeds, the third is node seeds, the fourth is hollow seeds, and the fifth is seed seeds. These are the five seeds. For these reasons, the five kinds of seeds exist in the world.

佛告比丘：「心当如月，清凉无热，至檀越家，专念不乱。复以何缘有诸江河？因日月有热，因热有炙，因炙有汗，因汗成江河，故世间有江河。有何因缘世间有五种子？有大乱风，从不败世界吹种子来生此国，一者根子，二者茎子，三者节子，四者虚中子，五者子子，是为五子。以此因缘，世间有五种子出。

When it is noon in Jambudvīpa, it is sunset in Pūrvavideha, sunrise in Aparagodānīya, and midnight in Uttarakuru. When it is noon in Aparagodānīya, sunset in Jambudvīpa, sunrise in Uttarakuru, and midnight in Pūrvavideha. When it is noon in Uttarakuru, sunset in Aparagodānīya, sunrise in Pūrvavideha, and midnight in Jambudvīpa. When it is noon in Pūrvavideha, sunset in Uttarakuru, sunrise in Jambudvīpa, and midnight in Aparagodānīya. Jambudvīpa is in the east of Jambudvīpa, Pūrvavideha is in the west. Jambudvīpa is in the west, Aparagodānīya is in the east. Aparagodānīya is in the west, Uttarakuru is in the east. Uttarakuru is in the west, Pūrvavideha is in the east.

「此阎浮提日中时，弗于逮日没，拘耶尼日出，郁单曰夜半；拘耶尼日中阎浮提日没，郁单曰日出，弗于逮夜半；郁单曰日中，拘耶尼日没，弗于逮日出，阎浮提夜半；若弗于逮日中，郁单曰日没，阎浮提日出，拘耶尼夜半。阎浮提东方，弗于逮为西方；阎浮提为西方，拘耶尼为东方；拘耶尼为西方，郁单曰为东方；郁单曰为西方，弗于逮为东方。

The reason Jambudvīpa is called Jambudvīpa is because below it there is a golden mountain, thirty yojanas high, and it is named after the Jambū tree that grows there, thus it is called Jambū gold. The fruit of the Jambū tree is like a mushroom, and its taste is like honey. There are five large branches on the tree, four on the four sides and one on top. The fruit on the eastern branch is eaten by the Gandharvas. The fruit on the southern branch is eaten by the people of seven countries: namely, the country of Kūlou, Kūlavap, Vidi, Sūvidi, Mandha, Brāhma, and Brāri. The fruit on the western branch is eaten by sea creatures. The fruit on the northern branch is eaten by birds and beasts. The fruit on the top branch is eaten by the heavenly beings of the stars. There are seven large black mountains north of the seven great countries: namely, Naked Earth, White Crane, Lizard, Immortal Mountain, High Mountain, Meditation Mountain, and Earth Mountain. On these seven black mountains live seven brāhman ascetics. The seven places where these seven ascetics live are named Santikīrti, Sūryaprabha, Lizard, Immortal, Palace Protector, Gaṇanā, and Increase.

「所以阎浮提名阎浮者，下有金山，高三十由旬，因阎浮树生，故得名为阎浮金。阎浮树其果如蕈，其味如蜜。树有五大孤，四面四孤，上有一孤，其东孤孤果干闼和所食；其南孤者七国人所食：一曰拘楼国、二曰拘罗婆、三名毘提、四名善毘提、五名漫陀、六名婆罗、七名婆梨；其西孤果海虫所食；其北孤果者禽兽所食；其上孤果者星宿天所食。七大国北有七大黑山：一曰裸土，二曰白鹤，三曰守宫，四者仙山，五者高山，六者禅山，七者土山。此七黑山上有七婆罗门仙人，此七仙人住处，一名善帝，二名善光，三名守宫，四名仙人，五者护宫，六者伽那那，七者增益。」

The Buddha told the monks, "After the sentient beings of the beginning of the eon ate the earth essence, they lived for a long time. Those who ate more had coarse and haggard complexions, while those who ate less had lustrous complexions. Then they knew that the complexions and appearances of sentient beings were superior and inferior, and they criticized each other, saying, 'I am better than you, you are not as good as me.' Because their minds were attached to each other and they harbored disputes, the earth essence disappeared. Then earth skin grew, resembling thin pancakes, with color, taste, and fragrance. At that time, the sentient beings gathered in one place, lamenting and crying, beating their chests and saying, 'Alas, what a disaster! Now the earth essence no longer appears.' It was like when people today obtain delicious food and praise it as excellent, but later lose it and become distressed. They were also like this, distressed and regretful. Later, they ate the earth skin and gradually tasted it. Those who ate more had coarse and haggard complexions, while those who ate less had lustrous complexions. Then they knew that the complexions and appearances of sentient beings were superior and inferior, and they criticized each other, saying, 'I am better than you, you are not as good as me.' Because their minds were attached to each other and they harbored disputes, the earth skin disappeared.

佛告比丘：「劫初众生食地味已，久住于世，其食多者颜色麤悴，其食少者颜色光润，然后乃知众生颜色形貌优劣，互相是非，言：『我胜汝，汝不如我。』以其心存彼我，怀诤竞故，地味消竭。又地皮生，状如薄饼，色味香洁。尔时，众生聚集一处，懊恼悲泣，椎胷而言：『咄哉为祸！今者地味初不复现。』犹如今人得盛美味，称言美善，后复失之以为忧恼，彼亦如是忧恼悔恨。后食地皮，渐得其味，其食多者颜色麤悴，其食少者颜色润泽，然后乃知众生颜色形貌优劣，互相是非，言：『我胜汝，汝不如我。』以其心存彼我，怀诤竞故，地皮消竭。

After that, earth skin grew again, becoming thicker and coarser, with a color like heavenly flowers, soft like heavenly garments, and a taste like honey. At that time, the sentient beings again took it to eat together, living for a long time. Those who ate more had increasingly worse complexions, while those who ate very little had lustrous complexions. Then they knew that the complexions and appearances of sentient beings were superior and inferior, and they criticized each other, saying, 'I am better than you, you are not as good as me.' Because their minds were attached to each other and they harbored disputes, the earth skin disappeared. After that, there was naturally grown rice, without any husks or chaff, not requiring any preparation, and with all kinds of delicious flavors. At that time, the sentient beings gathered and said, 'Alas, what a disaster! Now the earth skin suddenly no longer appears.' It was like when people today encounter misfortune and difficulties, exclaiming, 'Alas!' At that time, the sentient beings were also like this, lamenting and sighing in distress.

「其后复有地肤出，转更麤厚，色如天华，软若天衣，其味如蜜。时，诸众生复取共食，久住于世，食之多者颜色转损，食甚少者颜色光泽，然后乃知众生颜色形貌优劣，互相是非，言：『我胜汝，汝不如我。』以其心存彼我，怀诤竞故，地肤消竭。其后复有自然粳米，无有糠糩，不加调和，备众美味。尔时，众生聚集而言：『咄哉为祸！今者地肤忽不复现。』犹如今人遭祸逢难，称言：『苦哉！』尔时，众生亦复如是懊恼悲叹。

After that, the sentient beings began to take the rice to eat. Their bodies became coarse and ugly, with male and female forms. Looking at each other, they gave rise to lustful thoughts and engaged in impure conduct in private. Other sentient beings saw this and said, 'Alas, this is wrong! How can sentient beings give rise to such things together?' The man who engaged in impure conduct saw others scolding him and immediately repented, saying, 'What I did was wrong.' He then threw himself to the ground. The woman saw the man throw himself to the ground, repenting and not getting up. The woman then sent him food. Other sentient beings saw this and asked the woman, 'You are holding this food, to whom do you want to give it?' She replied, 'To that sentient being who repents and has fallen into unwholesome conduct, I will send food to him.' Because of these words, the world then had the name of unwholesome husbands; because of sending rice to her husband, she was named a wife.

「其后众生便共取粳米食之，其身麤丑，有男女形，互相瞻视，遂生欲想，共在屏处为不净行。余众生见言：『咄此为非！云何众生共生有如此事？』彼行不净男子者，见他呵责，即自悔过言：『我所为非。』即身投地。其彼女人见其男子以身投地，悔过不起，女人即便送食。余众生见，问女人言：『汝持此食，欲以与谁？』答曰：『彼悔过众生堕不善行者，我送食与之。』因此言故，世间便有不善夫主之名；以送饭与夫，因名之为妻。

After that, the sentient beings became increasingly indulgent in lust, and unwholesome dharmas increased. In order to conceal themselves, they built houses. Because of this, the name 'house' first appeared. After that, the sentient beings became increasingly indulgent in lust, and eventually became husband and wife. Other sentient beings, whose lifespan, conduct, and merit were exhausted, passed away from the Ābhāsvara Heaven and were reborn here in the womb. Because of this, the world had the name 'womb'. At that time, the city of Campā was first built, followed by the cities of Kāśī and Vārāṇasī, and then the city of Rājagṛha. It was built at sunrise and completed at sunrise. Because of this, the world then had the names of cities, counties, and kingdoms.

「其后众生遂为婬逸，不善法增，为自障蔽，遂造屋舍，以此因缘故，始有舍名。其后众生婬逸转增，遂成夫妻。有余众生寿、行、福尽，从光音天命终，来生此间，在母胎中，因此世间有处胎名。尔时，先造瞻婆城，次造伽尸婆罗捺城，其次造王舍城。日出时造，即日出时成。以此因缘，世间便有城郭、郡邑王所治名。

At that time, when the sentient beings first ate the naturally grown rice, it was harvested in the evening and ripened in the morning, harvested in the morning and ripened in the evening. After harvesting, it grew again, without any stalks. At that time, a sentient being silently thought to himself, 'Harvesting every day is tiring for me. I should now gather enough for several days.' He then gathered enough for several days. Later, another person said to him, 'Now let us go together to gather rice.' This person replied, 'I have already gathered enough for several days. If you want to gather, go as you please.' The other person then thought to himself, 'The previous person was able to gather enough for two days. How could I not be able to gather enough for three days?' This person then gathered enough for three days. Another person said to him, 'Let us go together to gather grain.' This person replied, 'I have already gathered enough for three days. If you want to gather, go as you please.' This person then thought to himself, 'The previous person was able to gather enough for three days. How could I not be able to gather enough for five days?' He then gathered enough for five days. At that time, because the sentient beings competed to store extra grain, the rice then grew husks and chaff. After harvesting, it did not grow again, and withered stalks appeared.

「尔时，众生初食自然粳米时，朝收暮熟，暮收朝熟，收后复生，无有茎秆。时，有众生默自念言：『日日收获，疲劳我为？今当并取以供数日。』即时并获，积数日粮。余人于后语此人言：『今可相与共取粳米。』此人答曰：『我已先积，不须更取。汝欲取者，自随意去。』后人复自念言：『前者能取二日余粮，我岂不能取三日粮耶？』此人即积三日余粮。复有余人语言：『共取粮去来。』此人答曰：『我已取三日余粮。汝欲取者，自随汝意。』此人念言：『彼人能取三日粮，我岂不能取五日粮耶？』取五日粮已。时，众生竞积余粮故，是时粳米便生糠糩，收已不生，有枯秆现。

At that time, the sentient beings gathered in one place, lamenting and weeping, beating their chests and saying, 'Alas, what is this?' They lamented and blamed themselves, saying, 'We were originally all born through transformation, with thought as our food, our bodies self-illuminating, with divine feet flying through the air, peacefully and freely. Later, the earth essence first appeared, with color and taste complete. At that time, we ate this earth essence and lived for a long time. Those who ate more had coarser complexions, while those who ate less still had radiant complexions. At that time, the sentient beings had thoughts of each other, giving rise to a mind of pride, saying, "My complexion is superior, yours is not as good." Because of the pride of contention over complexion, the earth essence disappeared. Another earth skin appeared, with color, aroma, and flavor complete. We then again ate it together and lived for a long time. Those who ate more had coarser complexions, while those who ate less still had radiant complexions. At that time, the sentient beings had thoughts of each other, giving rise to a mind of pride, saying, "My complexion is superior, yours is not as good." Because of the pride of contention over complexion, the earth skin disappeared. Another earth skin appeared, becoming coarser and thicker, with color, aroma, and flavor complete. We then again ate it together and lived for a long time. Those who ate more had coarser complexions, while those who ate less still had radiant complexions. At that time, the sentient beings had thoughts of each other, giving rise to a mind of pride, saying, "My complexion is superior, yours is not as good." Because of the pride of contention over complexion, the earth skin disappeared. Another naturally grown rice appeared, with color, aroma, and flavor complete. We then again ate it together, harvesting in the morning and ripening in the evening, harvesting in the evening and ripening in the morning. The harvest followed the harvest, without any carrying away. Because we competed to store it at that time, it then grew husks and chaff. After harvesting, it did not grow again, and there were withered stalks. We should now all together demarcate fields and houses, dividing the boundaries.

「尔时，众生集在一处，懊恼悲泣，拍胷而言：『咄此为哉！』自悼责言：『我等本皆化生，以念为食，身光自照，神足飞空，安乐无碍。其后地味始生，色味具足，时，我等食此地味，久住于世。其食多者颜色转麤，其食少者色犹光泽，于是众生心怀彼我，生憍慢心言：「我色胜，汝色不如。」诤色憍慢故，地味消灭。更生地皮，色香味具。我等时复共取食之，久住于世。其食多者色转麤悴，其食少者色犹光泽，于是众生心怀彼我，生憍慢心言：「我色胜，汝色不如。」诤色憍慢故，地皮消灭。更生地肤，转更麤厚，色香味具。我等时复共取食之，久住于世。其食多者色转麤悴，其食少者色犹光泽，于是众生心怀彼我，生憍慢心言：「我色胜，汝色不如。」诤色憍慢故，地肤灭。更生自然粳米，色香味具。我等时复共取食之，朝获暮熟，暮获朝熟，收以随生，无有载收。由我尔时竞共积聚故，便生糠糩，收已不生，现有根秆。我等今者宁可共封田宅，以分疅畔。』

At that time, they immediately divided the fields according to the boundaries, considering each other as different. Later, they secretly stored their own rice and stole the grain from others' fields. The other sentient beings saw this and said, 'What you are doing is wrong, what you are doing is wrong. How can you secretly store your own things and steal others' property?' They reprimanded, 'Do not do it again in the future.' When this did not stop, they still stole. The others again reprimanded, 'What you are doing is wrong, why do you not stop?' They then beat him with their hands and took him to the assembly, telling the people, 'This person secretly stores rice and steals grain from others' fields.' The thief again said, 'He beat me.' When the people heard this, they lamented and wept, beating their chests and saying, 'The world is turning evil, is this the birth of evil dharmas?' They then gave rise to the suffering of affliction and distress, which is the source of birth, old age, sickness, and death, falling into evil destinies. Because of the different boundaries of fields and houses, disputes arose, leading to enmity and no one able to resolve it. 'We should now establish a single impartial ruler who can well protect the people, rewarding the good and punishing the evil. We, the people, should each reduce and give to support him.'

「时，即共分田以异疅畔，计有彼我。其后遂自藏己米，盗他田谷。余众生见已，语言：『汝所为非，汝所为非。云何自藏己物，盗他财物？』即呵责言：『汝后勿复为盗。』如是不已，犹复为盗，余人复呵言：『汝所为非，何故不休？』即便以手杖打，将诣众中，告众人言：『此人自藏粳米，盗他田谷。』盗者复言：『彼人打我。』众人闻已，懊恼涕泣，拊胷而言：『世间转恶，乃是恶法生耶？』遂生忧结热恼苦报，此是生、老、病、死之原，坠堕恶趣。有田宅疅畔别异，故生诤讼，以致怨讐，无能决者。『我等今者宁可立一平等主，善护人民，赏善罚恶，我等众人各共减割以供给之。』

At that time, among the assembly, there was a person with a tall and handsome appearance, very majestic and virtuous. The people said to him, 'We now want to establish you as the ruler, to well protect the people, rewarding the good and punishing the evil. We should each reduce and give to support you.' When that person heard this, he immediately accepted the position as the ruler, rewarding those who deserved it and punishing those who deserved it. Thus, there was the name of the first democratic ruler. The first democratic ruler had a son named Precious. Precious had a son named Delicious. Delicious had a son named Silent Fasting. Silent Fasting had a son named Crown-Born. Crown-Born had a son named Good Conduct. Good Conduct had a son named House-Conduct. House-Conduct had a son named Wonderful Flavor. Wonderful Flavor had a son named Flavor Emperor. Flavor Emperor had a son named Water Immortal. Water Immortal had a son named Hundred Wisdoms. Hundred Wisdoms had a son named Desire. Desire had a son named Good Desire. Good Desire had a son named Cut Off Afflictions. Cut Off Afflictions had a son named Great Cut Off Afflictions. Great Cut Off Afflictions had a son named Treasure Store. Treasure Store had a son named Great Treasure Store. Great Treasure Store had a son named Good View. Good View had a son named Great Good View. Great Good View had a son named No Sorrow. No Sorrow had a son named Island. Island had a son named Plant Life. Plant Life had a son named Mountain Range. Mountain Range had a son named Divine Heaven. Divine Heaven had a son named Send Strength. Send Strength had a son named Solid Vehicle. Solid Vehicle had a son named Ten Vehicles. Ten Vehicles had a son named Hundred Vehicles. Hundred Vehicles had a son named Solid Bow. Solid Bow had a son named Hundred Bows. Hundred Bows had a son named Shepherd. Shepherd had a son named Good Thought.

「时，彼众中有一人形质长大，容貌端正，甚有威德，众人语言：『我等今欲立汝为主，善护人民，赏善罚恶，当共减割以相供给。』其人闻之，即受为主，应赏者赏，应罚者罚，于是始有民主之名。初民主有子，名曰珍宝。珍宝有子，名曰好味，好味有子，名曰静斋，静斋有子，名曰顶生，顶生有子，名曰善行，善行有子，名曰宅行，宅行有子，名曰妙味，妙味有子，名曰味帝，味帝有子，名曰水仙，水仙有子，名曰百智，百智有子，名曰嗜欲，嗜欲有子，名曰善欲，善欲有子，名曰断结，断结有子，名曰大断结，大断结有子，名曰宝藏，宝藏有子，名曰大宝藏，大宝藏有子，名曰善见，善见有子，名曰大善见，大善见有子，名曰无忧，无忧有子，名曰洲渚，洲渚有子，名曰殖生，殖生有子，名曰山岳，山岳有子，名曰神天，神天有子，名曰遣力，遣力有子，名曰牢车，牢车有子，名曰十车，十车有子，名曰百车，百车有子，名曰牢弓，牢弓有子，名曰百弓，百弓有子，名曰养牧，养牧有子，名曰善思。

From Good Thought onwards, there were ten clans of wheel-turning sage kings who succeeded each other without interruption. The first was called Gāndhāra, the second was called Tārāpā, the third was called Āyodhyā, the fourth was called Dānadhara, the fifth was called Gaṅga, the sixth was called Campa, the seventh was called Kurupā, the eighth was called Bāṇḍhu, the ninth was called Miśra, and the tenth was called Śroṇā. The king of Gāndhāra had five wheel-turning sage kings, the king of Tārāpā had five wheel-turning sage kings, the king of Āyodhyā had seven wheel-turning sage kings, the king of Dānadhara had seven wheel-turning sage kings, the king of Gaṅga had nine wheel-turning sage kings, the king of Campa had fourteen wheel-turning sage kings, the king of Kurupā had thirty-one wheel-turning sage kings, the king of Bāṇḍhu had thirty-two wheel-turning sage kings, the king of Miśra had eighty-four thousand wheel-turning sage kings, and the king of Śroṇā had one hundred and one wheel-turning sage kings. The last king was named Mahāsudarśana.

「从善思已来有十族，转轮圣王相续不绝。一名伽［少／兔］麤，二名多罗婆，三名阿叶摩，四名持施，五名伽楞伽，六名瞻婆，七名拘罗婆，八者般阇罗，九者弥私罗，十者声摩。伽［少／兔］麤王有五转轮圣王，多罗婆王有五转轮圣王，阿叶摩王有七转轮圣王，持施王有七转轮圣王，伽楞伽王有九转轮圣王，瞻婆王有十四转轮圣王，拘罗婆] cf.【丽】王有三十一转轮圣王，般阇罗王有三十二转轮圣王，弥私罗王有八万四千转轮圣王，声摩王有百一转轮圣王，最后有王，名大善生从。

The king Śroṇā had a son named Urubilvā, Urubilvā had a son named Kuru, Kuru had a son named Niṣadha, Niṣadha had a son named Siṃhahanu, Siṃhahanu had a son named Śuddhodana, Śuddhodana had a son named Bodhisattva, Bodhisattva had a son named Rāhula. Because of this past cause, there is the name of a kṣatriya.

「声摩王有子，名乌罗婆，乌罗婆有子，名渠罗婆，渠罗婆有子，名尼求罗，尼求罗有子，名师子颊，师子颊有子，名曰白净王，白净王有子，名菩萨，菩萨有子，名罗睺罗。由此本缘有刹利名。

At that time, a sentient being thought like this: 'All the family and possessions in the world are like thorns and boils. Now I should abandon them, enter the mountains to practice the path, and contemplate in a quiet place.' At that time, he immediately abandoned the thorns of the family, entered the mountains to a quiet place, contemplated under a tree, and went out of the mountains every day to beg for food in the village. When the villagers saw him, they respected and offered him, all praising him as good: 'This person is able to abandon family affairs, enter the mountains to seek the path, and leave unwholesome dharmas.' Because of this, he was called a brāhmaṇa. Among the brāhmaṇa assembly, those who were unable to practice meditation left the mountains and forests, wandered among humans, and said: 'I am unable to sit in meditation.' Because of this, they were called 'brāhmaṇas without meditation'. Passing through the lower villages, they practiced unwholesome dharmas and performed poisonous dharmas. Because of this, they gave rise to each other and were finally called 'poisonous'. Because of this cause and condition, there are brāhmaṇa lineages in the world.

「尔时，有一众生作是念言：『世间所有家属万物皆为刺棘痈疮，今宜舍离，入山行道，静处思惟。』时，即远离家刺，入山静处，树下思惟，日日出山，入村乞食。村人见已，加敬供养，众共称善：『此人乃能舍离家累，入山求道，以其能离恶不善法。』因是称曰为婆罗门。婆罗门众中有不能行禅者，便出山林，游于人间，自言：『我不能坐禅。』因是名曰无禅婆罗门，经过下村，为不善法，施行毒法，因是相生，遂便名毒。由此因缘，世间有婆罗门种。

Among those sentient beings, they practiced various occupations to support themselves. Because of this, there are householder lineages in the world.

「彼众生中习种种业以自营生，因是故世间有居士种。

Among those sentient beings, they practiced various skills to support themselves. Because of this, there are śūdra lineages in the world.

「彼众生中习诸技艺以自生活，因是世间有首陀罗种。

Before the Śākya lineage appeared in the world, there was the lineage of renunciants. Among the kṣatriya lineage, someone thought to themselves: 'The defilements of worldly love and affection are impure and not worth being attached to.' They then left home, shaved their hair and beard, donned the Dharma robes, and sought the path, saying: 'I am a renunciant! I am a renunciant!' Among the brahmin, householder, and śūdra lineages, someone also thought to themselves: 'The defilements of worldly love and affection are impure and not worth being attached to.' They then left home, shaved their hair and beard, donned the Dharma robes, and sought the path, saying: 'I am a renunciant! I am a renunciant!'

「世间先有此释种出已，然后有沙门种。刹利种中有人自思惟：『世间恩爱污秽不净，何足贪著也？』于是舍家，剃除须发，法服求道：『我是沙门！我是沙门！』婆罗门种、居士种、首陀罗种众中有人自思惟：『世间恩爱污秽不净，何足贪著？』于是舍家，剃除须发，法服求道：『我是沙门！我是沙门！』

If among the kṣatriya assembly, there are those who engage in unwholesome bodily, verbal, and mental actions, and after engaging in unwholesome actions, they perish and their lives end, they will experience suffering exclusively. Or among the brahmin, householder, and śūdra, there are those who engage in unwholesome bodily, verbal, and mental actions, and after engaging in unwholesome actions, they perish and their lives end, they will experience suffering exclusively. If among the kṣatriya lineage, there are those who engage in wholesome bodily, verbal, and mental actions, and after engaging in wholesome actions, they perish and their lives end, they will experience happiness exclusively. Or among the brahmin, householder, and śūdra, there are those who engage in wholesome bodily, verbal, and mental actions, and after engaging in wholesome actions, they perish and their lives end, they will experience happiness exclusively. If among the kṣatriya lineage, there are those who engage in two kinds of bodily actions, two kinds of verbal actions, and two kinds of mental actions, and after engaging in those two kinds of bodily, verbal, and mental actions, they perish and their lives end, they will experience both suffering and happiness. Or among the brahmin, householder, and śūdra, there are those who engage in two kinds of bodily actions, two kinds of verbal actions, and two kinds of mental actions, and after engaging in those two kinds of bodily, verbal, and mental actions, they perish and their lives end, they will experience both suffering and happiness.

「若刹利众中，有身行不善、口行不善、意行不善，行不善已，身坏命终，一向受苦。或婆罗门、居士、首陀罗，身行不善、口行不善、意行不善，彼行不善已，身坏命终，一向受苦。刹利种身行善、口行善、意念善，身坏命终，一向受乐。婆罗门、居士、首陀罗，身行善、口行善、意等念善，身坏命终，一向受乐。刹利种身中有二种行，口、意有二种行，彼身、意行二种已，身坏命终，受苦乐报。婆罗门、居士、首陀罗，身二种行，口、意二种行，彼身、意行二种行已，身坏命终，受苦乐报。

Among the kṣatriya assembly, there are those who shave their hair and beard, don the three Dharma robes, leave home to seek the path, cultivate the seven factors of awakening, and with firm faith leave home to practice the path, cultivate the unsurpassed pure practice, and in this very life realize for themselves: 'My birth is ended, the holy life has been established, what was to be done has been done, there is no more of this state.' Among the brahmin, householder, and śūdra, there are those who shave their hair and beard, don the three Dharma robes, leave home to seek the path, cultivate the seven factors of awakening, and with firm faith leave home to practice the path, cultivate the unsurpassed pure practice, and in this very life realize: 'My birth is ended, the holy life has been established, there is no more of this state.' Among these four kinds, the one who attains clear knowledge and realization, and becomes an arhat, is the foremost and best. At that time, Brahma spoke this verse:

「刹利众中剃除须发，服三法衣，出家求道，彼修七觉意，彼以信坚固出家为道，修无上梵行，于现法中自身作证：我生死已尽，梵行已立，所作已办，更不受后有。婆罗门、居士、首陀罗剃除须发，服三法衣，出家求道，彼修七觉意，彼以信坚固出家为道，修无上梵行，于现法中作证：我生死已尽，梵行已立，更不受后有。此四种中，出明行成，得阿罗汉为最第一。是时，梵天说是偈言：

The kṣatriya birth is the best, able to gather all kinds of families. The one who attains
clear knowledge and realization, and becomes an arhat, is the foremost and best among gods and humans.

「『刹利生为最，　　能集诸种姓，明行成具足，　　天人中为最。』」

The Buddha told the monks, "Brahma's recitation of this verse is well-spoken, not ill-spoken, well-received, not ill-received, and is approved by me. Why is that? I, the Tathāgata, Arhat, Perfectly Enlightened One, also recite this verse:

佛告诸比丘：「彼梵天说此偈为善说，非不善说，善受，非不善受，我所印可。所以者何？我今如来、至真、等正觉亦说此偈：

The kṣatriya birth is the best, able to gather all kinds of families. The one who attains
clear knowledge and realization, and becomes an arhat, is the foremost and best among gods and humans.

「『刹利生为最，　　能集诸种姓，明行成具足，　　天人中为最。』」

At that time, the bhikṣus, having heard the Buddha's teaching, joyfully received and practiced it.

尔时，诸比丘闻佛所说，欢喜奉行。

The long Āgama is complete. I take refuge in the Omniscient One. May all beings be at peace and ease. May sentient beings abide in the unconditioned. I too am included in this.

长阿含具足，归命一切智，一切众安乐，众生处无为，我亦在其例。

Translated from Chinese using Gemma-2-Mitra (Buddhist-NLP).

This is the classical Chinese root text of Dīrghāgama, a parallel to the Pali sutta(s) listed above. Source: CBETA (Taishō edition).
